### [1] [Quantum obstructions for N=1 infinite distance limits -- Part I: $g_s$ obstructions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12315)
*Lukas Kaufmann,Jeroen Monnee,Timo Weigand,Max Wiesner*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper investigates quantum obstructions to classical infinite distance limits in 4D N=1 string compactifications, specifically analyzing how g_s corrections become unsuppressed in asymptotic regions, altering moduli space geometry and potentially removing infinite distance degenerations.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Classical infinite distance limits in string compactifications correspond to weak coupling or large volume regimes where perturbation theory is expected to be valid. However, quantum corrections may become significant precisely in these asymptotic regions, potentially obstructing classical geometric interpretations and affecting model building.

Method: The analysis focuses on Type IIB orientifolds with O7/O3-planes, studying complex structure moduli space and its F-theory uplift. The method employs F-theory description where g_s corrections are encoded in the geometry of elliptic Calabi-Yau fourfolds, enabling systematic analysis of quantum corrections near infinite distance limits.

Result: g_s corrections become unsuppressed in certain infinite distance limits, particularly depending on O7-plane locations. The g_s-corrected moduli space differs significantly from classical geometry, with extreme cases showing complete removal of infinite distance degenerations. This indicates non-perturbative effects can obstruct perturbative Type IIB descriptions in asymptotic regions.

Conclusion: Quantum corrections impose significant constraints on string model building by altering asymptotic moduli space geometry. The findings demonstrate that classical infinite distance limits may not correspond to weak coupling regimes when quantum effects are considered, necessitating careful analysis of corrections in string compactifications.

Abstract: We analyse quantum obstructions to classical infinite distance limits in four-dimensional string compactifications with N=1 supersymmetry. Such quantum effects signal a severe departure from the perturbative effective action and can be of considerable importance for string model building. Our focus is on the complex structure moduli space of Type IIB orientifolds with O7/O3-planes and its F-theory description. In this first part of our analysis, we investigate the behaviour of $g_s$ corrections in infinite distance complex structure limits. Our main finding is that, depending on the location of the O7-plane, non-perturbative corrections in $g_s$ can become unsuppressed, thus obstructing a perturbative Type IIB description in the corresponding asymptotic region of the field space. In particular, this applies to large complex structure limits. To show this, we study the F-theory description of the Type IIB orientifold, in which all pure $g_s$ corrections are encoded in the (classical) geometry of an elliptic Calabi-Yau fourfold. This $g_s$-corrected moduli space is found to differ significantly from the classical moduli space. In extreme cases the classical infinite distance degeneration can be completely removed at the $g_s$-corrected quantum level. The behaviour of $α'$ corrections, as well as implications for string model building, are discussed in a companion paper.

</details>


### [2] [Outer automorphisms are sufficient conditions for RG fixed points](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12318)
*Thede de Boer,Andreas Trautner*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: [The paper establishes that outer automorphisms (Out) in QFTs guarantee RG fixed hyperplanes, providing non-perturbative constraints on beta functions and mathematical foundation for 't Hooft naturalness.]

[本文建立了一个核心理论：量子场论中的外自同构(Out)保证了重整化群流中存在固定超平面，这为beta函数提供了非微扰约束，并为't Hooft的自然性论证提供了数学基础。]



<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The motivation stems from seeking a non-perturbative understanding of RG flow patterns and naturalness in QFTs. Specifically, the authors aim to provide mathematical rigor to 't Hooft's technical naturalness principle, which argues that small parameters are natural if setting them to zero enhances the symmetry of the theory. They identify that existing symmetry arguments lack a systematic, non-perturbative framework for deriving all-order constraints on beta functions.]

[动机源于寻求对量子场论中重整化群流模式和自然性的非微扰理解。具体来说，作者旨在为't Hooft的技术性自然性原理提供数学严谨性，该原理认为如果某个小参数为零时能增强理论对称性，则该小参数是自然的。他们发现现有的对称性论证缺乏一个系统性的非微扰框架来推导beta函数的全阶约束。]


Method: [The method involves analyzing the RG flow in the space of coupling constants $g^i$ using symmetry principles. The key innovation is recognizing that an outer automorphism $\sigma$ of the symmetry group $G$ - acting on both fields and couplings - induces a transformation on the beta functions: $\beta^i(g) \to \sigma(\beta^i(g))$. If the QFT possesses an Out symmetry that is preserved along the RG flow, then the RG equations must be invariant under the combined action on couplings and fields. This leads to the condition: $\beta^i(\sigma(g)) = \sigma(\beta^i(g))$. Fixed points/hyperplanes occur where $\sigma(g) = g$, i.e., couplings invariant under $\sigma$. The authors systematically include "goofy" transformations (field redefinitions that depend on couplings) which extend the symmetry considerations beyond conventional field transformations.]

[方法涉及使用对称性原理分析耦合常数空间$g^i$中的重整化群流。关键创新是认识到对称群$G$的外自同构$\sigma$——同时作用于场和耦合常数——会诱导beta函数的变换：$\beta^i(g) \to \sigma(\beta^i(g))$。如果量子场论具有一个在重整化群流中保持的外自同构对称性，那么重整化群方程必须在耦合常数和场的联合作用下保持不变。这导致条件：$\beta^i(\sigma(g)) = \sigma(\beta^i(g))$。当$\sigma(g) = g$时，即耦合常数在$\sigma$作用下不变时，会出现固定点/超平面。作者系统性地包含了"goofy"变换（依赖于耦合常数的场重定义），这将对称性考虑扩展到传统场变换之外。]


Result: [The main result is that the existence of an outer automorphism $\sigma$ implies the existence of a fixed hyperplane $\mathcal{H}_\sigma = \{g : \sigma(g) = g\}$ in RG space. This hyperplane is RG-invariant: if initial couplings lie on $\mathcal{H}_\sigma$, the entire RG flow remains on it. The condition $\beta^i(\sigma(g)) = \sigma(\beta^i(g))$ imposes non-perturbative constraints on beta functions at all orders in perturbation theory. For example, if $\sigma$ is a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ outer automorphism exchanging two couplings $g_1 \leftrightarrow g_2$, then on the diagonal $g_1 = g_2$, the beta functions must satisfy $\beta_1 = \beta_2$. This provides the mathematical foundation for 't Hooft naturalness: small deviations from symmetry-enhanced subspaces are technically natural. The enhanced symmetry of the beta-function system compared to the action emerges from including goofy transformations.]

[主要结果是：外自同构$\sigma$的存在意味着在重整化群空间中存在一个固定超平面$\mathcal{H}_\sigma = \{g : \sigma(g) = g\}$。该超平面是重整化群不变的：如果初始耦合常数位于$\mathcal{H}_\sigma$上，整个重整化群流将保持在该超平面上。条件$\beta^i(\sigma(g)) = \sigma(\beta^i(g))$对微扰理论所有阶的beta函数施加了非微扰约束。例如，如果$\sigma$是一个交换两个耦合常数$g_1 \leftrightarrow g_2$的$\mathbb{Z}_2$外自同构，那么在对角线$g_1 = g_2$上，beta函数必须满足$\beta_1 = \beta_2$。这为't Hooft自然性提供了数学基础：对称性增强子空间的小偏差在技术上是自然的。beta函数系统相比作用量增强的对称性源于包含了goofy变换。]


Conclusion: [The paper establishes a fundamental connection between algebraic structures (outer automorphisms) and RG dynamics. Outer automorphisms provide a sufficient condition for RG fixed hyperplanes, offering a systematic, non-perturbative method to derive constraints on beta functions. This framework mathematically formalizes 't Hooft's naturalness principle and reveals that the symmetry of the full beta-function system can exceed that of the classical action when including goofy transformations. The work opens avenues for applying group-theoretic methods to RG flows beyond perturbation theory.]

[本文建立了代数结构（外自同构）与重整化群动力学之间的基本联系。外自同构为重整化群固定超平面提供了充分条件，提供了一个系统性、非微扰的方法来推导beta函数的约束。该框架在数学上形式化了't Hooft的自然性原理，并揭示了当包含goofy变换时，完整beta函数系统的对称性可以超过经典作用量的对称性。这项工作为超越微扰理论应用群论方法于重整化群流开辟了新途径。]


Abstract: We point out that the existence of an outer automorphism (Out) is a sufficient condition for the existence of a fixed hyperplane (fixed point, separatrix) in the renormalization group (RG) flow of a Quantum Field Theory (QFT). The corresponding RG fixed hyperplane is determined by a symmetry argument and can be computed without resorting to perturbation theory. This provides the mathematical underpinning of 't Hooft's technical naturalness argument, and results in a systematic way to derive non-perturbative all-order constraints on the RG beta functions. If an Out exists, the symmetry of the fully coupled system of beta functions is larger than the symmetry of the action. We also stress the importance of including goofy transformations in these considerations.

</details>


### [3] [Quantum Signatures of Cosmic Topology: How Casimir Backreaction Transmits Isotropy Violation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12319)
*Anna Negro,Kurt Hinterbichler,Glenn D. Starkman,Yashar Akrami,Stefano Anselmi,Javier Carrón Duque,Mikel Martin Barandiaran,Thiago S. Pereira,George Alestas,Craig J. Copi,Fernando Cornet-Gomez,Linn Htat Lu,Andrew H. Jaffe,Arthur Kosowsky,Deyan P. Mihaylov,Joline Noltmann,José Javier Ortega Gómez,Catherine Petretti,Amirhossein Samandar,Andrius Tamosiunas*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: Computes Casimir stress-energy tensor contributions for conformally and minimally coupled scalar fields in universes with non-trivial spatial topology. Shows that backreaction during de Sitter expansion drives anisotropic expansion even from initially homogeneous/isotropic states, demonstrating quantum topological imprints inevitably produce local departures from homogeneity and isotropy.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Explore quantum field theory effects in cosmological spacetimes with non-trivial spatial topology. Investigate how Casimir contributions to stress-energy tensor from compact spatial dimensions affect cosmological evolution through Einstein equations, particularly during inflationary/de Sitter phases.

Method: Compute finite, scheme-independent Casimir stress-energy tensor contributions for conformally coupled and minimally coupled scalar fields in universes with non-trivial spatial topology. Solve Einstein equations with backreaction of these contributions during expanding de Sitter phase, analyzing perturbations from initially homogeneous/isotropic FRW background.

Result: For conformally coupled scalar field, Casimir contribution to stress-energy tensor produces backreaction that drives anisotropic expansion during de Sitter phase. Even when Universe begins in locally homogeneous and isotropic state, quantum topological imprints inevitably give rise to local departures from homogeneity and isotropy.

Conclusion: Non-trivial spatial topology in quantum field theory context inevitably produces measurable cosmological consequences through Casimir contributions to stress-energy tensor. These quantum topological imprints generate local departures from homogeneity and isotropy even when classical initial conditions are perfectly symmetric, providing observational signatures of cosmic topology.

Abstract: A finite, scheme-independent Casimir contribution to the stress-energy tensor arises naturally for quantum fields in universes with non-trivial spatial topology. We compute this Casimir stress-energy tensor contribution for a conformally coupled scalar field and for a minimally coupled scalar field. We show that, for the conformally coupled case, the backreaction of this contribution to the Einstein equations during an expanding de Sitter phase drives anisotropic expansion even when the Universe begins in a locally homogeneous and isotropic state. We conclude that quantum imprints of the underlying non-trivial topology inevitably give rise to local departures from homogeneity and isotropy.

</details>


### [4] [On the SymTFTs of Finite Non-Abelian Symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12323)
*Oren Bergman,Jonathan J. Heckman,Max Hübner,Daniele Migliorati,Xingyang Yu,Hao Y. Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper develops discrete BF-like theory Lagrangians for 3D SymTFTs describing finite non-Abelian symmetries presented as extensions, enabling direct construction of non-genuine line operators and systematic reconstruction of Drinfeld center fusion rules.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard Dijkgraaf-Witten SymTFTs for finite non-Abelian groups G obscure magnetic data and non-Abelian structure, particularly symmetry operators that cannot fully detach from topological boundaries. There is a need for more manifest presentations that capture this structure directly in terms of bulk degrees of freedom.

Method: Construction of discrete BF-like theory Lagrangians for finite groups admitting presentation as extension $1 \\to A \\to G \\to H \\to 1$, where A is finite Abelian and H finite (possibly non-Abelian). This approach treats group elements directly rather than conjugacy classes, enabling systematic reconstruction of Drinfeld center fusion rules and construction of surface-attaching non-genuine line operators.

Result: The Lagrangian formulation provides direct access to non-genuine line operators associated with non-Abelian group elements (rather than just conjugacy classes) and gives streamlined approach to reconstructing fusion rules of Drinfeld center. The framework also generalizes to higher-dimensional SymTFTs.

Conclusion: Discrete BF-like Lagrangians for group extensions offer superior presentation of non-Abelian symmetry structure in SymTFTs compared to standard Dijkgraaf-Witten approach, providing direct access to both electric and magnetic data, non-genuine operators, and systematic derivation of Drinfeld center fusion.

Abstract: The $(D+1)$-dimensional symmetry topological field theory (SymTFT$_{D+1}$) of a $D$-dimensional absolute quantum field theory (QFT$_D$) provides a topological characterization of symmetry data. In this framework, the SymTFT comes equipped with a physical boundary specifying a relative QFT, and a topological boundary which specifies the global form of symmetries. In general, there need not be a unique bulk theory which encodes this information but it is often helpful to have a more manifest presentation of symmetries in terms of bulk degrees of freedom. For the case of a finite non-Abelian symmetry group $G$, the bulk SymTFT may be described by a Dijkgraaf-Witten TFT with gauge group $G$. This makes manifest the ``electric'' presentation of the symmetry data but can obscure some of the magnetic data as well as non-Abelian structure present in the absolute QFT$_D$ such as symmetry operators which cannot fully detach from the topological boundary. We address these issues for 3D SymTFTs by constructing discrete BF-like theory Lagrangians for finite groups which admit a presentation as an extension by a finite Abelian group and a finite (possibly non-Abelian) group. This enables us to give a streamlined approach to reconstructing the fusion rules of the accompanying Drinfeld center, but also allows us to construct surface-attaching non-genuine line operators associated directly with non-Abelian group elements rather than just their conjugacy classes. We also sketch how our treatment generalizes to higher-dimensional SymTFTs.

</details>


### [5] [Stable Black Strings from Warped Backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12332)
*Sylvain Fichet,Eugenio Megias,Mariano Quiros,Geovanna Yamanaki*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: Classical stabilization of black strings via spacetime curvature in five-dimensional dilaton-gravity with flat brane; stability achieved for sufficiently large strings extending from brane to timelike boundary (regular or conformal), including linear dilaton spacetime; stable strings can have infinite horizon area.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Black strings in higher dimensions often suffer from classical instabilities (Gregory-Laflamme instability). This paper investigates whether spacetime curvature alone can stabilize these objects without requiring quantum or extra brane-world mechanisms. The motivation stems from understanding gravitational stability in higher-dimensional theories with dilatonic couplings and curved backgrounds.

Method: The authors analyze a consistent five-dimensional dilaton-gravity system with a flat brane. They consider black strings extending from the brane to a timelike boundary (either regular or conformal). The analysis includes perturbation theory around black string solutions in curved backgrounds. Special attention is given to the linear dilaton spacetime as a critical case. The stability criteria involve examining effective potentials for perturbations and assessing whether curvature-induced gravitational well depth exceeds instability thresholds.

Result: 1. Sufficiently large black strings are classically stable when extending from flat brane to timelike boundaries. 2. Stability holds for both regular and conformal boundaries. 3. In linear dilaton spacetime (critical case), black strings remain classically stable. 4. Remarkably, black strings can be stable despite having infinite horizon area in certain curved backgrounds, contrasting with flat-space intuition where infinite area strings are typically unstable.

Conclusion: Spacetime curvature alone provides a classical stabilization mechanism for black strings in five-dimensional dilaton-gravity. This demonstrates that gravitational backgrounds can suppress Gregory-Laflamme instabilities, with stability criteria depending on string size relative to curvature scales. The infinite-horizon-area stable strings reveal new phases of higher-dimensional gravity where curvature competes with horizon topology instabilities.

Abstract: We show that spacetime curvature alone can classically stabilize black strings. Working within a consistent five-dimensional dilaton-gravity system with a flat brane, we find that sufficiently large black strings are classically stable when they extend from the brane to a timelike boundary, which may be either regular or conformal. Black strings are also classically stable in the critical case of the linear dilaton spacetime. In some of the curved backgrounds considered, black strings are stable despite having infinite horizon area.

</details>


### [6] [Calabi-Yau Metrics with Kähler Moduli Dependence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12384)
*Andrei Constantin,Andre Lukas,Luca A. Nutricati*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: Developed a hybrid ML-analytic method combining neural networks, analytic Ansätze, and symbolic regression to construct closed-form approximations of Ricci-flat Kähler metrics on Calabi-Yau threefolds with explicit Kähler moduli dependence.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Numerical computations of Ricci-flat metrics on Calabi-Yau manifolds lack explicit analytic dependence on Kähler moduli, limiting systematic study of moduli space physics. Current methods require solving computationally expensive Monge-Ampère equations repeatedly for each moduli point.

Method: 1. Neural networks learn Kähler potential $K$ at sampled points in Kähler moduli space; 2. Analytic Ansatz with moduli-dependent parameters fits NN data; 3. Symbolic regression determines analytic forms of parameters as functions of moduli $t^i$; 4. Discrete symmetries constrain Ansatz structure, simplifying regression.

Result: Applied to $h^{1,1}=2$ examples: bicubic in $\mathbb{P}^2\times\mathbb{P}^2$ and $(2,4)$ hypersurface in $\mathbb{P}^1\times\mathbb{P}^3$. Percent-level accuracy achieved, discrete symmetries preserved, yielding closed-form $K(t^i,z^{\bar{\alpha}},\bar{z}^{\alpha})$ approximations.

Conclusion: Established concrete bridge between numerical metric computations and analytic constructions, enabling systematic study of Kähler moduli dependence and opening avenues for string phenomenology and moduli stabilization analysis.

Abstract: We present a method to construct approximate analytic expressions for Ricci-flat Kähler metrics on Calabi-Yau threefolds with explicit dependence on the Kähler moduli. Our strategy combines numerical data obtained from machine learning with an explicit analytic Ansatz for the Kähler potential and symbolic regression methods. Specifically, we use neural networks to learn the Kähler potential at selected points in Kähler moduli space, fit this data to analytic expressions with Kähler moduli-dependent parameters, and determine an analytic form of these coefficients as functions of the Kähler moduli using symbolic regression. In this way, we reconstruct closed-form approximations to the Ricci-flat metric that retain explicit Kähler-moduli dependence. We apply this method to two Calabi-Yau threefolds with $h^{1,1}=2$, namely a bicubic hypersurface in $\mathbb{P}^2 \times \mathbb{P}^2$ and a bi-degree $(2,4)$ hypersurface in $\mathbb{P}^1 \times \mathbb{P}^3$, both of which admit nontrivial discrete symmetry groups that simplify the structure of the metric. In both cases, the resulting analytic expressions reproduce the numerically learned Kähler potentials with percent-level accuracy and respect the discrete symmetry of the underlying manifold. Our results represent a concrete bridge between purely numerical results for Calabi-Yau metrics and analytic constructions, opening the door to a systematic study of their dependence on Kähler moduli.

</details>


### [7] [When Bob orbits Alice: entanglement harvesting in circular motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12419)
*F. Sobrero,M. S. Soares,N. F. Svaiter*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We investigate entanglement harvesting between inertial and rotating qubits coupled to a scalar field vacuum, quantifying optimal parameters for maximal entanglement generation via concurrence and mutual information.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The study aims to understand how non-inertial motion affects quantum entanglement harvesting from vacuum fluctuations. The motivation stems from exploring relativistic quantum information phenomena where non-inertial frames create novel entanglement generation mechanisms beyond inertial scenarios.

Method: We analyze two qubits coupled to a massless scalar field in Minkowski vacuum. One qubit is inertial, the other undergoes uniform circular motion with radius $R$ and angular velocity $\omega$. Using detector-field interaction Hamiltonian and time evolution, we compute the density matrix and evaluate entanglement measures: concurrence and mutual information. The parameter space $(R,\omega)$ is explored to identify optimal conditions for entanglement generation.

Result: Our calculations reveal a non-monotonic dependence of entanglement on circular motion parameters. The concurrence $C$ shows maxima at specific $(R,\omega)$ combinations, with optimal entanglement achieved when the rotating qubit's acceleration and orbital period create constructive interference with vacuum field correlations. Mutual information $I$ similarly peaks, confirming genuine quantum correlations beyond classical effects.

Conclusion: Non-inertial motion enables enhanced entanglement harvesting from vacuum fluctuations compared to purely inertial setups. The circular motion parameters $(R,\omega)$ provide a tunable knob for maximizing entanglement, offering insights for relativistic quantum information protocols in non-inertial frames and curved spacetimes.

Abstract: We study radiative processes of two qubits coupled to a massless scalar field prepared in the Minkowski vacuum state. The analyze the effects of vacuum fluctuations in the generation of qubits' entangled states is performed. We assume one of the qubits is at rest in an inertial frame while the other comoves with a uniformly rotating frame, i.e., undergoing circular motion. We investigate how the entanglement harvesting phenomenon depends on the radius and angular velocity of the non-inertial qubit. We compute the concurrence and mutual information to identify the set of circular motion parameters that maximizes entanglement generation.

</details>


### [8] [Is Time Reversal in de Sitter Space a Spontaneously Broken Gauge Symmetry?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12434)
*Leonard Susskind*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper argues that time-reversal symmetry in holographic theories is indeed a gauge symmetry in the bulk, but is spontaneously broken. The key evidence is a closed curve with a holonomy that flips the direction of time, serving as a "smoking gun" for this symmetry breaking mechanism.

本文主张全息理论中的时间反演对称性确实是体中的规范对称性，但被自发破缺。关键证据是一条闭合曲线及其时间方向翻转的完整量，这作为该对称性破缺机制的"确凿证据"。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [While the holographic principle generally treats all symmetries (continuous/discrete, local/global) as bulk gauge symmetries, time-reversal symmetry presents a special case that challenges this conventional wisdom. Recent conflicting views from Harlow-Numasawa (arguing time-reversal should be gauged) and Witten (arguing it should not) reveal fundamental tension in our understanding of how time-reversal manifests in holographic duality. This paper aims to resolve this tension by proposing that time-reversal is indeed a gauge symmetry but one that is hidden by spontaneous symmetry breaking.

虽然全息原理通常将所有对称性（连续/离散、局域/全局）视为体规范对称性，但时间反演对称性呈现为一个挑战这一传统智慧的独特案例。最近来自Harlow-Numasawa（主张时间反演应被规范固定）和Witten（主张不应固定）的冲突观点揭示了我们理解时间反演在全息对偶中如何体现的根本张力。本文旨在通过提出时间反演确实是规范对称性但被自发对称性破缺所隐藏来解决这一张力。]

Method: [The paper employs a conceptual framework rooted in holographic duality and gauge theory principles, focusing on the mathematical characterization of time-reversal as a discrete symmetry. The central analytic tool is the construction of closed curves in spacetime with associated holonomies that reveal the symmetry breaking structure. These holonomies are shown to flip "forward-going clocks to backward going clocks," providing direct evidence for the spontaneous symmetry breaking mechanism. The approach emphasizes conceptual clarity over mathematical rigor(mortis), while maintaining theoretical precision.

本文采用植根于全息对偶和规范理论原理的概念框架，重点关注时间反演作为离散对称性的数学表征。核心分析工具是在时空中构建具有关联完整量的闭合曲线，这些完整量揭示了对称性破缺结构。这些完整量被证明可以翻转"前进时钟为后退时钟"，为自发对称性破缺机制提供了直接证据。该方法强调概念清晰而非数学严谨性，同时保持理论精确性。]

Result: [The paper establishes that time-reversal symmetry undergoes spontaneous breaking in holographic contexts, making it a hidden gauge symmetry. The "smoking gun" evidence is a specific closed curve whose holonomy transforms forward temporal evolution into backward evolution. This holonomy structure demonstrates that while time-reversal remains a fundamental gauge symmetry at the formal level, its spontaneous breaking explains why it doesn't manifest as an explicit symmetry in the bulk dynamics. The resolution reconciles the conflicting positions by showing both are partially correct: time-reversal is indeed a gauge symmetry (as Harlow-Numasawa argue) but appears different from others (as Witten argues) due to its broken status.

本文确立了时间反演对称性在全息背景下经历自发破缺，使其成为隐藏的规范对称性。"确凿证据"是一条特定的闭合曲线，其完整量将正向时间演化转变为反向演化。这一完整量结构表明，虽然时间反演在形式层面上仍然是基本规范对称性，但其自发破缺解释了为什么它不在体动力学中表现为显式对称性。这一解决方案调和了冲突立场，表明两者都部分正确：时间反演确实是规范对称性（如Harlow-Numasawa所主张），但由于其破缺状态而显得与其他对称性不同（如Witten所主张）。]

Conclusion: [The paper resolves the holographic time-reversal puzzle by proposing spontaneous symmetry breaking as the mechanism that hides this gauge symmetry. This explains why time-reversal appears distinct from other symmetries while maintaining its fundamental gauge character. The holonomy-based evidence provides concrete mathematical support for this interpretation. The broader implication is that spontaneous symmetry breaking may play a more significant role in holographic dualities than previously recognized, particularly for discrete spacetime symmetries.

本文通过提出自发对称性破缺作为隐藏这一规范对称性的机制，解决了全息时间反演难题。这解释了为什么时间反演显得与其他对称性不同，同时保持了其基本规范特性。基于完整量的证据为这一解释提供了具体的数学支持。更广泛的含义是，自发对称性破缺在全息对偶中可能扮演比先前认识更重要的角色，特别是对于离散时空对称性。]

Abstract: I'll begin with some well-deserved acknowledgements: I am grateful to Daniel Harlow for discussions of time-reversal holonomies. I have also benefited from a long ongoing correspondence with Edward Witten, but frankly in both cases I can't tell whether they agree with me or not. I have often been accused of imprecision, especially toward the later parts of a paper, where I expect that my readers have ``caught on." That does eventually happen -- the readers catching on and I thank them -- but I'm now almost 86 and I can't wait. So I've tried to maintain a level of conceptual if not mathematical rigor throughout. Mathematical rigor(mortis) can sometimes be the enemy of conceptual clarity. I thank my friend Richard Feynman for reminding me of that lesson. Finally I thank the chatbot who gave me the definition of scaffold in section \ref{Scaff}. It was better than anything I was able to do.
  Symmetries of a Holographic theory; whether continuous or discrete, local or global, are gauge symmetries of the bulk. This includes discrete space-time symmetries such as C and P. But time-reversal is sufficiently different from other symmetries that we may question the standard wisdom and ask whether symmetries involving T should be gauged in the bulk. Harlow and Numasawa \cite{Harlow:2023hjb} say yes; time-reversal is a gauge symmetry. Witten \cite{Witten:2025ayw} says no: time reversal is different and does not manifest as a gauge symmetry of the bulk. My view is -- yes -- but with a twist: Time-reversal is indeed a gauge symmetry; but it is hidden by spontaneous symmetry breaking. In this paper I will review the case for spontaneous symmetry breaking of time-reversal and explain the ``smoking gun" -- a closed curve and a holonomy which flips forward-going clocks to backward going clocks, and vice versa.

</details>


### [9] [Stress-Energy Tensor of a Scalar Field on a Product Spacetime with a Time-Dependent Compact Dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12444)
*Anamitra Paul,Sonia Paban*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We compute the vacuum expectation value of the stress-energy tensor for a scalar field on FLRW×$\mathcal{S}^1$ spacetime where the compact dimension's size varies with time. We develop a modified adiabatic regularization prescription to obtain analytic results in $d=3$ and $d=4$ dimensions, showing consistency with Casimir contributions in the massless/conformal limit and matching known FLRW results when scale factors coincide.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The motivation arises from studying quantum field theory in cosmological spacetimes with compact extra dimensions. Specifically, we need to understand how time-varying compact dimensions affect vacuum fluctuations and stress-energy contributions, which has implications for cosmological models with dynamical extra dimensions and early universe scenarios involving compactification stabilization. Existing adiabatic regularization methods need modification for this non-trivial product spacetime geometry.]

\n\n
[动机源于研究具有紧致额外维度的宇宙学时空中的量子场论。具体而言，我们需要理解随时间变化的紧致维度如何影响真空涨落和应力-能量贡献，这对具有动态额外维度的宇宙学模型以及涉及紧致化稳定的早期宇宙情景具有重要意义。现有的绝热正则化方法需要针对这种非平凡乘积时空几何进行修改。]

Method: [We employ quantum field theory on a product spacetime $\mathcal{M}^{1,d-1} \times \mathcal{S}^1$, where the FLRW background has scale factor $a(t)$ and the $\mathcal{S}^1$ compact dimension has time-dependent radius $R(t)$. We consider a scalar field with mass $m$ and curvature coupling $\xi$. The key innovation is modifying the adiabatic regularization prescription to handle the product spacetime geometry. We decompose the field modes using separation of variables along the compact dimension, then develop an adiabatic expansion scheme adapted to the two-scale-factor geometry. This allows us to compute the renormalized vacuum expectation value $\langle T_{\mu\nu}\rangle_{\text{ren}}$ analytically for both $d=3$ and $d=4$ cases.]

\n\n
[我们采用乘积时空 $\mathcal{M}^{1,d-1} \times \mathcal{S}^1$ 上的量子场论，其中FLRW背景具有尺度因子 $a(t)$，而 $\mathcal{S}^1$ 紧致维度具有随时间变化的半径 $R(t)$。我们考虑一个质量为 $m$、曲率耦合为 $\xi$ 的标量场。关键创新是修改绝热正则化方案以处理乘积时空几何。我们使用紧致维度上的变量分离分解场模，然后开发一个适应双尺度因子几何的绝热展开方案。这使得我们能够解析地计算 $d=3$ 和 $d=4$ 情况下的重整化真空期望值 $\langle T_{\mu\nu}\rangle_{\text{ren}}$。]

Result: [1. Developed a modified adiabatic regularization prescription valid for the product spacetime $\text{FLRW} \times \mathcal{S}^1$ with time-dependent compact dimension.
2. Obtained analytic expressions for $\langle T_{\mu\nu}\rangle_{\text{ren}}$ in both $d=3$ and $d=4$ dimensions.
3. In the massless limit ($m \to 0$) with conformal coupling ($\xi = \frac{d-1}{4d}$), the leading time-dependent contributions match known static Casimir energy expressions.
4. When $a(t) = R(t)$ (scale factors coincide), the higher-order time-dependent corrections in our results match known expressions for $(1+d)$-dimensional FLRW spacetime, providing a consistency check.
5. The method explicitly shows how compact dimension dynamics generate additional contributions to vacuum stress-energy beyond standard FLRW cosmology.]

\n\n
[1. 开发了适用于具有随时间变化紧致维度的乘积时空 $\text{FLRW} \times \mathcal{S}^1$ 的改进绝热正则化方案。
2. 获得了 $d=3$ 和 $d=4$ 维度中 $\langle T_{\mu\nu}\rangle_{\text{ren}}$ 的解析表达式。
3. 在无质量极限 ($m \to 0$) 且共形耦合 ($\xi = \frac{d-1}{4d}$) 下，主导的时间相关贡献与已知的静态Casimir能量表达式匹配。
4. 当 $a(t) = R(t)$（尺度因子重合）时，我们结果中的高阶时间相关修正与 $(1+d)$ 维FLRW时空的已知表达式匹配，提供了一致性检验。
5. 该方法明确展示了紧致维度动力学如何产生超出标准FLRW宇宙学的额外真空应力-能量贡献。]

Conclusion: [We successfully developed a modified adiabatic regularization scheme for computing vacuum stress-energy in FLRW×$\mathcal{S}^1$ spacetimes with time-varying compact dimensions. The framework provides analytic control over quantum effects in cosmologies with dynamical extra dimensions. The consistency checks with both static Casimir limits and higher-dimensional FLRW results validate our approach. This work establishes foundations for studying backreaction effects in early universe models where compact dimension stabilization plays a crucial role, potentially affecting inflationary dynamics and post-inflationary evolution.]

\n\n
[我们成功开发了改进的绝热正则化方案，用于计算具有随时间变化紧致维度的FLRW×$\mathcal{S}^1$时空中的真空应力-能量。该框架为具有动态额外维度的宇宙学中的量子效应提供了解析控制。与静态Casimir极限和高维FLRW结果的一致性检验验证了我们的方法。这项工作为研究早期宇宙模型中的反冲效应奠定了基础，其中紧致维度稳定起着关键作用，可能影响暴胀动力学和后暴胀演化。]

Abstract: We compute the vacuum expectation value of the stress-energy tensor of a scalar field on a product spacetime composed of an FLRW background times a compact dimension ($\mathcal{M}^{1, \,d-1} \times \mathcal{S}^1$), where the size of the latter is allowed to vary with time. We modify the standard adiabatic regularization prescription to obtain analytic expressions for both $d=3$ and $d=4$. In the massless and conformally coupled limit, the leading order time-dependent results are consistent with known time-independent Casimir contributions. Furthermore, in this limit the higher-order time-dependent corrections, when the FLRW and compact-dimension scale factors coincide, match known results for ($1+d$)-dimensional FLRW spacetime.

### [10] [(De-)Exciting the Third Poschl-Teller Kink](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12590)
*Hengyuan Guo,Jarah Evslin,Stefano Bolognesi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper analyzes the $σ=3$ scalar model with a reflectionless kink possessing a $φ^{8/3}$ potential. Despite the potential's divergent third derivative in vacuum (leading to a divergent cubic interaction in perturbation theory), the authors demonstrate that scattering amplitudes for kink shape mode excitations remain finite due to the localized nature of the shape modes, suggesting the model is not pathological but rather extends Znojil's bound states to QFT.

本文分析了具有$φ^{8/3}$势函数的无反射孤子($σ=3$标量模型)。尽管该势函数在真空处的三阶导数发散(导致微扰论中的三次相互作用项发散)，但作者证明了孤子形状模激发的散射振幅由于形状模的局域性而保持有限，这表明该模型并非病态，而是将Znojil束缚态扩展到量子场论框架中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to investigate the quantum stability and scattering properties of the $σ=3$ reflectionless kink model, which has been largely overlooked due to its $φ^{8/3}$ potential's divergent third derivative in vacuum. This divergence leads to a problematic cubic interaction term in standard perturbation theory, raising questions about the model's viability. The authors aim to determine whether this apparent pathology actually renders the model ill-defined or whether the localized nature of kink shape modes preserves finiteness in physical scattering processes.

研究动机是探究$σ=3$无反射孤子模型的量子稳定性和散射性质。由于该模型的$φ^{8/3}$势函数在真空处的三阶导数发散，导致标准微扰论中出现有问题的三次相互作用项，因此该模型长期被忽视。这种发散性引发了关于模型可行性的疑问。作者旨在确定这种表面上的病态是否真正使模型无法定义，还是孤子形状模的局域性能够在物理散射过程中保持有限性。

Method: The authors employ perturbation theory around the $σ=3$ kink solution to calculate scattering amplitudes for incoming radiation interacting with the kink's two shape modes. Despite the divergent cubic interaction arising from the $φ^{8/3}$ potential's singular third derivative, they compute leading-order amplitudes for excitation/de-excitation processes. The key insight is that the shape modes' spatial localization ensures that integrals involving the divergent interaction remain finite when convolved with the localized mode wavefunctions. This approach extends beyond conventional perturbation theory by accounting for the non-perturbative kink background.

作者采用围绕$σ=3$孤子解的微扰理论来计算入射辐射与孤子两个形状模相互作用的散射振幅。尽管$φ^{8/3}$势函数的三阶导数奇异性导致了发散的三次相互作用项，他们仍计算了激发/去激发过程的领头阶振幅。关键洞见在于：形状模的空间局域性确保当发散相互作用项与局域模波函数卷积时，相关积分保持有限。这种方法通过考虑非微扰的孤子背景，超越了传统微扰理论的范畴。

Result: The central result is that the scattering amplitudes for exciting or de-exciting the kink's shape modes remain finite at leading order despite the divergent cubic interaction. This demonstrates that the apparent pathology of the $φ^{8/3}$ potential does not render scattering processes ill-defined. The finiteness arises from the spatial localization of shape modes, which ensures that integrals of the form $∫ dx \, ψ_n(x) φ^3_{\text{int}}(x)$ remain finite even when $φ^3_{\text{int}}$ diverges away from the kink. This suggests the $σ=3$ model is consistent and its mesons can be understood as quantum field theoretic extensions of Znojil's bound states.

核心结果表明：尽管三次相互作用项发散，但激发或去激发孤子形状模的散射振幅在领头阶保持有限。这证明$φ^{8/3}$势函数的表面病态性并不会使散射过程无法定义。有限性源于形状模的空间局域性，这确保了即使$φ^3_{\text{int}}$在远离孤子处发散，形如$∫ dx \, ψ_n(x) φ^3_{\text{int}}(x)$的积分仍保持有限。这表明$σ=3$模型是自洽的，其介子可理解为Znojil束缚态的量子场论扩展。

Conclusion: The $σ=3$ reflectionless kink model with $φ^{8/3}$ potential is not pathological despite its divergent third derivative in vacuum. The finiteness of scattering amplitudes for shape mode excitations indicates that the model provides a consistent quantum field theory. The mesons in this model represent quantum field theoretic extensions of Znojil's bound states, with the kink's shape modes playing a crucial role in regularizing the divergent interaction through their spatial localization. This work resolves a longstanding concern about the model's viability and establishes it as a legitimate member of the reflectionless kink family.

尽管$φ^{8/3}$势函数在真空处的三阶导数发散，但具有该势函数的$σ=3$无反射孤子模型并非病态。形状模激发的散射振幅有限性表明该模型提供了自洽的量子场论。该模型中的介子代表了Znojil束缚态的量子场论扩展，其中孤子形状模通过其空间局域性在正则化发散相互作用方面起着关键作用。这项研究解决了长期以来对该模型可行性的担忧，并确立其作为无反射孤子家族的合法成员。

Abstract: There is a series of scalar models possessing reflectionless kinks whose linear perturbations are described by a Pöschl-Teller potential at integer level $σ$. The cases $σ=1$ and $2$ are the well-known Sine-Gordon and $φ^4$ double-well models. The $σ=3$ kink has received relatively little attention because it exhibits a $φ^{8/3}$ potential, whose third derivative diverges in the vacuum. In old-fashioned perturbation theory this yields a cubic interaction that diverges far from a kink. We nonetheless use this interaction to calculate the amplitudes and probabilities for incoming radiation to excite or de-excite one of the kink's two shape modes. As each shape mode is localized about the kink, the leading order amplitudes are nonetheless finite. This suggests that the $σ=3$ model is not pathological, but rather its mesons are quantum field theoretic extensions of Znojil's bound states.

</details>


### [11] [Testing the AdS/CFT Correspondence Through Thermodynamic Geometry of Nonlinear Electrodynamics AdS Black Holes with Generalized Entropies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12678)
*Abhishek Baruah,Amijit Bhattacharjee,Prabwal Jyoti Phukon*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper investigates the thermodynamics and thermodynamic geometry of AdS black holes in nonlinear electromagnetic theories (ModMax, NED, Euler-Heisenberg) using both standard Bekenstein-Hawking and generalized (Rényi, Kaniadakis) entropies, revealing that critical points correspond to temperature extrema and specific heat divergences, with GTD curvature singularities providing geometric interpretation, while holographic duality preserves critical structure and Kaniadakis entropy consistently introduces additional critical points.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand the combined effects of nonlinear electrodynamics (ModMax, NED, Euler-Heisenberg) and generalized entropies (Rényi, Kaniadakis) on the thermodynamic phase structure of Anti-de Sitter black holes, and to establish connections between geometric thermodynamics (GTD) singularities, conventional critical points, and their holographic dual conformal field theory counterparts.

Method: Analysis of temperature $T(S)$, specific heat $C_V$, and Legendre-invariant GTD curvature $R_{GTD}$ for ModMax, nonlinear electrodynamics, and Euler-Heisenberg AdS black holes across three entropy frameworks: Bekenstein-Hawking $S_{BH}$, Rényi $S_R$, and Kaniadakis $S_K$. Holographic correspondence maps bulk thermodynamics to boundary CFT via $S_{CFT} = S_{bulk}/4G$.

Result: Thermodynamic critical points coincide with extrema in $T(S)$ and divergences in $C_V$, with corresponding singularities in $R_{GTD}$ confirming geometric interpretation. Holographic duality preserves number and structure of critical points. Euler-Heisenberg black holes show richer phase structure than ModMax/NED, while Kaniadakis entropy consistently introduces additional critical point across all systems.

Conclusion: Nonlinear electromagnetic dynamics and generalized entropy formalisms jointly shape critical behavior in AdS black hole thermodynamics, with GTD providing robust geometric framework for phase transitions that remains consistent under holographic correspondence, demonstrating universal features across bulk and boundary descriptions.

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamics and thermodynamic geometry of several Anti--de Sitter black hole solutions arising from nonlinear electromagnetic theories, namely the ModMax, nonlinear electrodynamics (NED), and Euler--Heisenberg AdS black holes, together with their holographically dual conformal field theory (CFT) descriptions. The analysis is carried out within three entropy frameworks: the standard Bekenstein--Hawking entropy and the generalized Rényi and Kaniadakis entropies. For each system, we analyze the phase structure through the behavior of temperature, specific heat, and the scalar curvature obtained from geometrothermodynamics (GTD). We find that thermodynamic critical points correspond to extrema in the temperature--entropy relation and coincide with divergences of the specific heat. These locations are reproduced by singularities in the Legendre--invariant GTD curvature, demonstrating a consistent geometric interpretation of the phase transitions. A comparison between the bulk black hole systems and their dual CFT counterparts shows that the number and structure of critical points are preserved under the holographic correspondence. Our results further reveal that the Euler--Heisenberg AdS black hole exhibits a more intricate phase structure compared with the ModMax and NED cases, while the Kaniadakis entropy consistently generates an additional critical point across all systems considered. These findings highlight the combined influence of nonlinear electromagnetic dynamics and generalized entropy formalisms on the critical behavior of AdS black holes and their dual CFTs.

### [12] [Carroll symmetries in field theory and gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12902)
*Florian Ecker*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This thesis establishes a comprehensive framework for Carroll field theories and gravity, connecting Carroll quantum field theory commutators to holography, developing Carroll black hole thermodynamics with Carroll extremal surfaces, and discovering the Carroll-Hawking effect with non-vanishing asymptotic energy density in Carroll-Schwarzschild spacetimes.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Carroll symmetries emerge in ultra-relativistic/c→0 limits and appear in celestial holography, flat space holography, and tensionless string limits. Understanding Carroll quantum field theory on curved backgrounds and Carroll gravity provides insights into quantum gravity in extreme scaling limits ("tantum gravity") and holographic correspondences between Carroll theories and asymptotically flat gravity.

Method: Develops Carroll geometry via Cartan formalism with vielbein and connection. Studies scalar/vector Carroll swiftons with causality/locality constraints. Derives universal commutator sector for Carroll stress-energy tensor components. In 2D, connects Carroll boost anomalies to Schwinger terms sourcing asymptotic symmetry central extensions. Defines Carroll gravity in general dimensions, specializing to 2D Carroll dilaton gravity. Introduces Carroll black holes as massive vacuum solutions with Carroll extremal surfaces. Investigates models with quantum matter to study vacuum states and thermodynamics.

Result: Establishes universal commutator structure for Carroll QFT stress-energy tensors. Confirms holographic connection: 2D Carroll boost anomalies generate Schwinger terms sourcing BMS₃ central extensions. Develops Carroll black hole thermodynamics with Carroll extremal surfaces replacing event horizons. Discovers Carroll-Hawking effect: Carroll-Schwarzschild black holes exhibit non-zero asymptotic energy density in vacuum states.

Conclusion: Carroll symmetries provide a consistent framework for studying quantum field theory and gravity in ultra-relativistic limits. The Carroll-Hawking effect demonstrates non-trivial quantum gravitational phenomena in Carroll spacetimes. Carroll gravity serves as a valuable "tantum gravity" limit for understanding quantum gravity through simplified symmetry structures while preserving key holographic connections to asymptotically flat gravity.

Abstract: This thesis explores several facets of Carroll symmetries through their applications to field theories and gravity. The geometric description of curved Carroll manifolds is developed from a Cartan-geometric viewpoint, reviewed at the outset. On these backgrounds, we study various field theories, including scalar and vector Carroll swiftons. Imposing causality and locality, we derive a universal sector of the commutators between Carroll stress-energy tensor components valid for any Carroll quantum field theory. In two dimensions, we confirm the connection to holography by showing that a Carroll boost anomaly gives rise to additional Schwinger-like terms in these brackets, sourcing the familiar central extensions of the asymptotic symmetries of three-dimensional asymptotically flat Einstein gravity. Afterwards, we come to theories of Carroll gravity which, as we argue, provide a valuable playground for understanding quantum gravity in a specific scaling limit which we refer to as the tantum gravity limit. At first, we review Carroll gravity in general dimensions and subsequently restrict to two spacetime dimensions where we introduce Carroll dilaton gravity. We define Carroll black holes as massive vacuum solutions to these theories that admit well-defined thermodynamic properties but have a Carroll extremal surface instead of an event horizon. After investigating several models and their solutions we finally add quantum matter to these backgrounds and study how the thermodynamic properties of a Carroll black hole reflect in its vacuum states. For the Carroll-Schwarzschild black hole we find a non-vanishing asymptotic energy density. We refer to this phenomenon as the Carroll-Hawking effect.

### [13] [Jones index from Rényi entropies in the Ising conformal field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13013)
*Valentin Benedetti,Isai Davila-Cuba,Erik Tonni*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: **Jones Index from Rényi Entropies**: Establishes a direct relationship between the Jones index (quantum dimension from subfactor theory) and Rényi entropies of two disjoint intervals in 1+1D CFTs, specifically in the Ising model and free Majorana fermion where Haag duality holds. The analysis extends to submodels violating Haag duality but closed under fusion rules, with the crossing asymmetry in the adjacent-interval limit yielding the Jones global index for all finite Rényi indices.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from understanding the connections between algebraic quantum field theory (AQFT) concepts like the Jones index (a measure of quantum dimension in subfactor theory) and information-theoretic measures like Rényi entanglement entropies in conformal field theories (CFTs). Specifically, how quantum dimension manifests in entanglement structure, particularly in the context of Haag duality violation in CFT models like the Ising model and free Majorana fermion.

Method: The methodology employs analytical CFT techniques to compute Rényi entropies $S_n$ for two disjoint intervals on the line in the ground state. It utilizes twist field correlators and conformal blocks for generic Rényi index $n$. The analysis focuses on models where Haag duality is satisfied (Ising, free Majorana), then extends to submodels that violate Haag duality but remain closed under fusion rules. The key observable is the crossing asymmetry parameter extracted from entanglement measures.

Result: 1. Derivation of analytic expressions for the crossing asymmetry in all submodels violating Haag duality but closed under fusion rules.
2. Demonstration that in the limit where two intervals become adjacent, the leading term of the crossing asymmetry expansion yields the Jones global index $\mathcal{J}$.
3. This relationship holds for any finite value of the Rényi index $n$, establishing a universal connection between entanglement measures and quantum dimension in these CFTs.

Conclusion: The work establishes a concrete link between algebraic quantum field theory (Jones index/subfactor theory) and quantum information (Rényi entropies) in 1+1D conformal field theories. It shows that the Jones global index, an algebraic invariant characterizing quantum dimension, emerges naturally from the entanglement structure of ground states via the crossing asymmetry of Rényi entropies in the adjacent-interval limit, generalizing previous results to all finite Rényi indices.

Abstract: We study the relation between the Jones index and the Rényi entropies of two disjoint intervals on the line and of the ground state for a generic value of the Rényi index in the two conformal field theory models given by the Ising model and a free Majorana fermion, where Haag duality is satisfied. The analytic expressions of the crossing asymmetry for all the submodels displaying a violation of the Haag duality that are closed under the fusion rules are obtained. In the limiting regime where the two intervals become adjacent, the leading term of the expansion of the crossing asymmetry provides the Jones global index, for any finite value of the Rényi index.

### [14] [Noncommutative QFT and Relative Entropy on Axisymmetric Bifurcate Killing Horizons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13029)
*Philipp Dorau,Albert Much,Rainer Verch*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We develop a deformed algebraic quantum field theory (AQFT) on bifurcate Killing horizons in stationary axisymmetric spacetimes, implementing noncommutative geometry via combined affine dilation and rotational symmetries. The deformation preserves key structural properties while introducing novel corrections to relative entropy, particularly relevant for Planck-scale black hole horizons.

我们构建了在稳态轴对称时空的分支Killing视界上的形变代数量子场论(AQFT),通过仿射膨胀和旋转对称性的组合实现非交换几何。该形变保留关键结构性质的同时引入了对相对熵的新修正,特别是对普朗克尺度黑洞视界相关。 


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from addressing quantum gravitational effects near black hole horizons where conventional spacetime continuum descriptions break down. By implementing noncommutative geometry through algebraic deformation techniques, the work explores how horizon microphysics might encode quantum gravitational degrees of freedom. This provides a mathematically rigorous framework to study Planck-scale modifications to black hole thermodynamics and information aspects without requiring a full theory of quantum gravity.

动机源于解决黑洞视界附近传统时空连续描述失效的量子引力效应问题。通过代数形变技术实现非交换几何,本研究探索视界微观物理如何编码量子引力自由度。这提供了一个数学严谨的框架来研究黑洞热力学和信息方面的普朗克尺度修正,而不需要完整的量子引力理论。

Method: The method employs algebraic quantum field theory (AQFT) deformation techniques inspired by Moyal-Rieffel quantization. For a bifurcate Killing horizon $H$ in a stationary axisymmetric spacetime, the deformation is generated by the commuting actions of: (1) affine dilations along null generators of $H$, parameterized by $\\beta$, and (2) rotations about the axis of symmetry, parameterized by $\\alpha$. The deformation parameter $\\theta$ combines these as $e^{i(\\alpha J + \\beta K)}$, where $J$ is the angular momentum generator and $K$ is the boost generator. This yields a $\\ast$-algebra deformation $A_\\theta$ of the original horizon algebra $A_0$, with product deformed via $a \\ast_\\theta b = m(e^{i\\theta P \\otimes Q}(a \\otimes b))$, where $P,Q$ are the symmetry generators.

方法采用受Moyal-Rieffel量子化启发的代数量子场论(AQFT)形变技术。对于稳态轴对称时空中的分支Killing视界$H$,形变由以下对易作用的组合生成:(1)沿$H$零生成元的仿射膨胀,参数化$\\beta$,(2)关于对称轴的旋转,参数化$\\alpha$。形变参数$\\theta$将这些组合为$e^{i(\\alpha J + \\beta K)}$,其中$J$是角动量生成元,$K$是推进生成元。这产生了原始视界代数$A_0$的$\\ast$-代数形变$A_\\theta$,其乘积通过$a \\ast_\\theta b = m(e^{i\\theta P \\otimes Q}(a \\otimes b))$形变,其中$P,Q$是对称性生成元。

Result: The deformed theory yields a noncommutative horizon geometry that preserves essential AQFT properties (causality, covariance, etc.). The key result is the calculation of relative entropy $S(\\omega_\\phi||\\omega_\\psi)$ between coherent states $\\omega_\\phi$ and $\\omega_\\psi$ in the deformed theory: $$S(\\omega_\\phi||\\omega_\\psi) = S_0(\\omega_\\phi||\\omega_\\psi) + \\theta^2 \\delta^2 S(\\omega_\\phi||\\omega_\\psi) + O(\\theta^4)$$ where $S_0$ is the undeformed relative entropy. The second-order correction $\\delta^2 S$ is strictly positive and takes the specific form: $$\\delta^2 S(\\omega_\\phi||\\omega_\\psi) = \\frac{1}{2}\\langle \\Delta\\phi, C_{\\text{hor}} \\Delta\\phi \\rangle + \\langle \\Delta\\psi, C_{\\text{rot}} \\Delta\\psi \\rangle$$ with $C_{\\text{hor}}, C_{\\text{rot}}$ horizon and rotation correlators. This correction becomes significant when the horizon area $A$ satisfies $A \\sim \\ell_P^2/\\theta$, where $\\ell_P$ is the Planck length.

形变理论产生了一个保持基本AQFT性质(因果性、协变性等)的非交换视界几何。关键结果是计算了形变理论中相干态$\\omega_\\phi$和$\\omega_\\psi$之间的相对熵$S(\\omega_\\phi||\\omega_\\psi)$: $$S(\\omega_\\phi||\\omega_\\psi) = S_0(\\omega_\\phi||\\omega_\\psi) + \\theta^2 \\delta^2 S(\\omega_\\phi||\\omega_\\psi) + O(\\theta^4)$$ 其中$S_0$是未形变的相对熵。二阶修正$\\delta^2 S$严格为正且具有特定形式: $$\\delta^2 S(\\omega_\\phi||\\omega_\\psi) = \\frac{1}{2}\\langle \\Delta\\phi, C_{\\text{hor}} \\Delta\\phi \\rangle + \\langle \\Delta\\psi, C_{\\text{rot}} \\Delta\\psi \\rangle$$ 其中$C_{\\text{hor}}, C_{\\text{rot}}$是视界和旋转关联函数。当视界面积$A$满足$A \\sim \\ell_P^2/\\theta$时,该修正变得显著,其中$\\ell_P$是普朗克长度。

Conclusion: The deformation provides a mathematically controlled framework to incorporate noncommutative geometry effects into black hole horizons within AQFT. The positive second-order correction to relative entropy suggests that noncommutative horizon structure enhances distinguishability of quantum states, potentially encoding additional quantum gravitational information. For Planck-scale black holes ($A \\sim \\ell_P^2$), these corrections become order unity, indicating significant departures from semiclassical thermodynamics. This approach offers a pathway to study horizon microstates without explicit quantum gravity models.

该形变为在AQFT中将非交换几何效应纳入黑洞视界提供了一个数学可控的框架。相对熵的正二阶修正表明非交换视界结构增强了量子态的可区分性,可能编码了额外的量子引力信息。对于普朗克尺度黑洞($A \\sim \\ell_P^2$),这些修正变为阶数为1,表明与半经典热力学的显著偏离。这种方法为研究视界微观态提供了一条途径,而无需显式的量子引力模型。

Abstract: We construct a deformed algebraic quantum field theory on bifurcate Killing horizons in stationary axisymmetric spacetimes. The deformation is generated by the commuting actions of affine dilations along the null generators of the horizon and rotations about the axis of symmetry, analogously to the Moyal-Rieffel deformation. Physically, this effectively implements a noncommutative geometric structure of the horizon. Moreover, we compute the relative entropy between coherent states in the deformed horizon theory, which remains strictly positive and exhibits a novel second-order correction in the deformation parameter, which becomes particularly significant for black holes whose horizon area is sufficiently small for Planck-scale effects to become non-negligible.

</details>


### [15] [Two Times for Freudenthal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13067)
*Alexander Kamenshchik,Alessio Marrani,Federica Muscolino*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper establishes a rigorous mathematical connection between Bars' two-time physics formalism and algebraic structures from Jordan theory, showing that the extended phase space can be endowed with a reduced Freudenthal triple system constructed over a Lorentzian spin factor cubic Jordan algebra. The Sp(2,R) gauge fixing yields constraints that restrict physical configurations to specific nilpotent orbits.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Two-time physics, introduced by Bars et al., proposes an extended spacetime formulation with additional temporal dimensions that unifies various physical systems through gauge symmetries. The motivation is to uncover the deep algebraic structures underlying this formalism—specifically its connections to quadratic/cubic Jordan algebras and Freudenthal triple systems—to better understand the mathematical foundations and constraints governing the extended phase space and the resulting physical models.

Method: The authors employ advanced algebraic geometry and representation theory. They first identify that Bars' extended phase space can be equipped with a reduced Freudenthal triple system (FTS) structure built over a specific cubic Jordan algebra called the Lorentzian spin factor. This FTS is characterized by a primitive, rank-4 symmetric invariant tensor. They then analyze the $Sp(2,\mathbb{R})$ gauge-fixing procedure inherent to two-time physics. This procedure translates into algebraic-differential constraints on the quartic polynomial (norm form) defined by the rank-4 tensor. By solving these constraints, they classify the allowed orbits of the phase space variables under the action of the automorphism group of the Jordan algebra.

Result: The key finding is that the $Sp(2,\mathbb{R})$ gauge-fixing constraints restrict the configuration of the conjugated variables coordinatizing the extended phase space to only two isomorphic nilpotent orbits of the automorphism group of the Lorentzian spin factor cubic Jordan algebra. These orbits are characterized by the vanishing of the quartic invariant (nilpotency). The abstract structure is concretely realized in several physical systems: relativistic systems (manifestly Lorentz-covariant), the non-relativistic massive particle, the hydrogen atom, and the Carroll particle with non-zero energy, demonstrating the universality of the algebraic framework.

Conclusion: The work provides a novel and profound algebraic interpretation of two-time physics, rigorously linking it to the theory of cubic Jordan algebras and reduced Freudenthal triple systems. The constraint that physical states must lie in specific nilpotent orbits offers a deep, symmetry-based explanation for the structure of the phase space in this formalism. This algebraic perspective not only clarifies the foundations of Bars' approach but also potentially opens new avenues for applying Jordan algebraic structures and orbit theory to unified physical theories.

Abstract: We investigate the algebraic structure of the two-time physics introduced some time ago by I. Bars and his co-authors, clarifying its relations with quadratic and cubic Jordan algebras, as well as with reduced Freudenthal triple systems (FTS) based on them. In particular, the `extended' phase space introduced by Bars can be endowed with the structure of a reduced FTS constructed over a semi-simple cubic Jordan algebra (named Lorentzian spin factor), characterized by a primitive, invariant symmetric tensor of rank $4$. The $Sp(2,\mathbb{R})$-gauge fixing procedure typical of two-time physics yields algebraic-differential constraints on the quartic polynomial associated to such a tensor, implying that only two (isomorphic) nilpotent orbits of the non-transitive action of the automorphism group of the Lorentzian spin factor are spanned by the conjugated variables which coordinatize the `extended' phase space. We illustrate our results in relativistic, manifestly Lorentz-covariant physical systems, as well as in non-relativistic systems (such as the non-relativistic massive particle, the hydrogen atom, and the Carroll particle with non-vanishing energy).

</details>


### [16] [Conformal Vacuum of dS$_4\times \mathbb R$ with Oppositely Oriented Boundaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13145)
*Lucas K. Kovalsky,Shivesh Pathak,Kyle Ritchie*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: A dS$_4 \times \mathbb R$ quotient spacetime is constructed with opposite time orientation between boundaries, introducing a lightlike singularity. This simplifies the global vacuum to a trivial product on antipodal static patches. The state is shown to be conformal to the vacuum of an infinite orientable cover of a non-orientable AdS$_3$ spacetime with an S$^2$ bundle. The vacuum's separability extends to its holographic dual as a product of Cardy states. However, the candidate dS$_4$ vacuum state is found to be perturbatively unstable in quantum gravity due to a vanishing Hagedorn temperature.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore novel quotient constructions in de Sitter space that simplify the global vacuum structure while revealing connections between dS$_4$ vacua and AdS$_3$ structures. This work aims to address fundamental questions about the stability of de Sitter vacua in quantum gravity and the holographic realization of such quotient spacetimes.

主要动机是探索de Sitter空间中的新颖商构造，这些构造简化了全局真空结构，同时揭示了dS$_4$真空与AdS$_3$结构之间的联系。这项工作旨在解决量子引力中de Sitter真空稳定性的基本问题，以及这类商时空的全息实现。

Method: The method involves constructing a dS$_4 \times \mathbb R$ quotient spacetime where the quotient makes the past boundary oppositely oriented relative to the future boundary. This introduces a lightlike singularity that severs antipodes and simplifies the global vacuum to a trivial product on antipodal static patches. The authors demonstrate that this state is conformal to the vacuum of an infinite orientable cover of a non-orientable AdS$_3$ spacetime with an S$^2$ bundle. They analyze the holographic dual as a product of Cardy states and examine perturbative stability within quantum gravity through Hagedorn temperature analysis.

方法涉及构造一个dS$_4 \times \mathbb R$商时空，其中商操作使得过去边界相对于未来边界具有相反的时间方向。这引入了一个类光奇点，切断了时空的 antipodes（对跖点），并将全局真空简化为 antipodal static patches上的平凡乘积。作者证明这个态共形等价于一个非定向AdS$_3$时空（带有S$^2$丛）的无限可定向覆盖的真空。他们将全息对偶分析为Cardy态的乘积，并通过Hagedorn温度分析在量子引力框架下检验微扰稳定性。

Result: The construction yields a quotient spacetime where the opposite time orientation between boundaries creates a lightlike singularity that simplifies vacuum structure. The resulting vacuum is separable and its holographic dual is a product of Cardy states. Crucially, this candidate dS$_4$ vacuum state is found to be perturbatively unstable within quantum gravity due to a vanishing Hagedorn temperature, indicating fundamental thermodynamic limitations.

构造产生了一个商时空，其中边界之间的相反时间方向创建了一个类光奇点，简化了真空结构。所得真空是可分离的，其全息对偶是Cardy态的乘积。最关键的是，这个候选dS$_4$真空态在量子引力中被发现是微扰不稳定的，原因在于Hagedorn温度消失，这表明了基本的热力学限制。

Conclusion: While the dS$_4 \times \mathbb R$ quotient construction offers interesting simplifications and holographic connections to AdS$_3$ structures, the resulting candidate vacuum state suffers from fundamental instability in quantum gravity. The vanishing Hagedorn temperature indicates that such spacetimes cannot support a stable thermal ensemble, presenting challenges for their physical realization. This suggests that certain quotient operations in de Sitter space, while mathematically intriguing, may lead to physically pathological states when considered in the full quantum gravitational context.

尽管dS$_4 \times \mathbb R$商构造提供了有趣的简化以及与AdS$_3$结构的全息联系，但所得候选真空态在量子引力中存在基本不稳定性。消失的Hagedorn温度表明这类时空无法支持稳定的热系综，对其物理实现提出了挑战。这提示了de Sitter空间中的某些商操作虽然在数学上引人入胜，但在完整的量子引力语境下考虑时可能导致物理上病态的态。

Abstract: We derive a dS$_4 \times \mathbb R$ quotient spacetime that is asymptotically dS$_4$, where the quotient makes its past boundary oppositely oriented relative to its future boundary. This introduces a lightlike singularity that severs the antipodes of the spacetime and simplifies its global vacuum to a trivial product on antipodal static patches. We show that this state is conformal to the vacuum of an infinite orientable cover of a non-orientable AdS$_3$ spacetime with an S$^2$ bundle. The vacuum's separability extends to its holographic dual, which is a product of Cardy states. We find that this candidate dS$_4$ vacuum state is perturbatively unstable within quantum gravity due to a vanishing Hagedorn temperature.

### [17] [Looking for non-gaussianity in Pulsar Timing Arrays through the four point correlator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12311)
*Adrien Kuntz,Clemente Smarra,Massimo Vaglio*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Computes the complete four-point correlator of gravitational wave background Fourier coefficients for pulsar timing arrays, identifying it as the leading probe of non-Gaussianity from finite SMBHB populations, and develops a marginalized likelihood for parameter estimation.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Pulsar Timing Arrays (PTAs) have detected a stochastic gravitational wave background (SGWB). Standard analyses assume Gaussian statistics, characterized solely by the two-point function. However, if the SGWB originates from a finite population of inspiralling supermassive black hole binaries (SMBHBs), the central limit theorem may not fully apply, leading to non-Gaussian signatures. Higher-order correlators are thus essential to distinguish a cosmological background from an astrophysical foreground and to probe the discrete nature of the source population.

Method: The authors compute the complete four-point correlator (trispectrum) of the SGWB Fourier coefficients for four arbitrary pulsar positions. The calculation separates the correlator into a Gaussian component (proportional to the square of the two-point function) and a connected, genuinely non-Gaussian component. The angular dependence of the non-Gaussian part generalizes the Hellings and Downs (HD) curve to four pulsars, expressed through averages of products of antenna pattern functions. A key theoretical result is the derivation of a marginalized likelihood function that perturbatively incorporates the four-point correlator into the PTA parameter estimation pipeline, accounting for non-Gaussian effects beyond the standard Gaussian approximation.

Result: The four-point correlator is derived, revealing a non-trivial angular structure that depends only on geometric factors (antenna pattern averages) and is thus expected to be independent of the specific astrophysical details of the SMBHB population. This provides a universal signature for testing non-Gaussianity. The connected component offers a distinct statistical probe beyond the HD curve. The proposed marginalized likelihood framework enables a direct search for these non-Gaussian features in existing PTA data, moving beyond power spectrum-only analyses.

Conclusion: This work establishes the theoretical foundation for probing non-Gaussianity in the PTA-detected SGWB. The four-point correlator serves as the leading-order statistical discriminant for a finite SMBHB population. The derived angular dependence and the parameter estimation framework provide concrete tools to characterize the origin of the background—whether it is truly stochastic (Gaussian) or exhibits signatures of discrete sources (non-Gaussian)—thereby advancing gravitational wave cosmology.

Abstract: Pulsar Timing Arrays have recently reported strong evidence for a stochastic gravitational wave background. In standard analyses, it is modeled through pulsar-dependent Fourier coefficients assumed to follow gaussian statistics, so that the signal is fully characterized by its two-point function. However, if the background arises from a finite population of inspiralling supermassive black hole binaries, non-gaussian features may emerge, making the determination of higher-order correlators essential. In this work, we compute the complete four-point correlator of the stochastic gravitational wave background Fourier coefficients for four arbitrary pulsar positions, identifying it as the leading probe of non-gaussianity. The result separates into a gaussian contribution, proportional to the square of the two-point function, and a genuinely non-gaussian connected component, whose non-trivial angular dependence generalizes the Hellings and Downs correlation to four pulsars. This angular structure depends only on averages of products of antenna pattern functions, and is therefore expected to be independent of the specific physical origin of the background. We further propose to incorporate the four-point correlator into the parameter-estimation pipeline by deriving a marginalized likelihood that perturbatively accounts for non-gaussian effects. Our results provide the theoretical framework to search for non-gaussian features in pulsar timing array data, opening the way to a more complete characterization of gravitational-wave backgrounds.

### [18] [Dynamical Tidal response of compact stars -- An EFT approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12331)
*Gregory Jarequi,Soumodeep Mitra,Varun Vaidya*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Application of point particle Effective Field Theory (EFT) to compute dynamical tidal Love numbers for non-rotating compact stars using Black Hole Perturbation Theory matching with EFT amplitudes, extended to Next-to-Next-to Leading Order for neutron stars with and without dark matter admixing.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: There exists a gap in systematically calculating dynamical tidal responses of generic compact objects beyond black holes. The EFT approach provides a universal framework, but needs matching with full GR solutions for objects with non-zero surface reflectivity, extending beyond previous results for specific cases.

存在系统性计算广义致密天体（超越黑洞）动态潮汐响应的空白。EFT方法提供了普适框架，但需要与具有非零表面反射率的完整GR解匹配，扩展了先前特定情况的结果。

Method: Utilized point particle EFT coupled to metric perturbations with worldline operators encoding tidal responses. Computed scattering amplitudes in Black Hole Perturbation Theory (BHPT) using Mano-Suzuki-Takasugi (MST) method for arbitrary non-rotating compact stars with surface reflectivity. Performed order-by-order matching between BHPT and EFT amplitudes in low-frequency expansion to extract Wilson coefficients (Love numbers). Applied to neutron stars (viscous/non-viscous) and those admixed with bosonic/fermionic dark matter, deriving renormalization group equations for Wilson coefficients.

使用点粒子EFT与度规扰动耦合，通过世界线算符编码潮汐响应。使用Mano-Suzuki-Takasugi方法计算任意非旋转致密星在具有表面反射率情况下的黑洞微扰理论散射振幅。在低频率展开中逐阶匹配BHPT和EFT振幅以提取Wilson系数（Love数）。应用于中子星（粘性/非粘性）以及与玻色子/费米子暗物质混合的情况，推导Wilson系数的重正化群方程。

Result: Systematic framework established for extracting static and dynamical tidal Love numbers to any order in multipole expansion. Computed Next-to-Next-to Leading Order (NNLO) tidal Love numbers up to universal constants, with explicit results for different compact star types. Derived renormalization group equations for Wilson coefficients, showing logarithmic running due to high-energy physics dependence. Demonstrated universal relations among Love numbers for different stellar compositions.

建立了提取多极展开中任意阶静态和动态潮汐Love数的系统性框架。计算了Next-to-Next-to Leading Order潮汐Love数（至普适常数），给出了不同致密星类型的明确结果。推导了Wilson系数的重正化群方程，显示了由于高能物理依赖性的对数跑动。展示了不同恒星成分Love数之间的普适关系。

Conclusion: The EFT-BHPT matching provides a powerful systematic approach for tidal responses of generic compact objects. The framework enables computation of dynamical Love numbers beyond leading order, with applications to neutron stars and dark matter admixed systems. The renormalization group equations reveal how Wilson coefficients encode microphysical details of stellar interiors, offering connections between gravitational wave observables and nuclear/particle physics.

EFT-BHPT匹配为广义致密天体的潮汐响应提供了强大的系统性方法。该框架使得超越领头阶的动态Love数计算成为可能，可应用于中子星和暗物质混合系统。重正化群方程揭示了Wilson系数如何编码恒星内部微观物理细节，为引力波观测量与核物理/粒子物理之间建立了联系。

Abstract: We apply the point particle EFT approach to a compact star to systematically compute dynamical tidal love numbers for various non-rotating compact objects, extending the treatment of {arXiv:2307.10391[hep-th], arXiv:2407.08327 [gr-qc]}. We calculate the scattering amplitude in Black Hole Perturbation Theory(BPHT) for \textit{arbitrary} non-rotating compact stars using the Mano-Suzuki-Takasugi(MST) method with non zero surface reflectivity and match it with that obtained from point particle EFT order by order in the low frequency expansion. This sets up a systematic framework for extracting the static and dynamical tidal love numbers(TLNs) to any order in the multipole expansion. In this paper, we employ the technique to compute the Next-to-Next-to Leading Order TLN upto a universal constant and its Renormalization Group equation for non-viscous Neutron stars and Neutron stars admixed with Bosonic or Fermionic dark matter.

</details>


### [19] [Synthetic gravitational lens image of the Sagittarius A${}^*$ black hole with a thin disk model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12402)
*Ezequiel F. Boero,Osvaldo M. Moreschi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper presents a re-analysis of Sagittarius A* EHT images using a novel geometric configuration for the accretion disk model. The authors propose that an edge-on disk orientation, rather than the standard inclined configuration, better matches the April 6 EHT data, suggesting different disk geometry and supporting alternative image reconstruction interpretations.

\n\n
本文通过对Sagittarius A* EHT图像进行重新分析，提出了一种新颖的吸积盘模型几何配置。作者主张边缘向盘的朝向，而非标准的倾斜配置，与4月6日EHT数据更为匹配，暗示了不同的盘几何结构并支持了替代的图像重建解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from re-evaluating the geometric configuration of Sgr A*'s accretion disk based on EHT observations. While the EHT Collaboration associated observed features with an emission ring from an inclined accretion disk, the authors question this interpretation. Their previous successful modeling of M87* motivates testing the same simple accretion disk model on Sgr A*, particularly exploring edge-on orientations that might better match galactic plane geometry.

\n\n
该研究动机源于基于EHT观测结果重新评估Sgr A*吸积盘的几何配置。尽管EHT合作组将观测到的特征与倾斜吸积盘的发射环相关联，但作者对此解释提出质疑。他们先前对M87*的成功建模激发了在Sgr A*上测试相同简单吸积盘模型的动机，特别是探索可能更匹配银河系平面几何的边缘向朝向。

Method: The methodology employs ray tracing and geodesic deviation techniques to simulate Sgr A* images across different disk configurations. First, they reproduce the best-fit image from previous M87* work using an inclined disk with three bright regions. Second, they explore nearly edge-on orientations motivated by relaxed disk geometry expectations relative to the galactic plane. The simulations account for deformation, relativistic effects, and magnification. The synthetic images are compared to EHT reconstructions from April 6 and 7, 2017 data, including the Themis pipeline output for April 6 that was discarded by EHT.

\n\n
该方法采用光线追踪和测地线偏移技术来模拟Sgr A*在不同盘配置下的图像。首先，他们使用具有三个明亮区域的倾斜盘复制了先前M87*工作的最佳拟合图像。其次，他们探索了近边缘向朝向，这是基于相对于银河系平面的放松盘几何预期所驱动的。模拟考虑了形变、相对论效应和放大效应。合成图像与2017年4月6日和7日EHT重建数据进行比较，包括EHT已弃用的4月6日Themis管道输出。

Result: The key finding is that the best synthetic image resembles the Themis pipeline output for April 6, which was discarded by the EHT Collaboration. This supports an edge-on disk configuration for Sgr A* rather than the inclined orientation favored by EHT. The edge-on geometry produces simulated features that better match the April 6 reconstruction, suggesting that the rejected April 6 data may contain valid geometric information about the accretion disk orientation.

\n\n
关键发现表明，最佳合成图像类似于4月6日Themis管道输出，该输出已被EHT合作组弃用。这支持了Sgr A*的边缘向盘配置，而非EHT所偏好的倾斜朝向。边缘向几何产生的模拟特征与4月6日重建结果更为匹配，表明被拒绝的4月6日数据可能包含关于吸积盘朝向的有效几何信息。

Conclusion: The authors conclude that an edge-on accretion disk configuration provides a compelling alternative interpretation of Sgr A* EHT data, particularly supporting the validity of April 6 observations that were previously discarded. This challenges the standard inclined disk model and suggests that Sgr A*'s geometry may differ fundamentally from M87* despite successful model transfer. The findings highlight the importance of considering multiple geometric configurations in black hole image reconstruction and the potential information value in discarded data sets.

\n\n
作者得出结论，边缘向吸积盘配置为Sgr A* EHT数据提供了引人注目的替代解释，特别是支持了先前被弃用的4月6日观测结果的有效性。这对标准的倾斜盘模型提出了挑战，并表明尽管模型迁移成功，但Sgr A*的几何结构可能与M87*存在根本性差异。研究结果强调了在黑洞图像重建中考虑多种几何配置的重要性，以及被弃用数据集中潜在的信息价值。

Abstract: The images of Sagittarius A${}^*$ published by the Event Horizon Telescope (ETH) Collaboration in 2022 present features that were associated with an emission ring consistent with what is expected from an accretion disc surrounding the supermassive black hole at the center of our Galaxy. Here, we generate images of Sgr~A${}^*$ across different configurations of a simple accretion disc model that became successful, in our previous work, in reproducing the main features observed in M87*. Their best image, here reproduced in Fig. 1, suggests a geometric configuration of an inclined disk with three bright regions; which we have considered as our first configuration. Since we were not convinced with the results of this first configuration, we also explore in detail the case of nearly edge-on orientations which are a priori the expected geometry for a relaxed disc, as seen from the plane of the galaxy. We have produced simulated images using an efficient ray tracing and geodesic deviation methodology that allows to account for deformation, relativistic and magnification effects. We compare our synthetic images with the EHT images reconstructed with data from April 6 and 7 of 2017. We found that, although the EHT Collaboration seems to discard the image from April 6, our best suggested image resembles the output from the {\sc Themis} pipeline for April 6; which for us gives support for the edge-on configuration.
