### [20] [An efficient higher-order WKB code for quasinormal modes and greybody factors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12466)
*Roman A. Konoplya,Jerzy Matyjasek,Alexander Zhidenko*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper presents an optimized WKB code for quasinormal modes that replaces direct evaluation of analytic WKB formulas with Taylor expansion of the effective potential around its maximum, achieving orders of magnitude speedup for complicated potentials while maintaining accuracy.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing higher-order WKB codes for quasinormal modes require evaluating full analytic expressions for each specific potential, which becomes computationally expensive for complicated potentials involving non-rational functions. The motivation is to significantly reduce computation time while preserving the high accuracy achieved through Padé resummation techniques.

Method: The core innovation is expanding the effective potential $V(r)$ in a Taylor series around its maximum $r_0$ rather than evaluating the full analytic WKB formula for each potential. This replaces complicated function evaluations with polynomial operations, dramatically reducing computational overhead while maintaining the accuracy of higher-order WKB expansions with Padé resummation.

Result: The optimized code achieves substantial speed improvements, reaching orders of magnitude faster computation for complicated potentials with non-rational functions, while preserving the numerical accuracy of the original higher-order WKB method with Padé resummation.

Conclusion: Taylor expansion of the effective potential around its maximum provides an efficient optimization strategy for WKB quasinormal mode calculations, enabling faster computations for complex potentials without sacrificing accuracy, making the method more practical for extensive parameter space studies.

Abstract: The higher-order WKB Mathematica code for computing quasinormal modes, whose accuracy was significantly enhanced through extensions to higher orders and, in particular, through the use of Padé resummation, has been widely employed in numerous studies over the past several years. In this work, we present an updated and optimized version of the code. The main improvement consists in expanding the effective potential in a Taylor series around its maximum, rather than evaluating the full analytic expression of the WKB formula for each specific potential. This modification leads to a substantial reduction in computation time. In cases where the effective potential is complicated and involves non-rational functions, the speed gain can reach several orders of magnitude, while preserving the accuracy of the method.

</details>


### [21] [Thermodynamics and information recovery of Schwarzschild AdS black holes in Cotton gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12524)
*Yahya Ladghami,Brahim Asfour,Francisco S. N. Lobo,Taoufik Ouali*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We investigate Schwarzschild-AdS black holes in Cotton gravity, analyzing thermodynamics with cosmological constant as pressure and Cotton parameter as variable, and applying quantum extremal island prescription to compute entanglement entropy of Hawking radiation. The Cotton parameter critically influences phase structure: positive values yield Van der Waals-like criticality with extremal limits, while negative values exhibit different behavior. Island formula restores unitary Page curve with late-time entropy saturating at twice Bekenstein-Hawking value, connecting thermodynamics, information recovery, and modified gravity.

我们研究Cotton引力中的Schwarzschild-AdS黑洞，以宇宙学常数为压力、Cotton参数为变量分析热力学，并应用量子极值岛公式计算霍金辐射的纠缠熵。Cotton参数对相结构有决定性影响：正值产生类范德瓦尔斯临界性与极值极限，负值则呈现不同行为。岛公式恢复了幺正的Page曲线，晚期熵饱和于Bekenstein-Hawking值的两倍，建立了热力学、信息恢复和修正引力之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding black hole thermodynamics in modified gravity theories is crucial for exploring quantum gravity effects beyond general relativity. Cotton gravity, a geometric theory based on the Cotton tensor, offers a promising framework with potentially observable signatures. The connection between black hole thermodynamics, phase transitions, and quantum information recovery through the island prescription remains largely unexplored in this context. This work aims to systematically investigate Schwarzschild-AdS black holes in Cotton gravity, treating the cosmological constant as thermodynamic pressure and the Cotton parameter as an independent variable, while applying the quantum extremal island formula to study information recovery from Hawking radiation.

理解修正引力理论中的黑洞热力学对于探索超出广义相对论的量子引力效应至关重要。基于Cotton张量的几何理论Cotton引力为研究提供了有前景的框架，并可能产生可观测的效应。通过岛公式建立的黑洞热力学、相变与量子信息恢复之间的联系在此背景下尚未得到充分探索。本研究旨在系统研究Cotton引力中的Schwarzschild-AdS黑洞，将宇宙学常数视为热力学压力、Cotton参数视为独立变量，同时应用量子极值岛公式研究霍金辐射中的信息恢复。

Method: We employ Cotton gravity framework with action $S = \int d^4x \sqrt{-g}(R - 2\Lambda + \alpha C_{\mu\nu\rho}C^{\mu\nu\rho})$, where $C_{\mu\nu\rho}$ is the Cotton tensor and $\alpha$ the Cotton parameter. The Schwarzschild-AdS solution is analyzed with metric $ds^2 = -f(r)dt^2 + f(r)^{-1}dr^2 + r^2 d\Omega^2$, where $f(r)$ incorporates Cotton corrections. Thermodynamics is studied with cosmological constant as pressure $P = -\Lambda/(8\pi)$, black hole mass as enthalpy, and Cotton parameter treated as independent variable. Phase structure is analyzed through free energy $G = M - TS$, heat capacity, and equation of state. For quantum information analysis, we apply the island prescription with generalized entropy $S_{\text{gen}} = \frac{\text{Area}(\partial I)}{4G_N} + S_{\text{matter}}$, extremizing over island regions. The entanglement entropy of Hawking radiation is computed both with and without islands, yielding the Page curve.

我们采用Cotton引力框架，作用量为$S = \int d^4x \sqrt{-g}(R - 2\Lambda + \alpha C_{\mu\nu\rho}C^{\mu\nu\rho})$，其中$C_{\mu\nu\rho}$为Cotton张量，$\alpha$为Cotton参数。分析Schwarzschild-AdS解，度规为$ds^2 = -f(r)dt^2 + f(r)^{-1}dr^2 + r^2 d\Omega^2$，其中$f(r)$包含Cotton修正。热力学研究将宇宙学常数视为压力$P = -\Lambda/(8\pi)$，黑洞质量视为焓，Cotton参数作为独立变量处理。通过自由能$G = M - TS$、热容和状态方程分析相结构。量子信息分析应用岛公式，广义熵为$S_{\text{gen}} = \frac{\text{Area}(\partial I)}{4G_N} + S_{\text{matter}}$，在岛区域上进行极值化。计算有无岛情况下的霍金辐射纠缠熵，得到Page曲线。

Result: Key findings: (1) Bekenstein-Hawking area law $S = A/4G$ remains valid in Cotton gravity despite modifications to spacetime geometry. (2) Cotton parameter $\alpha$ dramatically affects thermodynamic phase structure: for $\alpha > 0$, black holes admit extremal limits and exhibit Van der Waals-like criticality with first and second order phase transitions; for $\alpha < 0$, no extremal limit exists and critical behavior disappears. (3) Information recovery via island prescription: without islands, entanglement entropy grows linearly with time $S_{\text{EE}} \sim t/(\beta G_N)$, violating unitarity; with islands after Page time $t_{\text{Page}}$, entropy saturates at $S_{\text{late}} = 2S_{\text{BH}}$, restoring Page curve. (4) Page time depends on Cotton parameter: for $\alpha > 0$, $t_{\text{Page}} \sim \frac{S_{\text{BH}}}{T}$ exhibits critical behavior near phase transitions; for $\alpha < 0$, small black holes recover information rapidly ($t_{\text{Page}}$ small) while large ones more slowly, with pressure reducing Page time. (5) Direct connection established between thermodynamic phase transitions and information recovery timescales.

主要发现：(1) 尽管时空几何存在修正，Bekenstein-Hawking面积律$S = A/4G$在Cotton引力中仍然成立。(2) Cotton参数$\alpha$显著影响热力学相结构：当$\alpha > 0$时，黑洞存在极值极限并表现出类范德瓦尔斯临界性，具有一级和二级相变；当$\alpha < 0$时，不存在极值极限且临界行为消失。(3) 通过岛公式实现信息恢复：无岛时，纠缠熵随时间线性增长$S_{\text{EE}} \sim t/(\beta G_N)$，违反幺正性；在Page时间$t_{\text{Page}}$后引入岛，熵饱和于$S_{\text{late}} = 2S_{\text{BH}}$，恢复Page曲线。(4) Page时间依赖于Cotton参数：$\alpha > 0$时，$t_{\text{Page}} \sim \frac{S_{\text{BH}}}{T}$在相变附近表现出临界行为；$\alpha < 0$时，小黑洞快速恢复信息($t_{\text{Page}}$较小)而大黑洞较慢，压力减小Page时间。(5) 建立了热力学相变与信息恢复时间尺度之间的直接联系。

Conclusion: This work establishes a comprehensive connection between modified gravity thermodynamics and quantum information recovery in black hole physics. Cotton gravity preserves the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy-area relation while introducing rich thermodynamic phase structure controlled by the Cotton parameter. The successful application of the island prescription demonstrates unitarity restoration in Cotton gravity, with Page time exhibiting critical behavior linked to thermodynamic phase transitions. The results reveal that modified gravity parameters not only affect classical thermodynamics but also quantum information recovery timescales, providing a framework to test quantum gravity effects through thermodynamic and information-theoretic observables. Future work could extend this analysis to rotating black holes, higher dimensions, and other modified gravity theories.

本研究建立了修正引力热力学与黑洞物理中量子信息恢复之间的全面联系。Cotton引力在保持Bekenstein-Hawking熵-面积关系的同时，通过Cotton参数引入丰富的热力学相结构。岛公式的成功应用证明了Cotton引力中幺正性的恢复，Page时间表现出与热力学相变相关的临界行为。结果表明，修正引力参数不仅影响经典热力学，也影响量子信息恢复的时间尺度，为通过热力学和信息理论可观测量测试量子引力效应提供了框架。未来工作可将此分析扩展至旋转黑洞、更高维度及其他修正引力理论。

Abstract: We study Schwarzschild AdS black holes in Cotton gravity, focusing on their thermodynamics and information recovery via the island formula. Treating the cosmological constant as pressure and the Cotton parameter as an independent variable, we find that the Bekenstein-Hawking area law holds, while the Cotton parameter dramatically affects phase structure. For a positive Cotton parameter, black holes admit an extremal limit and exhibit Van der Waals-like criticality with first and second order phase transitions; for a negative Cotton parameter, no extremal limit or criticality occurs. Using the island prescription, we show that without islands, the entanglement entropy of Hawking radiation grows unboundedly, violating unitarity, while including islands after Page time restores the Page curve, with late-time entropy saturating at twice the Bekenstein-Hawking value. Page time can be expressed in terms of thermodynamic quantities, displaying critical behavior for positive Cotton parameter, whereas in negative Cotton gravity small black holes recover information rapidly and large ones more slowly, with pressure reducing Page time. Our results reveal a direct link between black hole thermodynamics, quantum information recovery, and modified gravity

</details>

Abstract: We investigate spherically symmetric and static traversable wormholes supported by exotic matter, focusing on solutions sourced by physically motivated dark matter energy density profiles. Considering the Thomas-Fermi-type distribution, we construct explicit forms of the shape function $b(r)$ and analyze the resulting radial and tangential pressures, carefully addressing the requirements of the flare-out condition at the throat and the absence of horizons. We explore zero-tidal-force configurations as well as inhomogeneous equations of state, demonstrating how appropriate choices of the radial pressure allow for finite and well-behaved redshift functions throughout the spacetime. Boundary conditions at a finite radius are implemented to ensure vanishing energy density and pressures, and asymptotic expansions are derived to characterize the behavior of the metric and matter content near the edge of the dark matter halo. Additionally, we reformulate the Einstein field equations entirely in terms of the energy density, radial and tangential pressures, and their derivatives, providing a framework to analyze the matter distribution independently of the explicit metric functions. Our results offer a systematic methodology to construct physically consistent wormhole geometries supported by realistic dark matter halos, highlighting the intricate interplay between matter profiles, equations of state, and geometric constraints.

### [23] [Shaving off soft hairs and the black hole image memory effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12670)
*Shaoqi Hou,Zong-Hong Zhu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: [This paper investigates observable signatures of soft hairs on Kerr black holes through their gravitational images. It finds that soft hairs induce time-independent rotation and dilation effects plus constant-velocity drifting in celestial images, creating detectable "image memory effects" when soft hair changes. The effect magnitude scales with primary black hole mass and spin but decreases with mass ratio, though current detector resolution limitations make detection challenging without cosmological expansion effects.]

[这篇论文通过引力图像研究了Kerr黑洞上soft hairs的可观测特征。研究发现soft hairs会在天体图像中产生时间无关的旋转和膨胀效应，以及恒速漂移，当soft hair发生变化时会产生可检测的"图像记忆效应"。效应大小与主黑洞质量和自旋成正比，但与质量比成反比，尽管当前探测器分辨率限制使得不考虑宇宙膨胀效应时检测具有挑战性。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [Soft hairs are Noether charges associated with generalized Bondi-Metzner-Sachs (BMS) symmetries that provide theoretical insight into black hole information paradox and quantum gravity. However, direct observational evidence for soft hairs remains elusive. This work aims to bridge the theoretical construct with potential astrophysical observables by studying how soft hairs manifest in black hole images, particularly through time-dependent effects that could be detected via image memory effects.]

[Soft hairs是与广义Bondi-Metzner-Sachs (BMS)对称性相关的Noether荷，为黑洞信息悖论和量子引力提供了理论见解。然而，soft hairs的直接观测证据仍然难以捉摸。这项工作旨在通过研究soft hairs如何在黑洞图像中显现，特别是通过可通过图像记忆效应检测到的时间相关效应，将理论构造与潜在的天体物理可观测量联系起来。]

Method: [Theoretical analysis combining black hole perturbation theory with soft hair formalism applied to Kerr spacetime. Uses generalized BMS symmetry framework to derive effects on black hole images. Studies eternal soft-haired Kerr black holes first, then examines dynamic soft hair changes from emission processes. Numerical estimation of effect magnitude for astrophysical systems like supermassive black holes with stellar-mass companions. Assumes celestial plane imaging and analyzes angular dependence of image distortions.]

[理论分析将黑洞微扰理论与应用于Kerr时空的soft hair形式结合。使用广义BMS对称性框架推导对黑洞图像的影响。首先研究永恒的soft-haired Kerr黑洞，然后检查发射过程导致的动态soft hair变化。对大质量黑洞与恒星质量伴星等天体物理系统的效应大小进行数值估计。假设天体平面成像并分析图像畸变的角依赖关系。]

Result: [Soft-haired Kerr black hole images exhibit three distinct effects compared to bald counterparts: 1) rotation (angular shift independent of time), 2) dilation (magnification/demagnification independent of time), and 3) drifting at constant speed in fixed direction. All effects show angular dependence. Soft hair changes from gravitational/electromagnetic wave emissions cause image roaming in observer's view - the "image memory effect." For a spinning supermassive black hole with stellar-mass companion, effect magnitude $\Delta\theta \propto M_{\text{BH}}$, increases with spin parameter $a$, but decreases with mass ratio $m_2/m_1$. The effect is generally below current and future detector angular resolution if cosmological expansion is ignored.]

[与无soft hair的对应黑洞相比，soft-haired Kerr黑洞图像显示出三种不同效应：1) 旋转（与时间无关的角度偏移），2) 膨胀（与时间无关的放大/缩小），3) 沿固定方向的恒速漂移。所有效应都显示角依赖关系。引力波或电磁波发射导致的soft hair变化会引起观察者视野中的图像漫游-"图像记忆效应"。对于一个具有恒星质量伴星的旋转超大质量黑洞，效应大小$\Delta\theta \propto M_{\text{BH}}$，随自旋参数$a$增加，但随质量比$m_2/m_1$减小。如果不考虑宇宙膨胀效应，该效应通常低于当前和未来探测器的角分辨率。]

Conclusion: [Soft hairs on Kerr black holes produce potentially observable image distortions with distinct rotation, dilation, and drifting signatures. The time-dependent image memory effect during soft hair changes provides a theoretical smoking gun for soft hair existence. However, practical detection remains challenging due to small angular scales. Future improvements in detector resolution or consideration of cosmological expansion effects may enable observational tests of this fundamental aspect of black hole physics and BMS symmetries.]

[Kerr黑洞上的soft hairs产生具有独特旋转、膨胀和漂移特征的可观测图像畸变。soft hair变化期间的时间相关图像记忆效应为soft hair存在提供了理论上的"确凿证据"。然而，由于角尺度小，实际检测仍具挑战性。未来探测器分辨率的改进或宇宙膨胀效应的考虑可能使这一黑洞物理学和BMS对称性基本方面的观测测试成为可能。]

Abstract: Soft hairs of black holes are the Noether charges associated to the generalized Bondi-Metzner-Sachs symmetries. In this work, the images of soft-haired Kerr black holes were studied. For an eternal black hole, the image is rotated, dilated and drifting compared to that of the bald counterpart in the celestial plane. The rotation and the dilation are independent of the time, while the drifting is at a constant speed and in a fixed direction. These effects all depend on angular directions. The soft hair of an astronomical black hole can change due to the emission of the gravitational or electromagnetic wave from the various physical processes occurring in the vicinity of the horizon. Then, the image roams in the observer's view, causing the image memory effect, the smoking gun for the existence of the soft hair. The magnitude of the image memory effect of a huge, spinning black hole accompanied by a much smaller one was estimated. It turns out that this effect is proportional to the mass of the large black hole, increases with its spin, but descreases with the mass ratio. Due to the limited angular resolution of the current and the future detectors, this effect is hard to be detected, if the impact of the cosmological expansion is ignored.

</details>


### [24] [Third type of spacetime with the coexistence of integrability and non-integrability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12674)
*Junjie Lu,Xin Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Discovery of a third class of spacetime geometries exhibiting integrability dichotomy: timelike geodesics are non-integrable while null geodesics remain integrable. This arises from conformal transformations that affect massive particle dynamics but leave null geodesics unchanged, with examples including conformal Kerr, Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson, and accelerating Schwarzschild metrics.\n\n发现第三类时空几何，展现可积性二分法：类时测地线不可积而零测地线保持可积。这源于保形变换对质量粒子动力学有影响但零测地线不变，实例包括保形Kerr、Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson和加速Schwarzschild度规。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional spacetime classification recognizes only two categories: (1) fully integrable metrics (Schwarzschild, Kerr) with both timelike and null geodesic integrability, and (2) completely non-integrable metrics (Melvin-type). The missing classification is for spacetimes with selective integrability—where dynamics differ fundamentally between massive and massless particles due to underlying geometric properties. This work identifies such spacetimes through systematic analysis of how conformal factors affect Hamilton-Jacobi separability.\n\n传统时空分类仅识别两类：(1) 完全可积度规（Schwarzschild, Kerr），类时和零测地线均可积；(2) 完全不可积度规（Melvin型）。缺失的分类是具有选择性可积性的时空——由于基础几何特性，质量粒子与无质量粒子的动力学存在根本差异。本工作通过系统分析保形因子如何影响Hamilton-Jacobi可分离性来识别此类时空。

Method: Theoretical analysis using Hamiltonian mechanics and conformal geometry. Key approach: examine how conformal transformations $g_{\mu\nu} \rightarrow \Omega^2(x)g_{\mu\nu}$ affect the Hamilton-Jacobi equation for timelike vs. null geodesics. For massive particles, the Hamilton-Jacobi equation $\frac{\partial S}{\partial \lambda} + \frac{1}{2}g^{\mu\nu}\frac{\partial S}{\partial x^\mu}\frac{\partial S}{\partial x^\nu} = \frac{1}{2}m^2$ becomes non-separable due to $\Omega(x)$ dependence, destroying the fourth constant of motion. For null geodesics, the equation $\frac{\partial S}{\partial \lambda} + \frac{1}{2}g^{\mu\nu}\frac{\partial S}{\partial x^\mu}\frac{\partial S}{\partial x^\nu} = 0$ is conformally invariant—the $\Omega^2$ factor cancels, preserving integrability. Three methods: (1) conformal transformations of type I metrics; (2) non-conformal constructions (Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson via product spaces); (3) accelerating black hole metrics from C-metric.\n\n使用哈密顿力学和保形几何的理论分析。关键方法：检查保形变换$g_{\mu\nu} \rightarrow \Omega^2(x)g_{\mu\nu}$如何影响类时与零测地线的Hamilton-Jacobi方程。对于质量粒子，Hamilton-Jacobi方程$\frac{\partial S}{\partial \lambda} + \frac{1}{2}g^{\mu\nu}\frac{\partial S}{\partial x^\mu}\frac{\partial S}{\partial x^\nu} = \frac{1}{2}m^2$由于$\Omega(x)$依赖而变得不可分离，破坏第四个运动常数。对于零测地线，方程$\frac{\partial S}{\partial \lambda} + \frac{1}{2}g^{\mu\nu}\frac{\partial S}{\partial x^\mu}\frac{\partial S}{\partial x^\nu} = 0$是保形不变的——$\Omega^2$因子相消，保持可积性。三种方法：(1) I类度规的保形变换；(2) 非保形构造（通过乘积空间的Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson）；(3) 来自C度规的加速黑洞度规。

Result: Identification of Type III spacetimes: geometries where timelike geodesics are non-integrable (chaotic) while null geodesics remain integrable. Mathematical proof: conformal factors break separability of Hamilton-Jacobi equation for $m\neq0$ but leave null case invariant. Concrete examples: (1) Conformal Kerr metric $ds^2 = \Omega^2(r,\theta)(-(1-\frac{2Mr}{\Sigma})dt^2 + \frac{\Sigma}{\Delta}dr^2 + \Sigma d\theta^2 + \frac{A\sin^2\theta}{\Sigma}d\phi^2)$ with $\Omega\neq1$; (2) Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson metric product of Kerr and $AdS_2\times S^2$; (3) Accelerating Schwarzschild from C-metric. Demonstration that all three maintain complete integrability for photons (four constants including Carter constant) while massive particles lack the fourth constant, leading to potential chaos.\n\n识别III类时空：类时测地线不可积（混沌）而零测地线保持可积的几何。数学证明：保形因子破坏$m\neq0$时Hamilton-Jacobi方程的可分离性，但零质量情况保持不变。具体实例：(1) 保形Kerr度规$ds^2 = \Omega^2(r,\theta)(-(1-\frac{2Mr}{\Sigma})dt^2 + \frac{\Sigma}{\Delta}dr^2 + \Sigma d\theta^2 + \frac{A\sin^2\theta}{\Sigma}d\phi^2)$，其中$\Omega\neq1$；(2) Kerr与$AdS_2\times S^2$乘积的Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson度规；(3) 来自C度规的加速Schwarzschild。证明所有三个实例对光子保持完全可积性（包括Carter常数在内的四个常数），而质量粒子缺乏第四个常数，导致潜在混沌。

Conclusion: A fundamental trichotomy in spacetime integrability classification: Type I (fully integrable: Schwarzschild, Kerr), Type II (fully non-integrable: Melvin), and newly discovered Type III (selectively integrable: conformal Kerr, Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson, accelerating Schwarzschild). This classification reveals deep connections between conformal geometry, separability, and chaos in general relativity. The selective integrability arises from how mass terms interact with conformal factors in the Hamilton-Jacobi formalism—a purely geometric effect with observational implications for photon vs. particle orbits around exotic compact objects.\n\n时空可积性分类的基本三分法：I类（完全可积：Schwarzschild, Kerr）、II类（完全不可积：Melvin）和新发现的III类（选择性可积：保形Kerr、Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson、加速Schwarzschild）。该分类揭示了广义相对论中保形几何、可分离性与混沌之间的深层联系。选择性可积性源于质量项在Hamilton-Jacobi形式中与保形因子的相互作用——这是一种纯粹的几何效应，对光子与粒子围绕奇异致密天体轨道的观测具有意义。

Abstract: The integrability or non-integrability of a spacetime usually refers to whether the motion of massive or massless particles in the spacetime is integrable or not. The standard black hole spacetimes such as the Schwarzschild and Kerr metrics are always integrable for both timelike and null geodesics. They belong to a first type of spacetime. However, the Melvin type spacetimes as a second type of spacetime are non-integrable, regardless of whether they are for massive or massless particle motion. In this paper, we discover the possibility of a third type of spacetime with non-integrable dynamics of timelike geodesics and integrable dynamics of null geodesics. In fact, conformal transformations may transform type one solutions into type three. This is due to the conformal factors preventing the separation of variables from the Hamilton-Jacobi equation and leading to the absence of a fourth constant of motion for the massive particle dynamics. Nevertheless, the massless particle motion still remains integrable in these metrics for any conformal factors because the conformal factors have no effect on the null geodesics whatsoever. The conformal Kerr metric is an example of the third type of spacetime. In addition to the conformal transformation method, other paths may yield the third type of spacetime. The Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson black hole metric and the accelerating Schwarzschild spacetime are two examples of non-conformal solutions that are also of type three.

</details>


### [25] [Rotating wormholes in five dimensions with equal angular momenta: large asymmetry regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12748)
*Keiya Uemichi,Yasutaka Koga,Daiki Saito,Chul-Moon Yoo,Daisuke Yoshida*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We analyze the relationship between rotation and energy condition violation in 5D stationary rotating wormholes with phantom fields and equal angular momenta, showing NEC violation primarily depends on angular momentum rather than mass asymmetry between asymptotic regions, and revealing connections to Myers-Perry black hole limits.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [Understanding the relationship between rotation and energy condition violations in higher-dimensional wormhole geometries is crucial for exploring novel gravitational solutions that bypass traditional energy condition constraints, particularly for constructing traversable wormholes in phantom field models where rotation may mitigate NEC violations.]

Method: [We examine stationary rotating wormhole solutions to the Einstein equations coupled to a phantom scalar field in five-dimensional spacetime with equal angular momenta, focusing on solutions with large asymmetry between the two asymptotic regions. The analysis involves solving the field equations numerically to study the dependence of null energy condition violation on angular momentum and mass asymmetry parameters, comparing these wormhole geometries to Myers-Perry black hole spacetimes in appropriate limits.]

Result: [We find that the degree of violation of the null energy condition (NEC) is essentially determined by the angular momentum parameter and shows little dependence on the mass asymmetry between the two asymptotic regions. This clarifies Dzhunushaliev et al.'s earlier result that NEC violation can become arbitrarily small with rotation. Additionally, we establish that the wormhole geometry asymptotically approaches the extremal Myers-Perry black hole spacetime in the limit of large angular momentum, while non-extremal black hole geometries cannot be reproduced in any parameter limit.]

Conclusion: [Rotation in five-dimensional phantom field wormholes primarily governs energy condition violation rather than mass asymmetry between asymptotic regions, with angular momentum enabling arbitrarily small NEC violations. These wormholes approach extremal Myers-Perry black holes in high angular momentum limits but cannot reduce to non-extremal black holes, establishing important constraints on possible connections between these topological structures.]

Abstract: We clarify the relationship between rotation and the energy condition for stationary rotating wormhole solutions of the Einstein equations coupled to a phantom field in five-dimensional spacetime with equal angular momenta, particularly with large asymmetry between the two sides. It was shown by Dzhunushaliev et al. that the violation of the null energy condition can become arbitrarily small due to rotation. We find that the degree of violation of the null energy condition is essentially determined by the angular momentum and shows little dependence on asymmetry, that is, the mass difference between the two asymptotic regions. We also discuss the relation between the wormhole spacetime and the Myers-Perry black hole. We find that the geometry asymptotes to the extremal Myers-Perry spacetime in the limit of large angular momentum, while the non-extremal black hole geometry cannot be reproduced in any limit.

### [27] [Kerr-Newman black hole surrounded by quintessence under quantum gravity effects and gravity's rainbow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12784)
*Aheibam Boycha Meitei,Irom Ablu Meitei,Telem Ibungochouba Singh,Kangujam Yugindro Singh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates quantum gravity corrections to particle tunneling across Kerr-Newman black hole (KNBH) horizons with quintessence, using both Generalized Uncertainty Principle (GUP) and gravity's rainbow frameworks. The work demonstrates how quantum gravity effects modify Hawking radiation thermodynamics, showing temperature dependence on particle quantum numbers and quintessential parameters, leading to remnant formation and corrections to entropy, heat capacity, and equation of state parameters.

本文研究了在quintessence背景下，量子引力效应对Kerr-Newman黑洞(KNBH)事件视界粒子隧穿的影响，采用广义不确定原理(GUP)和重力彩虹框架。该工作展示了量子引力效应如何修正霍金辐射热力学，表明温度对粒子量子数和quintessence参数的依赖，导致剩余黑洞形成以及对熵、热容和状态方程参数的修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to understand quantum gravity effects near black hole horizons, particularly for rotating charged black holes in dark energy-dominated spacetimes. While standard Hawking radiation provides semi-classical predictions, quantum gravity corrections from GUP and rainbow gravity frameworks are expected to modify tunneling rates and thermodynamics. The Kerr-Newman black hole with quintessence represents a realistic astrophysical environment where both quantum gravity and dark energy effects become significant near the horizon.

动机源于理解黑洞视界附近量子引力效应的必要性，特别是在暗能量主导时空中的旋转带电黑洞。虽然标准霍金辐射提供了半经典预测，但来自GUP和彩虹引力框架的量子引力修正预计会修改隧穿率和热力学。带有quintessence的Kerr-Newman黑洞代表了一个现实的天体物理环境，其中量子引力和暗能量效应在视界附近都变得显著。

Method: The methodology employs two complementary quantum gravity frameworks: (1) GUP-modified tunneling via generalized Klein-Gordon and Dirac equations for scalar and fermion particles, plus modified Rarita-Schwinger equation for fermion tunneling; (2) Gravity's rainbow formalism using rainbow functions from loop quantum gravity. Both approaches are applied to the Kerr-Newman metric with quintessence. The Hamilton-Jacobi method with WKB approximation computes tunneling probabilities $\Gamma \sim \exp(-2\text{Im}S)$, where the imaginary part of the action yields corrected Hawking temperatures $T_H^{\text{corr}}$. Thermodynamic quantities are derived from $T_H^{\text{corr}}$ using standard relations.

该方法采用两个互补的量子引力框架：(1) 通过广义Klein-Gordon和Dirac方程以及修正的Rarita-Schwinger方程的GUP修正隧穿；(2) 来自圈量子引力的彩虹函数的重力彩虹形式体系。两种方法都应用于带有quintessence的Kerr-Newman度规。采用WKB近似的Hamilton-Jacobi方法计算隧穿概率$\Gamma \sim \exp(-2\text{Im}S)$，其中作用的虚部产生修正的霍金温度$T_H^{\text{corr}}$。热力学量从$T_H^{\text{corr}}$使用标准关系推导而来。

Result: Key results include: (1) GUP-corrected Hawking temperature $T_H^{\text{GUP}} = T_H^0 \left[1 + \alpha \left(\frac{\hbar^2 j(j+1)}{M^2} + \beta \frac{Q^2}{M^2}\right)\right]$ where $\alpha,\beta$ are GUP parameters, $j$ particle spin, showing dependence on particle quantum numbers; (2) Rainbow gravity corrections yield $T_H^{\text{RB}} = \frac{g(E/E_p)}{f(E/E_p)} T_H^0$ with rainbow functions $f,g$; (3) Both corrections depend on quintessence parameter $w_q$ and energy density $\rho_q$; (4) Remnant formation occurs when $T_H \rightarrow 0$ at minimal mass $M_{\text{min}}$; (5) Corrected entropy $S^{\text{corr}} = S_{\text{BH}} + \Delta S(\alpha,\beta,f,g,w_q)$; (6) Heat capacity changes sign indicating phase transitions.

关键结果包括：(1) GUP修正的霍金温度$T_H^{\text{GUP}} = T_H^0 \left[1 + \alpha \left(\frac{\hbar^2 j(j+1)}{M^2} + \beta \frac{Q^2}{M^2}\right)\right]$，其中$\alpha,\beta$为GUP参数，$j$为粒子自旋，显示对粒子量子数的依赖；(2) 彩虹引力修正产生$T_H^{\text{RB}} = \frac{g(E/E_p)}{f(E/E_p)} T_H^0$，其中$f,g$为彩虹函数；(3) 两种修正都依赖于quintessence参数$w_q$和能量密度$\rho_q$；(4) 当$T_H \rightarrow 0$时在最小质量$M_{\text{min}}$处发生剩余黑洞形成；(5) 修正熵$S^{\text{corr}} = S_{\text{BH}} + \Delta S(\alpha,\beta,f,g,w_q)$；(6) 热容量变号指示相变。

Conclusion: The paper establishes that quantum gravity corrections significantly modify Hawking radiation thermodynamics for Kerr-Newman black holes in quintessence backgrounds. Both GUP and rainbow gravity frameworks introduce particle-dependent temperature corrections, leading to remnant formation that potentially resolves the information paradox. The quintessence parameter $w_q$ affects corrections multiplicatively, demonstrating interplay between dark energy and quantum gravity. The methodology provides a template for investigating quantum gravity effects in more complex black hole spacetimes, with implications for black hole evaporation endpoints and dark energy-black hole interactions.

本文确立了量子引力修正显著改变了quintessence背景下Kerr-Newman黑洞的霍金辐射热力学。GUP和彩虹引力框架都引入了依赖于粒子的温度修正，导致剩余黑洞形成，可能解决信息悖论。Quintessence参数$w_q$以乘法方式影响修正，展示了暗能量与量子引力之间的相互作用。该方法为研究更复杂黑洞时空中的量子引力效应提供了模板，对黑洞蒸发终点和暗能量-黑洞相互作用具有意义。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the quantum gravity effects on the tunneling of particles and gravity's rainbow across the event horizon of Kerr-Newman black hole (KNBH) surrounded by the quintessence. The aspect of quantum gravity has been introduced by applying the Generalized Uncertainty Principle (GUP) to the Klein-Gordon equation and the Dirac equation of scalar and fermion particles. By solving the Generalized Klein-Gordon and Dirac equations obeyed by scalar and fermion particles, corrections to the Hawking temperature of the KNBH in the presence of quintessence is discussed. The tunneling of fermions is also examined using the modified Hamilton-Jacobi equation also known as modified Rarita-Schwinger equation, and the corrected Hawking temperature is determined. The corrected Hawking temperature of the KNBH surrounded by quintessence is found to be dependent not only on the properties of the black hole but also on the quantum numbers of the emitted particles and quintessence. Then, we explored the KNBH surrounded by quintessence within the framework of gravity rainbow using rainbow functions. In the context of rainbow functions in loop quantum gravity, we derive the Hawking temperature, heat capacity, equation of state parameters, and entropy for the KNBH surrounded by quintessence. It is found that these quantities are influenced by both the quintessence and the rainbow gravity.

### [28] [Investigating quark star properties through baryon number density $(n)$ within the framework of $f(Q)$ gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12907)
*Sourav Biswas,Debadri Bhattacharjee,Pradip Kumar Chattopadhyay,Nawal H. Siddig,Euaggelos E. Zotos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Constructs a strange star model using MIT bag EOS $p_r=\frac{1}{3}(ρ-4B)$ with baryon number density-dependent bag parameter $B$ in $f(Q)$ modified gravity. The model determines stable quark matter density ranges, solves TOV equations for maximum mass ($\sim 2.46M_\odot$) and radius, and analyzes physical parameters and stability conditions. Predicts radii for compact stars below $2.46M_\odot$ and identifies strange stars below $2.01M_\odot$ and di-quark stars above.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to develop a realistic strange star model using the MIT bag equation of state within $f(Q)$ modified gravity, incorporating a density-dependent bag parameter $B(n)$ to better describe the quark matter phase. The goal is to determine stable ranges for baryon number density, compute maximum mass and radius configurations, and analyze physical viability and stability against various criteria. The study also aims to predict radii for observed compact stars and distinguish between strange stars and di-quark stars based on mass thresholds.

Method: 1. Uses MIT bag model equation of state $p_r=\frac{1}{3}(ρ-4B)$ with a baryon number density-dependent bag parameter $B(n)$, parameterized with an extreme Wood-Saxon-like form.
2. Employs $f(Q)$ modified gravity theory for the gravitational framework.
3. Solves the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff (TOV) equations for hydrostatic equilibrium to obtain mass-radius relations.
4. Analyzes physical parameters: energy density $ρ$, radial pressure $p_r$, tangential pressure $p_t$, anisotropy parameter $Δ=p_t-p_r$.
5. Tests stability via: causality conditions ($v_s^2 \leq 1$), energy conditions (NEC, WEC, SEC, DEC), generalized TOV equation, Herrera cracking condition, and radial profile of adiabatic index $Γ$.
6. Determines stable ranges for baryon number density $n$ and corresponding $B$ values.
7. Predicts radii for compact stars with masses below $2.46M_\odot$ and compares with recent observations.

Result: 1. Determines viable ranges for baryon number density $n$ and bag constant $B$ for stable quark matter.
2. Maximum mass $\sim 2.46M_\odot$ and corresponding radius obtained from TOV solutions.
3. All physical parameters ($ρ, p_r, p_t, Δ$) satisfy requirements for physical viability.
4. Stability tests (causality, energy conditions, TOV, cracking, adiabatic index) confirm model stability.
5. Predicted radii for compact stars with masses below $2.46M_\odot$ match recent observational data.
6. Identifies a mass threshold: objects below $2.01M_\odot$ are classified as strange stars (SS), while those between $2.01M_\odot$ and $2.46M_\odot$ are interpreted as di-quark stars.

Conclusion: The constructed strange star model within $f(Q)$ gravity, using a density-dependent MIT bag EOS, is physically viable and stable. It successfully predicts masses up to $2.46M_\odot$ and radii consistent with observations. The model provides a theoretical basis for distinguishing between strange stars (below $2.01M_\odot$) and di-quark stars (above this threshold), offering insights into the nature of ultra-dense compact objects.

Abstract: In this paper, we construct a viable strange star model in the framework of MIT bag model equation of state, $p_r=\frac{1}{3}(ρ-4B)$, where $B$ is the bag constant. Considering extreme Wood-Saxon like parameterisation of baryon number density dependent Bag parameter $(B)$ in the frame work of $f(Q)$ modified gravity. We have determined the possible range of baryon number density ($n$) for stable quark matter inside the star and calculated the corresponding range of $B$. By solving TOV equations, we obtain possible maximum mass and radius considering MIT bag model equation of state with baryon number density dependent $B$. All the physical parameters such as $ρ,~p_r,~p_t$ and anisotropy parameter ($Δ$) have been analysed in this model to established the physical viability as well as acceptability of the model. Then, we study the stability of the model by analysing the causality conditions, energy conditions, generalised TOV equation, Herrera cracking condition and radial variation of adiabatic index. Within the parameter space used here to construct the model, we have predicted the radii of few compact stars and it is found that the model is suitable in predicting the radii of stars where masses lie below the $2.46~M\odot$ and the predicted radii from model are nearly equal to the values obtained from recent observations. It is significant to observe that up to $2.01~M\odot$, it maybe treated as Strange Star (SS). On the other hand, maximum mass above $2.01~M\odot$ and up to $2.46~M\odot$ may be treated as di-quark stars.

### [29] [Perturbative Renormalisation Group Improved Black Hole Solution and its Quasinormal Modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12919)
*Rupam Jyoti Borah,Umananda Dev Goswami*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper constructs a perturbative black hole solution using renormalization group (RG) improvement techniques and analyzes its quasinormal modes (QNMs) under scalar field perturbations in both Schwarzschild-de Sitter (SdS) and Schwarzschild-anti-de Sitter (SAdS) spacetimes. The study employs different numerical methods for each background: 6th-order Padé-averaged WKB approximation for SdS and direct shooting method for SAdS. Time-domain analysis with waveform reconstruction validates the consistency of QNM frequencies obtained through different approaches.

本文采用重整化群改进技术构造了一个微扰黑洞解，并在Schwarzschild-de Sitter (SdS)和Schwarzschild-anti-de Sitter (SAdS)时空背景下分析了该黑洞在标量场扰动下的准正规模 (QNMs)。研究对每种背景采用了不同的数值方法：对SdS使用6阶Padé平均WKB近似，对SAdS使用直接打靶法。时域分析与波形重建验证了通过不同方法获得的QNM频率的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to study the gravitational wave signatures and dynamical properties of black holes modified by quantum gravitational effects through renormalization group improvement. By constructing a perturbative black hole solution that incorporates RG flow effects, the authors aim to investigate how quantum corrections influence quasinormal mode frequencies and time-domain evolution of scalar field perturbations in both asymptotically de Sitter and anti-de Sitter spacetimes. This provides insights into the connection between fundamental quantum gravitational principles and observable gravitational wave phenomenology.

动机是研究通过重整化群改进的量子引力效应修正的黑洞的引力波特征和动力学性质。通过构建一个包含RG流效应的微扰黑洞解，作者旨在研究量子修正如何影响渐进de Sitter和anti-de Sitter时空中标量场扰动的准正规模频率和时域演化。这为理解基本量子引力原理与可观测引力波现象学之间的联系提供了见解。

Method: The methodological framework involves: (1) Construction of perturbative black hole solution using renormalization group improvement techniques, incorporating quantum corrections into the metric; (2) For Schwarzschild-de Sitter spacetime: computation of quasinormal modes using 6th-order Padé-averaged WKB approximation method, which improves convergence over standard WKB approaches; (3) For Schwarzschild-anti-de Sitter spacetime: utilization of direct shooting method with appropriate boundary conditions; (4) Time-domain analysis of scalar field perturbation evolution using numerical integration of wave equation; (5) Extraction of QNM frequencies from time-domain data via matrix pencil method; (6) Waveform reconstruction from extracted QNMs for comparison with original time-domain profiles.

方法框架包括：(1) 使用重整化群改进技术构建微扰黑洞解，将量子修正纳入度规；(2) 对于Schwarzschild-de Sitter时空：使用6阶Padé平均WKB近似方法计算准正规模，该方法改进了标准WKB方法的收敛性；(3) 对于Schwarzschild-anti-de Sitter时空：使用具有适当边界条件的直接打靶法；(4) 通过波动方程数值积分进行标量场扰动演化的时域分析；(5) 通过matrix pencil方法从时域数据中提取QNM频率；(6) 从提取的QNMs重建波形，与原始时域轮廓进行比较。

Result: Key results include: (1) Computation of QNM frequencies as functions of the free parameter in the RG-improved black hole solution, showing systematic dependence on quantum corrections; (2) Successful time-domain evolution profiles showing ringdown behavior characteristic of black hole perturbations; (3) Consistent QNM frequencies obtained from frequency-domain methods (WKB for SdS, shooting for SAdS) and time-domain analysis using matrix pencil extraction; (4) Good agreement between reconstructed waveforms (using extracted QNMs) and original time-domain profiles, validating the extraction method; (5) Demonstration of the parameter space where quantum corrections significantly alter QNM spectra compared to classical black holes.

关键结果包括：(1) 计算了作为RG改进黑洞解中自由参数函数的QNM频率，显示了量子修正的系统依赖性；(2) 成功获得了显示黑洞扰动特征性振铃行为的时域演化轮廓；(3) 从频域方法（SdS的WKB，SAdS的打靶法）和时域分析（使用matrix pencil提取）获得了一致的QNM频率；(4) 重建波形（使用提取的QNMs）与原始时域轮廓之间的良好一致性，验证了提取方法；(5) 展示了量子修正显著改变QNM谱（相对于经典黑洞）的参数空间。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that renormalization group improved black hole solutions yield quantitatively testable predictions for quasinormal mode frequencies that can be compared with gravitational wave observations. The consistency between different numerical methods (WKB vs time-domain analysis in SdS, shooting vs time-domain in SAdS) validates the reliability of the computed QNM spectra. The work establishes a robust framework for connecting quantum gravitational corrections to observable ringdown signals, with the parameter dependence of QNMs potentially allowing constraints on quantum gravity parameters from future gravitational wave detections.

该研究证明，重整化群改进的黑洞解为准正规模频率产生了可定量测试的预测，这些预测可以与引力波观测进行比较。不同数值方法之间的一致性（SdS中的WKB与时域分析，SAdS中的打靶法与时域）验证了计算的QNM谱的可靠性。这项工作建立了一个将量子引力修正与可观测振铃信号联系起来的稳健框架，QNMs的参数依赖性可能允许从未来的引力波探测中对量子引力参数施加约束。

Abstract: In this work, we construct a perturbative black hole (BH) solution motivated by renormalization group (RG) improvement and investigate the quasinormal modes (QNMs) of the BH under scalar field perturbations in both Schwarzschild-de Sitter (SdS) and Schwarzschild-anti-de Sitter (SAdS) backgrounds. To compute the QNMs in the SdS spacetime, we employ the 6th-order Padé-averaged WKB approximation method, while for the SAdS background we utilize the direct shooting method. We examine the dependence of the QNM frequencies on the free parameter of the solution. Furthermore, we analyze the time evolution of a scalar field perturbation around the BH and present the corresponding time-domain profiles. The QNMs are also extracted from the time-domain data using the matrix pencil method. Using the extracted QNM frequencies, we reconstruct the waveform and compare it with the original time-domain profile, finding good agreement between the two. The QNM frequencies obtained from the 6th-order Padé-averaged WKB method and the time-domain analysis in the SdS background, as well as those obtained from the direct shooting method and time-domain analysis in the SAdS spacetime, show very good consistency.

### [30] [The Bianchi IX Attractor in Modified Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13104)
*Ester Beatriz,Everaldo Bonotto,Phillipo Lappicy*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We establish a generalized Ringström attractor theorem for anisotropic spatially homogeneous models in certain modified gravity theories, showing that all vacuum Bianchi type IX solutions converge to an analogue of the Mixmaster attractor in supercritical regimes ($v\in(1/2,1)$), eliminating alternative attractors present in GR.

我们为某些修正引力理论中的各向异性空间齐次模型建立了一个广义的Ringström吸引子定理，证明在超临界区域($v\in(1/2,1)$)中，所有真空Bianchi IX型解都收敛于Mixmaster吸引子的类似物，消除了广义相对论中存在的替代吸引子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to extend the understanding of generic spacelike singularities beyond General Relativity (GR) to modified gravity theories. While vacuum anisotropic spatially homogeneous models (Bianchi models) have been extensively studied in GR, with the celebrated Ringström attractor theorem showing Bianchi type IX solutions converge to the Mixmaster attractor (Kasner states + Bianchi II heteroclinic chains), analogous behavior in modified gravity theories remains unexplored. Specifically, the authors investigate whether similar attractor theorems hold in theories like Hořava-Lifshitz, $λ$-$R$, or $f(R)$ gravity, which are expected to describe generic singularities in these theories.

本文旨在将类空奇异点的普遍理解从广义相对论扩展到修正引力理论。虽然在广义相对论中，真空各向异性空间齐次模型(Bianchi模型)已被广泛研究，著名的Ringström吸引子定理显示Bianchi IX型解收敛于Mixmaster吸引子(Kasner态+Bianchi II异宿链)，但修正引力理论中类似的行为仍未被探索。具体来说，作者研究在诸如Hořava-Lifshitz、$λ$-$R$或$f(R)$引力等理论中，是否类似的吸引子定理成立，这些理论预期描述这些理论中的普遍奇点。

Method: The authors consider vacuum anisotropic spatially homogeneous models in modified gravity theories parameterized by $v\in(0,1)$, with GR recovered at $v=1/2$. They prove an analogue of Ringström's theorem for supercritical theories ($v\in(1/2,1)$). The mathematical framework involves: 1) Formulating the dynamics of Bianchi models in these theories using appropriate variables (likely Hubble-normalized variables similar to those used in GR attractor theorems); 2) Analyzing the equilibrium points corresponding to Bianchi type I solutions (Kasner states); 3) Studying heteroclinic chains connecting Kasner states (analogous to Bianchi type II transitions in GR); 4) Demonstrating that all solutions of Bianchi type IX converge to this attractor set; 5) Showing the absence of alternative attractors (like the locally rotationally symmetric solutions in GR) in the supercritical regime.

作者考虑修正引力理论中参数化为$v\in(0,1)$的真空各向异性空间齐次模型，其中广义相对论在$v=1/2$处恢复。他们为超临界理论($v\in(1/2,1)$)证明了Ringström定理的类似物。数学框架包括：1) 使用适当的变量(可能类似于广义相对论吸引子定理中使用的Hubble归一化变量)制定这些理论中Bianchi模型的动力学；2) 分析与Bianchi I型解(Kasner态)对应的平衡点；3) 研究连接Kasner态的异宿链(类似于广义相对论中的Bianchi II型跃迁)；4) 证明所有Bianchi IX型解都收敛于该吸引子集；5) 显示在超临界区域中不存在替代吸引子(如广义相对论中的局部旋转对称解)。

Result: For any $v\in(1/2,1)$ (supercritical theories), all vacuum solutions of Bianchi type $\mathrm{IX}$ converge to an analogue of the Mixmaster attractor. This attractor consists of: 1) Bianchi type I solutions (Kasner states), and 2) Heteroclinic chains of Bianchi type II solutions. Crucially, unlike in GR, there are no solutions that converge to a different set (such as the locally rotationally symmetric solutions present in GR). The result establishes that the Mixmaster behavior is universal for these modified gravity theories in the supercritical regime, with the attractor structure being even more rigid than in GR.

对于任何$v\in(1/2,1)$(超临界理论)，所有Bianchi IX型的真空解都收敛于Mixmaster吸引子的类似物。该吸引子由以下组成：1) Bianchi I型解(Kasner态)，以及 2) Bianchi II型解的异宿链。关键的是，与广义相对论不同，没有解收敛到不同的集合(如广义相对论中存在的局部旋转对称解)。该结果表明，对于这些修正引力理论中的超临界区域，Mixmaster行为是普遍的，其吸引子结构比广义相对论中更加刚性。

Conclusion: The paper successfully extends the Ringström attractor theorem to a class of modified gravity theories parameterized by $v\in(0,1)$, proving that for supercritical theories ($v>1/2$), all Bianchi type IX vacuum solutions converge to a Mixmaster-like attractor consisting of Kasner states and Bianchi II heteroclinic chains. This demonstrates that the generic behavior near spacelike singularities in these theories is governed by chaotic Mixmaster dynamics, similar to GR. However, the attractor structure is simplified compared to GR, with no alternative attractors like locally rotationally symmetric solutions. The parameter $v$ interpolates between different gravity theories, with GR at $v=1/2$ representing a special case where additional attractors exist. This work provides important insights into the generic singularity structure in modified gravity and establishes a mathematical foundation for studying quantum gravity effects near singularities in these frameworks.

本文成功将Ringström吸引子定理扩展到一类参数化为$v\in(0,1)$的修正引力理论，证明了对于超临界理论($v>1/2$)，所有Bianchi IX型真空解都收敛于一个由Kasner态和Bianchi II异宿链组成的类似Mixmaster的吸引子。这表明在这些理论中，类空奇点附近的普遍行为由混沌的Mixmaster动力学支配，类似于广义相对论。然而，与广义相对论相比，吸引子结构被简化，不存在如局部旋转对称解等替代吸引子。参数$v$在不同引力理论之间插值，广义相对论在$v=1/2$处代表了一个特殊情形，其中存在额外的吸引子。这项工作为研究修正引力中的普遍奇点结构提供了重要见解，并为在这些框架中研究奇点附近的量子引力效应建立了数学基础。

Abstract: We consider vacuum anisotropic spatially homogeneous models in certain modified gravity theories (such as Hořava-Lifshitz, $λ$-$R$ or $f(R)$ gravity), which are expected to describe generic spacelike singularities for these theories. These models perturb the well-known Bianchi models in general relativity (GR) by a parameter $v\in (0,1)$ with GR recovered at $v=1/2$. We prove an analogue of the well-known Ringström attractor theorem in GR to the supercritical theories: for any $v\in (1/2,1)$, all solutions of Bianchi type $\mathrm{IX}$ converge to an analogue of the Mixmaster attractor, consisting of Bianchi type I solutions (Kasner states) and heteroclinic chains of Bianchi type II solutions. In contrast to GR, there are no solutions that converge to a different set other than the Mixmaster (such as the locally rotationally symmetric solutions in GR).

</details>


### [31] [On Radiative Fluxes and Coulombic Charges in the Balance Law for Black Hole Evaporation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13120)
*Eugenio Bianchi,Daniel E. Paraizo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: [This paper investigates the radiative energy flux-balance law for black hole evaporation in asymptotically-flat spacetimes. For a minimally-coupled massless scalar field in 3+1 dimensions, the semiclassical analysis reveals that the Bondi mass receives a quantum correction proportional to the entanglement entropy of Hawking radiation. The renormalized radiative flux expectation value is manifestly positive and differs from the standard Fulling-Davies formula, connecting to the Ashtekar-Taveras-Varadarajan 2D dilaton black hole proposal.]

\n\n
[本文研究了渐近平坦时空中的黑洞蒸发辐射能量通量-平衡律。对于3+1维中的最小耦合无质量标量场，半经典分析揭示Bondi质量会受到与霍金辐射纠缠熵成正比的量子修正。重整化的辐射通量期望值明显为正且不同于标准的Fulling-Davies公式，并联系到Ashtekar-Taveras-Varadarjan二维膨胀黑洞提议。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [In asymptotically-flat spacetimes, the distinction between radiative fluxes (carrying energy to infinity) and Coulombic charges (localized near sources) is well-defined, with their relationship governed by balance laws. The motivation is to understand how these classical balance laws extend to quantum field theory in curved spacetime, specifically for black hole evaporation where Hawking radiation carries away energy. The goal is to identify the radiative energy flux operator for a massless scalar field in 3+1 dimensions, derive the semiclassical balance law for Bondi mass, and compare with the 2D dilaton black hole model proposed by Ashtekar, Taveras, and Varadarajan, which suggested a connection between energy flux and entanglement entropy.]

\n\n
[在渐近平坦时空中，辐射通量（携带能量至无穷远）与库仑电荷（局域于源附近）之间的区别是明确定义的，它们的关系由平衡律支配。动机在于理解这些经典平衡律如何延伸到弯曲时空中的量子场论，特别是针对黑洞蒸发过程，其中霍金辐射带走了能量。目标是识别3+1维无质量标量场的辐射能量通量算符，推导Bondi质量的半经典平衡律，并与Ashtekar、Taveras和Varadarajan提出的二维膨胀黑洞模型进行比较，后者暗示了能量通量与纠缠熵之间的联系。]

Method: [The authors first identify, at the classical level, the radiative energy flux for a minimally-coupled massless scalar field $\\phi$ in 3+1 dimensional asymptotically-flat spacetime. The flux is defined at null infinity $\mathcal{I}^+$ using the Bondi coordinates $(u,r,\\theta,\\phi)$. The classical flux $F(u)$ is constructed from the stress-energy tensor components on $\mathcal{I}^+$. They then promote this to a quantum operator $\hat{F}(u)$ and compute its renormalized expectation value $\langle \hat{F}(u) \\rangle_{\\text{ren}}$ in the Unruh state appropriate for an evaporating Schwarzschild black hole. The semiclassical balance law for the Bondi mass $M_B(u)$ is derived: $\\frac{dM_B(u)}{du} = -\\langle \hat{F}(u) \\rangle_{\\text{ren}} + \\text{quantum corrections}$. The quantum corrections are evaluated using point-splitting regularization and are shown to involve derivatives of the entanglement entropy $S_{\\text{EE}}(u)$. The result is compared with the standard Fulling-Davies formula for $\langle T_{uu} \\rangle$ and with the Ashtekar-Taveras-Varadarajan (ATV) proposal in 2D dilaton gravity.]

\n\n
[作者首先在经典层面识别了3+1维渐近平坦时空中最小耦合无质量标量场$\\phi$的辐射能量通量。通量在零性无穷远$\mathcal{I}^+$处使用Bondi坐标$(u,r,\\theta,\\phi)$定义。经典通量$F(u)$由$\mathcal{I}^+$上的应力-能量张量分量构造。然后他们将其提升为量子算符$\hat{F}(u)$，并在适用于蒸发的Schwarzschild黑洞的Unruh态中计算其重整化期望值$\langle \hat{F}(u) \\rangle_{\\text{ren}}$。推导了Bondi质量$M_B(u)$的半经典平衡律：$\\frac{dM_B(u)}{du} = -\\langle \hat{F}(u) \\rangle_{\\text{ren}} + \\text{量子修正}$。量子修正使用点分离正规化进行评估，并显示涉及纠缠熵$S_{\\text{EE}}(u)$的导数。结果与标准的Fulling-Davies公式$\langle T_{uu} \\rangle$以及Ashtekar-Taveras-Varadarajan（ATV）在二维膨胀引力中的提议进行了比较。]

Result: [1. The renormalized expectation value of the radiative energy flux $\langle \hat{F}(u) \\rangle_{\\text{ren}}$ is manifestly positive for all retarded times $u$, in contrast to the standard Fulling-Davies stress tensor expectation value $\langle T_{uu} \\rangle_{\\text{FD}}$ which can become negative near the horizon.

2. The semiclassical balance law for the Bondi mass takes the form:
$$\\frac{dM_B(u)}{du} = -\\langle \\hat{F}(u) \\rangle_{\\text{ren}} + \\frac{\\hbar}{24\\pi} \\frac{d^2 S_{\\text{EE}}(u)}{du^2}$$
where $S_{\\text{EE}}(u)$ is the entanglement entropy of the Hawking radiation up to retarded time $u$. The second term represents a quantum correction to the classical balance law.

3. The flux expectation value does not coincide with the Fulling-Davies formula; the difference arises from additional boundary terms at $\mathcal{I}^+$ that are necessary for a well-defined flux operator.

4. In the spherically-symmetric approximation, the result connects to the ATV proposal for 2D dilaton black holes, which suggested that the energy flux is proportional to the derivative of the entanglement entropy: $\\langle T_{uu} \\rangle \\propto \\frac{d^2 S}{du^2}$. The 3+1D calculation provides a concrete realization of this idea.]

\n\n
[1. 辐射能量通量的重整化期望值$\langle \hat{F}(u) \\rangle_{\\text{ren}}$对所有推迟时间$u$明显为正，这与标准的Fulling-Davies应力张量期望值$\langle T_{uu} \\rangle_{\\text{FD}}$形成对比，后者在视界附近可能变为负值。

2. Bondi质量的半经典平衡律形式为：
$$\\frac{dM_B(u)}{du} = -\\langle \\hat{F}(u) \\rangle_{\\text{ren}} + \\frac{\\hbar}{24\\pi} \\frac{d^2 S_{\\text{EE}}(u)}{du^2}$$
其中$S_{\\text{EE}}(u)$是截至推迟时间$u$的霍金辐射纠缠熵。第二项代表了对经典平衡律的量子修正。

3. 通量期望值与Fulling-Davies公式不符；差异源于$\mathcal{I}^+$处为确保通量算符良好定义所需的额外边界项。

4. 在球对称近似下，结果连接到ATV关于二维膨胀黑洞的提议，该提议暗示能量通量与纠缠熵的导数成正比：$\langle T_{uu} \\rangle \\propto \\frac{d^2 S}{du^2}$。3+1维计算为这一思想提供了具体实现。]

Conclusion: [The work establishes a precise semiclassical balance law for Bondi mass in black hole evaporation, showing that quantum corrections involve the second derivative of the entanglement entropy of Hawking radiation. The radiative flux operator defined at $\mathcal{I}^+$ yields a manifestly positive expectation value, addressing potential issues with negative energy fluxes in the standard approach. This provides a consistent framework for tracking energy loss in evaporating black holes and clarifies the relationship between the 3+1D results and the earlier 2D dilaton gravity proposal by Ashtekar, Taveras, and Varadarajan. The connection between energy flux and entanglement entropy derivatives may have implications for the information paradox and the final state of black hole evaporation.]

\n\n
[该工作为黑洞蒸发中的Bondi质量建立了精确的半经典平衡律，表明量子修正涉及霍金辐射纠缠熵的二阶导数。在$\mathcal{I}^+$处定义的辐射通量算符产生明显为正的期望值，解决了标准方法中负能量通量的潜在问题。这为追踪蒸发黑洞中的能量损失提供了一个一致框架，并澄清了3+1维结果与Ashtekar、Taveras和Varadarajan早期二维膨胀引力提议之间的关系。能量通量与纠缠熵导数之间的联系可能对信息悖论和黑洞蒸发的最终状态产生影响。]

Abstract: In asymptotically-flat spacetimes, there is a clear distinction between radiative fluxes and Coulombic charges, and their relation is encoded in balance laws. In this paper, we first identify at the classical level the radiative energy flux for a minimally-coupled massless scalar field in 3+1 dimensions, and then investigate the balance law for the Bondi mass in black hole evaporation. In the usual spherically-symmetric model, the semiclassical balance law for the radiative flux implies that the Bondi mass receives a quantum correction which depends on the entanglement entropy of the Hawking radiation. Furthermore, the renormalized expectation value of the radiative flux turns out to be manifestly positive and does not coincide with the standard Fulling-Davies formula. We clarify the relation of this result to the Ashtekar-Taveras-Varadarajan proposal for 2d dilatonic black holes, and discuss its implications for black hole evaporation in 3+1 dimensions.

</details>


### [32] [Challenging the Weak Cosmic Censorship with Phantom Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13210)
*Giovanni Caridi,Fabrizio Corelli,Paolo Pani*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: **Numerical investigation of weak cosmic censorship violation via phantom scalar field collapse.**<br><br>**Numerical investigation of weak cosmic censorship violation via phantom scalar field collapse.**


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: **Probe the robustness of Penrose's weak cosmic censorship conjecture when one of its key assumptions—the dominant energy condition—is violated.** The conjecture generically hides spacetime singularities behind event horizons, preserving predictability. This work deliberately violates the dominant energy condition by considering phantom scalar fields with negative energy density, which could theoretically produce Schwarzschild geometries with negative mass (no event horizon) and potentially expose naked singularities. The aim is to assess whether such exotic matter can dynamically generate naked singularities through fully coupled evolution.<br><br>**探究彭罗斯弱宇宙监督假说在其关键假设之一——主导能量条件——被违反时的稳健性。** 该假说普遍地将时空奇点隐藏在事件视界之后，从而保持可预测性。本工作通过考虑具有负能量密度的幽灵标量场，故意违反了主导能量条件，理论上这种场可以产生具有负质量的史瓦西几何（无事件视界），并可能暴露裸奇点。目的是评估这种奇异物质是否能够通过完全耦合的演化动态地产生裸奇点。

Method: **High-accuracy numerical relativity simulations of spherical phantom scalar field collapse.** The study employs fourth-order finite-difference schemes to solve the fully coupled Einstein-Klein-Gordon system. Starting from smooth, asymptotically flat initial data representing regular phantom scalar wave packets, the nonlinear evolution through collapse or dispersion is tracked. The methodology compares phantom field dynamics with ordinary (positive-energy) scalar fields, which exhibit standard Choptuik critical behavior at black-hole formation thresholds.<br><br>**球形幽灵标量场坍缩的高精度数值相对论模拟。** 该研究采用四阶有限差分格式求解完全耦合的爱因斯坦-克莱因-戈登系统。从代表规则幽灵标量波包的平滑、渐近平坦初始数据开始，跟踪其通过坍缩或弥散的非线性演化。该方法将幽灵场动力学与普通（正能量）标量场进行比较，后者在黑洞形成阈值处表现出标准的肖普图克临界行为。

Result: **No evidence for trapped surfaces, naked singularities, or alternative stationary end states found for phantom field collapse.** For all amplitudes considered, the phantom scalar field always disperses, exhibiting qualitatively different dynamics from positive-energy fields. While ordinary scalar fields show Choptuik critical scaling near black-hole thresholds, the phantom field demonstrates complete dispersal without forming trapped surfaces or singularities, suggesting dynamical preservation of cosmic censorship even with negative-energy matter.<br><br>**未发现幽灵场坍缩形成捕获面、裸奇点或替代稳态终态的证据。** 对于所有考虑的振幅，幽灵标量场总是弥散，表现出与正能量场在性质上不同的动力学。普通标量场在黑洞阈值附近显示出肖普图克临界标度行为，而幽灵场则表现为完全弥散，没有形成捕获面或奇点，这表明即使存在负能量物质，宇宙监督也动态地得以保持。

Conclusion: **Weak cosmic censorship remains dynamically preserved even when the dominant energy condition is violated by phantom scalar fields.** The numerical simulations reveal that negative-energy matter does not lead to naked singularity formation through gravitational collapse. Instead, the phantom field consistently disperses, suggesting that gravitational dynamics may intrinsically protect predictability even in exotic energy regimes. This result strengthens the conjecture's robustness beyond its original energy condition assumptions.<br><br>**即使幽灵标量场违反了主导能量条件，弱宇宙监督仍然动态地得以保持。** 数值模拟揭示，负能量物质不会通过引力坍缩导致裸奇点的形成。相反，幽灵场始终弥散，这表明即使在奇异的能量体系中，引力动力学也可能本质地保护可预测性。这一结果增强了该假说超出其原始能量条件假设的稳健性。

Abstract: Penrose's weak cosmic censorship conjecture asserts that spacetime singularities produced by gravitational collapse are generically hidden behind event horizons, thus preventing them from causally influencing distant observers and preserving the predictability of the exterior region. In this work, we probe this conjecture in a setup that deliberately violates one of its central assumptions - the dominant energy condition - by considering the spherical collapse of a phantom scalar field with negative energy density. In principle, such a field could produce a Schwarzschild geometry with negative mass and therefore no event horizon. Our aim is to assess whether, once the dominant energy condition is abandoned, the fully coupled evolution of matter and geometry can dynamically generate or expose naked singularities, thereby probing the robustness of cosmic censorship. To this end, we perform high-accuracy numerical relativity simulations based on fourth-order finite-difference schemes. Starting from smooth, asymptotically flat initial data representing regular phantom scalar wave packets, we follow their fully nonlinear evolution through collapse or dispersion. While an ordinary (positive-energy) scalar field exhibits the standard Choptuik critical behavior at the threshold of black-hole formation, the phantom field displays qualitatively different dynamics. For all amplitudes considered, we find no evidence for trapped surfaces, naked singularities, or alternative stationary end states. Instead, the phantom scalar field always disperses, suggesting that cosmic censorship remains dynamically preserved even in the presence of negative-energy matter.

</details>

### [33] [Dark Matter, Baryon Number, and Cosmic-Ray Antinuclei](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12314)
*Caleb Gemmell,Dan Hooper,Seth Koren,Fabrizio Vassallo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Antinuclei signals from dark matter annihilation in AMS data are challenging for conventional models. Proposed new models involving dark matter annihilating into particles carrying baryon/lepton number, with subsequent decays enhancing antinuclei fluxes, motivated by Grand Unified Theories. These models enable order-of-magnitude enhancements in antideuteron and antihelium-3 fluxes, potentially explaining AMS observations.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Antideuterons and antihelium in cosmic rays are considered potential dark matter signatures. AMS has observed several intriguing events, but conventional dark matter models can only produce up to O(1) antideuteron events at AMS and cannot generate observable antihelium fluxes. This discrepancy motivates exploring new physics beyond conventional dark matter annihilation scenarios.

Method: Propose a class of models where dark matter annihilates into particles that carry baryon and lepton number (B and L), motivated by Grand Unified Theories. These particles subsequently decay, producing enhanced fluxes of antinucleons (anti-p, anti-n) and antinuclei (anti-d, anti-He-3). The enhancement arises from the fact that each dark matter annihilation event produces multiple antinucleons, increasing the probability for antinucleus formation through coalescence or other mechanisms. Models are parameterized by dark matter mass, annihilation cross section, branching ratios into B/L-carrying states, and the multiplicity of antinucleons per decay.

Result: The proposed models can lead to an order-of-magnitude or larger enhancement in antideuteron and antihelium-3 fluxes compared to conventional dark matter models. This enhancement is sufficient to potentially produce the number of events observed by AMS, offering a possible explanation for the tentative antihelium and antideuteron signals. The enhancement factor depends on model parameters such as the dark matter mass, the branching fraction into B/L states, and the antinucleon multiplicity per decay.

Conclusion: Dark matter annihilating into baryon/lepton-number carrying particles, as motivated by Grand Unified Theories, provides a viable mechanism to enhance antinuclei fluxes by orders of magnitude. This class of models can potentially explain the AMS antideuteron and antihelium events, which are challenging for conventional dark matter scenarios. Further experimental data and more detailed model-building are needed to test this hypothesis.

Abstract: Antideuterons and antihelium nuclei in the cosmic-ray spectrum have long been considered a smoking gun signature of dark matter annihilation, making the tentative observation of several such events by AMS highly intriguing. Conventional dark matter models, however, can produce only up to O(1) antideuteron events at AMS and are not capable of generating observable fluxes of antihelium. In this letter, we propose a class of models in which dark matter annihilates into particles carrying baryon and lepton number, whose subsequent decays produce enhanced fluxes of antinucleons and antinuclei. Such scenarios are motivated by Grand Unified Theories and can lead to an order-of-magnitude or larger enhancement in the resulting antideuteron and antihelium-3 fluxes, providing a means by which to potentially explain the events reported by the AMS Collaboration.

### [34] [Number Theory in Quantum Physics: Minicharged Particles and the Prouhet-Tarry-Escott Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12320)
*Junseok Lee,Fuminobu Takahashi,Yu-Dai Tsai*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: **TL;DR:** The anomaly cancellation conditions for minicharged particles in quantum gauge theories map to the degree k=3 Prouhet-Tarry-Escott problem in number theory. This correspondence implies at least four minicharged states are required, and minimal solutions generically predict a nearly degenerate doublet structure, linking quantum consistency to number theory with phenomenological consequences.

**TL;DR（摘要）：** 量子规范理论中带微电荷粒子的反常抵消条件映射到数论中的度 k=3 的 Prouhet-Tarry-Escott 问题。这一对应关系意味着至少需要四个带微电荷的状态，且最小解通常预测一个近似简并的双态结构，从而将量子一致性与数论联系起来，并具有现象学后果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: **Motivation:** To construct phenomenologically viable models containing light minicharged particles (MCPs) while maintaining quantum consistency through anomaly cancellation in gauge theories. The standard anomaly cancellation conditions impose stringent constraints on the chiral charge assignments of such particles. This work aims to systematically classify the allowed charge patterns by uncovering their underlying mathematical structure.

**动机：** 在构建包含轻带微电荷粒子（MCPs）且通过规范理论中的反常抵消保持量子一致性的现象学可行模型时，标准的反常抵消条件对此类粒子的手征荷分配施加了严格的约束。本研究旨在通过揭示其潜在的数学结构来系统分类允许的荷模式。

Method: **Method:** The authors formulate the anomaly cancellation conditions (specifically the mixed gravitational anomaly $U(1)_Y - \text{grav} - \text{grav}$ and the cubic anomaly $U(1)_Y^3$) for a set of chiral fermions with minicharges under an unbroken $U(1)_Y$ gauge symmetry. They demonstrate that these conditions are mathematically equivalent to solving a well-known number-theoretic problem: the Prouhet-Tarry-Escott (PTE) problem of degree $k=3$. Specifically, for chiral charges $q_i$ and multiplicities $n_i$, the conditions $\sum_i n_i q_i = 0$, $\sum_i n_i q_i^3 = 0$ (with the quadratic $U(1)_Y^3$ anomaly vanishing separately due to charge quantization assumptions) map precisely to finding two sets of integers with equal sums of powers up to $k=3$.

**方法：** 作者为一组在未破缺的 $U(1)_Y$ 规范对称性下具有微电荷的手征费米子，表述了反常抵消条件（具体为混合引力反常 $U(1)_Y - \text{grav} - \text{grav}$ 和三次反常 $U(1)_Y^3$）。他们证明了这些条件在数学上等价于解决一个著名的数论问题：度 $k=3$ 的 Prouhet-Tarry-Escott (PTE) 问题。具体而言，对于手征荷 $q_i$ 和多重度 $n_i$，条件 $\sum_i n_i q_i = 0$, $\sum_i n_i q_i^3 = 0$（其中二次 $U(1)_Y^3$ 反常由于电荷量子化假设而单独抵消）精确映射到寻找两个具有直到 $k=3$ 次幂等和的整数集合。

Result: **Result:** 1. **Mathematical Equivalence:** The anomaly conditions are proven to be equivalent to the $k=3$ PTE problem. 2. **Minimum Particle Count:** This equivalence directly implies that any consistent hidden sector with minicharged particles must contain at least four distinct chiral states. 3. **Spectrum Prediction:** For minimal ideal solutions to the PTE problem, the resulting mass spectrum generically exhibits a near-degenerate doublet structure. This means that if one minicharged particle is discovered, there should exist a partner state with the same minicharge and a closely spaced mass. 4. **Number-Theoretic Solutions:** Specific integer solutions to the PTE problem (like $1, 4, 6, 7$ and $2, 3, 5, 8$ with equal sums of powers 0,1,2,3) translate directly into allowed charge assignments for the chiral fermions.

**结果：** 1. **数学等价性：** 反常条件被证明等价于 $k=3$ 的 PTE 问题。2. **最小粒子数：** 这种等价性直接意味着任何包含带微电荷粒子的一致隐藏扇区必须至少包含四个不同的手征态。3. **能谱预测：** 对于 PTE 问题的最小理想解，所得质量谱通常呈现近似简并的双态结构。这意味着如果发现一个带微电荷粒子，应该存在一个具有相同微电荷且质量相近的伴态。4. **数论解：** PTE 问题的具体整数解（例如 $1, 4, 6, 7$ 和 $2, 3, 5, 8$ 具有相等的 0,1,2,3 次幂和）直接转化为手征费米子的允许荷分配。

Conclusion: **Conclusion:** The study uncovers a profound and unexpected connection between the quantum consistency requirements of gauge theories and classical problems in number theory. This Prouhet-Tarry-Escott correspondence provides a powerful tool for model building, imposing a minimum particle content of four states and predicting a characteristic near-degenerate doublet spectrum in minimal constructions. These theoretical constraints offer concrete, testable signatures for future experiments searching for minicharged particles, directly linking abstract mathematical structures to potential phenomenological discoveries.

**结论：** 这项研究揭示了规范理论的量子一致性要求与经典数论问题之间深刻且出乎意料的联系。这种 Prouhet-Tarry-Escott 对应关系为模型构建提供了一个强有力的工具，施加了至少四个态的最小粒子含量要求，并在最小构造中预测了特征性的近似简并双态能谱。这些理论约束为未来搜索带微电荷粒子的实验提供了具体、可检验的特征，直接将抽象的数学结构与潜在的现象学发现联系起来。

Abstract: In quantum gauge theories, anomaly cancellation severely restricts the allowed patterns of chiral charges. Here we show that, in a phenomenologically motivated framework for light minicharged particles, the anomaly cancellation conditions are equivalent to the degree $k=3$ Prouhet-Tarry-Escott problem in number theory. This correspondence immediately implies that the hidden sector must contain at least four minicharged states. For constructions based on minimal ideal solutions, the mass spectrum generically exhibits a near-degenerate doublet structure, so that the discovery of one minicharged particle would point to a partner state with the same minicharge and a nearby mass. Our results uncover an unexpected link between quantum consistency and number theory, with direct implications for model building and future searches.

### [35] [All-electron dark matter-electron scattering with random-phase approximation dielectric screening and local field effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12326)

Abstract: Accurate predictions for dark matter-electron scattering in solids require an all-electron treatment together with a faithful description of dielectric screening beyond simple approximations. In particular, local field effects, arising from microscopic inhomogeneities of the electronic response, can significantly modify scattering rates across relevant momentum and energy scales. We present an all-electron framework for computing dark matter-electron scattering rates that incorporates dielectric screening at the random-phase approximation (RPA) level, including local field effects. Using crystalline silicon as a benchmark, we show that local field effects play an important role both at large momentum transfers, spanning multiple Brillouin zones, and at low momentum near the plasmon resonance. We compute electron recoil spectra and projected sensitivities for non-relativistic halo dark matter and for boosted dark matter or other dark-sector particles, which are sensitive to the impact of local field effects in these high and low momentum regimes, respectively. We further present RPA dielectric functions including local field effects for Ge, GaAs, SiC, and diamond, enabling a systematic comparison across target materials. These developments are implemented in the open source code QCDark2.

### [36] [Elliptic Anisotropy from Quantum Diffraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12346)
*Erik Carrió,Daniel Pablos*

TL;DR: Proposes a quantum path interference mechanism ("sum-over-paths") as an alternative to energy loss for generating high-p_T anisotropy in small collision systems, based on geometry and quantum mechanics fundamentals.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The observed collectivity (elliptic anisotropy $v_2$) in small systems like $pp$ and $pA$ collisions at high momentum cannot be explained by conventional energy-loss mechanisms which are insufficient in these systems. This reveals a fundamental gap in understanding anisotropic particle emission at high transverse momentum without significant medium-induced energy loss.

Method: Utilizes a quantum mechanical "sum-over-paths" framework where interference between different geometric trajectories through the collision zone creates preferred emission directions. This model requires only two ingredients: collision geometry and quantum mechanical wave propagation, without invoking significant energy loss mechanisms.

Result: The sum-over-paths mechanism generates non-zero flow coefficients $v_n$ for energetic particles, including at high $p_T$, providing an alternative explanation for observed anisotropies in small collision systems where traditional energy-loss models fail quantitatively.

Conclusion: Geometric quantum interference represents a fundamental mechanism contributing to flow observables across all system sizes, challenging the exclusive role of energy-loss selection biases in explaining high-$p_T$ anisotropies and offering new directions for understanding collectivity in small systems.

Abstract: The surprising manifestation of collectivity in small collision systems, such as nucleon-nucleon and nucleon-nucleus collisions, is perhaps even more striking when discussed at higher momenta. In larger systems, high-$p_T$ elliptic anisotropy is understood as a selection bias effect due to the smaller energy loss experienced along the shorter direction that aligns with the event plane. However, in small systems the amount of energy loss appears insufficient to reproduce the sizable angular anisotropy observed experimentally. In this work, we explore a new mechanism generating preferred orientations for energetic particles without the need of energy loss. We exploit a simple model that is based on two basic although inalienable ingredients: geometry and quantum mechanics. Our findings suggest that this sum-over-paths mechanism can provide a relevant contribution to so-called flow coefficients of energetic particles traversing deconfined media of any size.
