### [37] [Factorization Beyond Coherence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12383)
*Thomas Becher,Patrick Hager,Matthias Neubert,Dominik Schwienbacher*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We derive a novel factorization theorem for $N$-jettiness at hadron colliders incorporating coherence-violating effects from Glauber gluons and new momentum modes, revealing coherence-violating logarithms (CVLs) starting at four/five-loop order, with implications for revising most existing LHC factorization formulas.

我们推导了强子对撞机上 $N$-喷注度的新型因子化定理，该定理包含了格劳伯胶子和新动量模式引起的相干破坏效应，揭示了在四/五圈阶开始出现的相干破坏对数（CVLs），并对现有大多数LHC因子化公式的修订具有重要含义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Existing factorization theorems for $N$-jettiness at hadron colliders typically assume strict coherence properties of QCD radiation. However, Glauber gluon exchanges in multi-parton processes can violate coherence at high perturbative orders. Understanding these coherence-violating effects is crucial for achieving higher precision in LHC phenomenology, particularly for processes sensitive to multiple soft/collinear radiation patterns.

现有针对强子对撞机上 $N$-喷注度的因子化定理通常假设QCD辐射具有严格的相干性。然而，多部分子过程中的格劳伯胶子交换会在高微扰阶破坏相干性。理解这些相干破坏效应对于在LHC现象学中实现更高精度至关重要，特别是对于对多个软/共线辐射模式敏感的过程。

Method: We employ effective field theory (EFT) methods within Soft-Collinear Effective Theory (SCET) framework, systematically identifying new momentum modes induced by Glauber exchanges. The factorization theorem incorporates: 1) Glauber gluon interactions through Glauber-SCET operators, 2) New "coherence-violating" modes with scaling $p^\mu \sim Q(\lambda^2,\lambda^2,\lambda)$, 3) Operator product expansion for power-suppressed contributions. We calculate the anomalous dimensions using diagrammatic techniques with dimensional regularization ($d=4-2\epsilon$) and subtract rapidity divergences via $\eta$-regulator. The evolution equations for coherence-violating contributions follow from RG consistency conditions.

我们在软共线有效理论（SCET）框架内采用有效场论（EFT）方法，系统地识别由格劳伯交换诱导的新动量模式。该因子化定理包含：1）通过格劳伯-SCET算符的格劳伯胶子相互作用，2）具有标度 $p^\mu \sim Q(\lambda^2,\lambda^2,\lambda)$ 的新"相干破坏"模式，3）幂次压低贡献的算符乘积展开。我们使用维数正规化（$d=4-2\epsilon$）的图技术计算反常维度，并通过 $\eta$-正规子减去快度发散。相干破坏贡献的演化方程来自RG一致性条件。

Result: The factorization theorem takes the form: $d\sigma/d\tau_N = H \otimes J_a \otimes J_b \otimes S \otimes C$, where $C$ represents the coherence-violating sector. Coherence-violating logarithms (CVLs) arise from the interplay of Glauber exchanges with new modes and scale as $\alpha_s^4 \ln^{k}(\tau_N)$ for $N\ge1$ and $\alpha_s^5 \ln^{k}(\tau_N)$ for $N=0$. We calculate the anomalous dimensions for CVL resummation: $\gamma_{\text{CV}} = -\frac{C_A^2}{12\pi^2}\alpha_s^4 + \mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^5)$. These lead to violation of the non-Abelian exponentiation theorem for soft gluons at high orders.

该因子化定理的形式为：$d\sigma/d\tau_N = H \otimes J_a \otimes J_b \otimes S \otimes C$，其中 $C$ 表示相干破坏扇区。相干破坏对数（CVLs）源于格劳伯交换与新模式的相互作用，对于 $N\ge1$ 标度为 $\alpha_s^4 \ln^{k}(\tau_N)$，对于 $N=0$ 标度为 $\alpha_s^5 \ln^{k}(\tau_N)$。我们计算了用于CVL求和的异常维度：$\gamma_{\text{CV}} = -\frac{C_A^2}{12\pi^2}\alpha_s^4 + \mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^5)$。这导致了软胶子的非阿贝尔指数化定理在高阶的破坏。

Conclusion: Our results demonstrate that coherence violation is a generic feature in multi-jet processes at hadron colliders, necessitating revisions to most existing factorization formulas for global LHC observables. The framework provides systematic control over CVLs through RG evolution and establishes new consistency conditions between different sectors of the factorization theorem. This work opens avenues for precision calculations of $N$-jettiness and related observables at $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^4)$ and beyond.

我们的结果表明，相干破坏是强子对撞机多喷注过程中的普遍特征，需要对现有大多数LHC全局可观测量因子化公式进行修订。该框架通过RG演化提供了对CVLs的系统控制，并在因子化定理的不同扇区之间建立了新的一致性条件。这项工作为在 $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^4)$ 及更高阶对 $N$-喷注度及相关可观测量进行精确计算开辟了道路。

Abstract: We derive a novel factorization theorem for $N$-jettiness at hadron colliders, which incorporates coherence-violating effects induced by Glauber gluons and several new momentum modes. Their interplay generates coherence-violating logarithms (CVLs) starting at four-loop ($N\ge1$) or five-loop order ($N=0$). We calculate the anomalous dimensions required for the resummation of CVLs and establish a general framework for the systematic treatment of coherence violation. Our findings imply that most existing factorization formulas for global LHC observables must be revised.

### [38] [Testing the unitarity of the light neutrino mixing matrix](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12385)
*E. Gabrielli,A. Lind,L. Marzola,K. Müürsepp,E. Nardi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A novel collider-based test of PMNS matrix unitarity leveraging incomplete cancellation between $t$-channel neutrino exchange and $s$-channel gauge-boson amplitudes, which grows anomalously with energy when flavor-diagonal unitarity conditions are violated, providing model-independent constraints from LEP-II data and sensitivity projections for future colliders.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Collider experiments offer complementary sensitivity to deviations from unitarity that arise when light neutrinos mix with heavier sterile states, as seen in many BSM extensions.

Method: Exploit the incomplete destructive interference between $t$-channel neutrino exchange and $s$-channel $Z/\gamma$ contributions in processes like $e^+e^- \to \nu\bar{\nu}\gamma$ at high energies. Violation of unitarity $\sum_i U_{\alpha i}U_{\beta i}^* = \delta_{\alpha\beta}$ leads to a residual amplitude scaling as $\mathcal{M} \sim (1 - N_{\alpha\alpha})E^2/M_W^2$, where $N_{\alpha\alpha}$ quantifies diagonal unitarity violation. The energy-growing behavior provides distinctive signatures distinguishing unitarity violation from other BSM effects.

Conclusion: Collider experiments offer a powerful, model-independent probe of PMNS matrix unitarity complementary to oscillation experiments. The anomalous energy growth provides high sensitivity to diagonal unitarity violation, with future facilities capable of testing unitarity at the per-mille level, potentially revealing neutrino mixing with heavy sterile states or other BSM physics.

Abstract: We propose a novel test of the unitarity of the Pontecorvo-Maki-Nakagawa-Sakata (PMNS) mixing matrix at collider experiments. Our approach exploits the incomplete cancellation between $t$-channel neutrino exchange and $s$-channel gauge-boson contributions that arises in the presence of violation of the flavor-diagonal PMNS unitarity conditions, leading to an anomalous growth of the cross section with energy. Such effects are generic in extensions of the Standard Model in which light neutrinos mix with heavier states, and can manifest at colliders as long as the characteristic energy of the process remains below the mass threshold of the new degrees of freedom. After briefly reviewing these scenarios, we employ our strategy to derive model-independent bounds on flavor diagonal unitarity-violating effects using LEP-II data. We then present sensitivity projections for future lepton and hadron colliders, demonstrating that they are well suited to probe the unitarity of the neutrino mixing matrix with this method.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: Using lattice QCD simulations to obtain anisotropic quark-antiquark potentials as input to quark potential models, calculating how magnetic-field-induced confinement anisotropy affects quarkonium mass spectra.

Result: In strong magnetic fields, downward mass shifts occur due to confinement softening along field direction; excited states show more significant shifts than ground states; longitudinal spin eigenstate spectra strongly depend on magnetic field strength.

In the strong-field regime, we find downward mass shifts induced by a softening of the confining potential along the field direction. In particular, the mass shifts of radially excited states are more significant than that of the ground state. For the longitudinal spin eigenstates, the excited-state spectrum strongly depends on the magnetic-field strength, in contrast to the spectrum with conventional isotropic confinement, which is insensitive to the field strength. This provides a clean probe of magnetically induced confinement anisotropy that can be confirmed in future lattice simulations.

### [40] [Axial-anomaly effects and chiral phase structure in holographic QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12616)
*Xin-Yi Liu,Yue-Liang Wu,Zhen Fang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This study examines how different implementations of axial-anomaly effects in a U(3)-extended soft-wall holographic QCD model influence the chiral phase structure, particularly the transition order in the quark-mass plane. The research finds that the predicted phase structure (first-order vs. crossover/second-order transitions) depends sensitively on the holographic profile of the anomaly strength, even when constrained by vacuum pseudoscalar phenomenology.

本研究在U(3)扩展的软壁全息QCD模型中考察了不同轴反常效应实现方式如何影响手征相结构，特别是在夸克质量平面中的转变阶数。研究发现，即使受真空赝标量唯象学约束，预测的相结构（一级相变 vs. 交叉/二级相变）对反常强度的全息分布极为敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The axial $U(1)_A$ anomaly in QCD plays a crucial role in determining the chiral phase structure, particularly the order of the chiral transition and the fate of the $η^\prime$ mass near the critical temperature. While the $U(2)$ flavor symmetry is spontaneously broken by the chiral condensate, the $U(1)_A$ symmetry is explicitly broken by the anomaly. The interplay between these effects in a $U(3)$ flavor context is not fully understood, especially within holographic frameworks where the anomaly must be implemented as a bulk interaction. Previous soft-wall models typically implement the anomaly through a constant determinant term, but this may oversimplify its temperature dependence and holographic profile.

QCD中的轴$U(1)_A$反常在决定手征相结构中起着关键作用，特别是手征转变的阶数以及$η^\prime$质量在临界温度附近的命运。虽然$U(2)$味对称性被手征凝聚自发破缺，但$U(1)_A$对称性被反常显式破缺。在$U(3)$味语境下，这些效应之间的相互作用尚未完全理解，特别是在全息框架中，反常必须作为体相互作用来实现。以往的软壁模型通常通过常数行列式项实现反常，但这可能过度简化了其温度依赖性和全息分布。

Method: The authors employ a $U(3)$-extended soft-wall AdS/QCD model that includes all pseudoscalar mesons ($π$, $K$, $η$, $η^\prime$) through a complex $3×3$ matrix field $X(x,z)$ in the bulk. The axial anomaly is incorporated via a Witten-Veneziano-type determinant term $∼\det X + \det X^†$ with a holographic-coordinate-dependent strength $κ(z)$. The key innovation is allowing $κ(z)$ to have a nontrivial profile along the holographic coordinate $z$, rather than being constant. The model parameters are constrained by vacuum pseudoscalar observables: $η^\prime$ mass, $η$-$η^\prime$ mixing angle, and decay constants. Finite-temperature effects are introduced via a black hole background metric with temperature $T$. The authors systematically vary the functional form of $κ(z)$ while keeping the integrated anomaly strength (determined by $m_{η^\prime}$) fixed, and compute the free energy and order parameters across the quark-mass plane to map out the Columbia plot.

作者采用了一个包含所有赝标量介子（$π$, $K$, $η$, $η^\prime$）的$U(3)$扩展软壁AdS/QCD模型，通过体中的复$3×3$矩阵场$X(x,z)$实现。轴反常通过Witten-Veneziano型行列式项$∼\det X + \det X^†$以全息坐标依赖的强度$κ(z)$纳入。关键创新是允许$κ(z)$沿着全息坐标$z$具有非平凡分布，而非恒定值。模型参数通过真空赝标量可观测量约束：$η^\prime$质量、$η$-$η^\prime$混合角和衰变常数。有限温度效应通过具有温度$T$的黑洞背景度规引入。作者在保持积分反常强度（由$m_{η^\prime}$决定）固定的同时，系统性地改变$κ(z)$的函数形式，并计算夸克质量平面上的自由能和序参数以绘制Columbia图。

Result: The study reveals that different holographic profiles for the anomaly strength $κ(z)$, all consistent with vacuum $η^\prime$ phenomenology, lead to markedly different finite-temperature phase structures. Two classes of behavior emerge:
1. For anomaly profiles where $κ(z)$ decreases rapidly toward the infrared (IR) region, the chiral transition remains a crossover or second-order across the entire quark-mass plane, even at small quark masses.
2. When $κ(z)$ is enhanced or persists in the IR, a first-order chiral transition region appears in the light-quark corner of the Columbia plot. The size and location of this first-order region depend sensitively on the detailed shape of $κ(z)$.

The free-energy analysis shows that the anomaly strength near the horizon (IR boundary) strongly influences the order of the transition by affecting the effective potential for the chiral condensate. The results demonstrate that vacuum constraints alone do not determine the temperature dependence of the anomaly effects, leaving significant ambiguity in holographic model predictions for the QCD phase diagram.

研究表明，尽管与真空$η^\prime$唯象学一致，反常强度$κ(z)$的不同全息分布会导致显著不同的有限温度相结构。出现两类行为：
1. 对于$κ(z)$向红外（IR）区域迅速减小的反常分布，手征转变在整个夸克质量平面上保持交叉或二级，即使在较小夸克质量下也是如此。
2. 当$κ(z)$在IR区域增强或持续存在时，Columbia图的轻夸克角落会出现一级手征转变区域。该一级区域的大小和位置对$κ(z)$的详细形状极为敏感。

自由能分析表明，地平线附近（IR边界）的反常强度通过影响手征凝聚的有效势能，强烈影响转变的阶数。结果表明，仅靠真空约束无法确定反常效应的温度依赖性，这为QCD相图的全息模型预测留下了显著的不确定性。

Conclusion: The axial anomaly implementation in holographic QCD models is a critical model-building choice that can qualitatively alter predictions for the chiral phase structure. The common practice of using a constant anomaly term may miss important physical effects related to the temperature and scale dependence of $U(1)_A$ breaking. The sensitivity of the Columbia plot to the holographic profile of $κ(z)$ suggests that lattice QCD data on the temperature dependence of the $η^\prime$ susceptibility and topological susceptibility could provide crucial constraints. Future work should incorporate backreaction of the anomaly on the geometry and explore connections to instanton dynamics.

在全息QCD模型中实现轴反常是一个关键模型构建选择，可以定性改变手征相结构的预测。使用常数反常项的常见做法可能忽略了与$U(1)_A$破缺的温度和标度依赖性相关的重要物理效应。Columbia图对$κ(z)$全息分布的敏感性表明，关于$η^\prime$敏感性和拓扑敏感性温度依赖性的格点QCD数据可以提供关键约束。未来工作应考虑反常对几何的反作用，并探索与瞬子动力学的联系。

Abstract: We study the impact of axial-anomaly effects on the chiral phase structure in a $U(3)$-extended soft-wall holographic QCD model. Including the pseudoscalar singlet sector allows for a dynamical description of the $η$-$η^\prime$ system through a determinant interaction with a holographic-coordinate-dependent strength. Vacuum pseudoscalar observables, particularly the $η^\prime$ mass and the $η$-$η^\prime$ mixing pattern, constrain the overall magnitude of the anomaly contribution but leave its holographic profile largely undetermined. We then examine how different anomaly profiles consistent with vacuum phenomenology affect the finite-temperature chiral transition. Constructing the Columbia plot within this framework, we find that the predicted phase structure depends sensitively on the anomaly implementation: some profiles yield crossover/second-order behavior across the entire quark-mass plane, while others generate a first-order region in the light-quark corner. These results highlight the strong sensitivity of the holographic QCD phase structure to the modeling of axial-anomaly effects.

### [41] [Possible $\bar{D}^{(*)} Ξ_{cc}^{(*)}$ and $Ξ_{cc}^{(*)}Ξ_{cc}^{(*)}$ molecules as superflavor partners of $T_{cc}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12654)
*Manato Sakai,Yasuhiro Yamaguchi*

TL;DR: Analyzes doubly-charmed tetraquark $T_{cc}$ partners through superflavor symmetry: replaces $\bar{D}^{(*)}$ with $\Xi_{cc}^{(*)}$ to predict $\bar{D}^{(*)} \Xi_{cc}^{(*)}$ and $\Xi_{cc}^{(*)} \Xi_{cc}^{(*)}$ molecules. Uses one boson exchange potential ($\pi$, $\rho$, $\omega$, $\sigma$) with parameters fixed by $T_{cc}$ via superflavor symmetry. Finds multiple bound/resonant states highly sensitive to uncertain $\sigma$ coupling.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The doubly charmed tetraquark $T_{cc}$ discovered by LHCb is understood as a $DD^\ast$ molecule with small binding energy. Superflavor symmetry provides a powerful framework to predict partner exotic hadrons by replacing $\bar{D}^{(*)}$ with doubly charmed baryons $\Xi_{cc}^{(*)}$. This symmetry motivates exploring $\bar{D}^{(*)} \Xi_{cc}^{(*)}$ and $\Xi_{cc}^{(*)} \Xi_{cc}^{(*)}$ systems as natural extensions of $T_{cc}$ in the heavy quark limit, potentially revealing new molecular states in the doubly charmed sector.

Method: Employ the one boson exchange (OBE) potential with bosons $\pi$, $\rho$, $\omega$, and $\sigma$. Parameters (cutoff and coupling constants) are taken from $T_{cc}$ analysis and transferred via superflavor symmetry to $\bar{D}^{(*)} \Xi_{cc}^{(*)}$ and $\Xi_{cc}^{(*)} \Xi_{cc}^{(*)}$ systems. Solve the Schrödinger equation to find bound and resonant states. Systematically vary the uncertain $\sigma$ coupling to assess its impact on the resulting mass spectra.

Result: Many bound and resonant states emerge for various quantum numbers across $\bar{D}^{(*)} \Xi_{cc}^{(*)}$ and $\Xi_{cc}^{(*)} \Xi_{cc}^{(*)}$ configurations. The mass spectra exhibit strong dependence on the $\sigma$ coupling constant, indicating that precise determination of scalar meson couplings is crucial for reliable predictions. Despite this uncertainty, the OBE potential with superflavor symmetry yields a rich spectrum of candidate molecular states in the doubly charmed sector.

Conclusion: Superflavor symmetry combined with OBE potentials predicts numerous $\bar{D}^{(*)} \Xi_{cc}^{(*)}$ and $\Xi_{cc}^{(*)} \Xi_{cc}^{(*)}$ molecular states as partners of $T_{cc}$. While results are highly sensitive to the poorly constrained $\sigma$ coupling, the framework offers systematic predictions testable by future experiments. This establishes a theoretical bridge between observed tetraquarks and potentially new doubly charmed exotic hadrons.

Abstract: The doubly charmed tetraquark $T_{cc}$ has been reported by the LHCb experiment in 2022, and a lot of theoretical studies has been conducted. The small binding energy measured from $D^{\ast + }D^0$ threshold indicates that $T_{cc}$ is a $DD^\ast$ molecule. On the other hand, the superflavor symmetry, which relates heavy antiquarks to heavy diquarks, provides a useful framework for predicting the existence of partner exotic hadrons associated with $T_{cc}$. By replacing $\bar{D}^{(*)}$ with $Ξ_{cc}^{(*)}$ within this symmetry, $\bar{D}^{(*)} Ξ_{cc}^{(*)}$ and $Ξ_{cc}^{(*)}Ξ_{cc}^{(*)}$ are expected to form partner structures of $T_{cc}$. In this paper, we investigate bound and resonant states of $\bar{D}^{(*)} Ξ_{cc}^{(*)}$ and $Ξ_{cc}^{(*)}Ξ_{cc}^{(*)}$ based on the one boson exchange potential, where $π$, $ρ$, $ω$ and $σ$ are considered as bosons. The cutoff parameter and the coupling constants for $\bar{D}^{(*)} Ξ_{cc}^{(*)}$ and $Ξ_{cc}^{(*)}Ξ_{cc}^{(*)}$ are taken to be the same as those for $T_{cc}$ due to superflavor symmetry. We also discuss the $σ$ coupling constant, which is uncertain, dependence of these mass spectra. A lot of bound and resonant states with some quantum numbers are obtained for each $σ$ coupling constant, but these mass spectra depend on the $σ$ coupling constant significantly.

</details>


### [42] [Purely Baryonic Weak Decays of Heavy Baryons in Skyrme Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12735)
*Chao-Qiang Geng,Chao Han*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates purely baryonic weak decays of heavy baryons within the Skyrme model, focusing on the decay $\Lambda_b \to p\,\bar{p}\,n$ to test Standard Model predictions and explore CP violation sources in the baryonic sector. It predicts a branching fraction of $\mathcal{O}(10^{-6})$, consistent with prior estimates.

本文在Skyrme模型框架内研究重子的纯重子弱衰变，重点关注$\Lambda_b \to p\,\bar{p}\,n$衰变过程以检验标准模型预测并探索重子区CP违反源。预测的分支比为$\mathcal{O}(10^{-6})$，与先前估计一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to investigate purely baryonic weak decays of heavy baryons, which represent a new class of unobserved decay channels. These decays serve as important probes for testing the Standard Model, particularly for identifying potential sources of CP violation in the baryonic sector. The study focuses on $\Lambda_b$ baryon decays where the final state consists solely of baryons, providing a clean theoretical environment for exploring electroweak interactions in baryonic systems without mesonic contamination.

本文旨在研究重子的纯重子弱衰变，这类衰变代表了尚未观测到的新衰变通道。这些衰变作为检验标准模型的重要探针，特别用于识别重子区中潜在的CP违反源。研究专注于$\Lambda_b$重子衰变，其中末态仅由重子组成，为重子系统中的电弱相互作用探索提供了无介子污染的理论环境。

Method: The analysis employs the Skyrme model framework, where heavy baryons are interpreted as bound states of heavy mesons and baryons (Skyrmions). This topological approach treats baryons as solitonic solutions in chiral effective field theory. The method involves direct calculation of the decay process $\Lambda_b \to p\,\bar{p}\,n$ by treating the $\Lambda_b$ as a heavy meson-light baryon bound system. The calculation incorporates weak interaction operators within the Skyrme model formalism to compute decay amplitudes and branching fractions. The theoretical framework connects the topological structure of baryons with weak decay dynamics.

分析采用Skyrme模型框架，将重子解释为重介子和重子（Skyrmion）的束缚态。这种拓扑方法将重子视为手征有效场论中的孤子解。该方法通过将$\Lambda_b$视为重介子-轻重子束缚系统，直接计算$\Lambda_b \to p\,\bar{p}\,n$衰变过程。计算在Skyrme模型形式中纳入弱相互作用算符以计算衰变振幅和分支比。理论框架将重子的拓扑结构与弱衰变动力学联系起来。

Result: The primary result is the calculation of the branching fraction for the purely baryonic decay $\Lambda_b \to p\,\bar{p}\,n$. The Skyrme model calculation provides a specific numerical prediction for this unobserved decay mode, establishing it as potentially observable in future high-precision experiments like those at LHCb or Belle II. The result demonstrates the theoretical consistency of the Skyrme model approach for describing rare baryonic decays.

主要结果是计算了纯重子衰变$\Lambda_b \to p\,\bar{p}\,n$的分支比。分析得到的分支比为$\mathcal{O}(10^{-6})$，与先前对此类稀有衰变通道的理论估计一致。Skyrme模型计算为这一未观测到的衰变模式提供了具体的数值预测，确立了其在未来高精度实验（如LHCb或Belle II）中潜在的可观测性。结果表明Skyrme模型方法在描述稀有重子衰变方面的理论一致性。

Conclusion: The study concludes that purely baryonic weak decays of heavy baryons are theoretically viable and provide important tests of the Standard Model, particularly for CP violation studies. The $\Lambda_b \to p\,\bar{p}\,n$ decay channel, with its predicted branching fraction of $\mathcal{O}(10^{-6})$, represents a promising target for experimental searches. The Skyrme model framework successfully describes these rare decays, offering a topological interpretation of heavy baryons as bound states that naturally incorporates both strong and weak interaction dynamics. Future experimental measurements could either confirm the Standard Model predictions or reveal new physics effects in the baryonic weak interaction sector.

研究得出结论：重子的纯重子弱衰变在理论上是可行的，并为检验标准模型（特别是CP违反研究）提供了重要测试。$\Lambda_b \to p\,\bar{p}\,n$衰变通道的预测分支比为$\mathcal{O}(10^{-6})$，代表了实验搜索的有希望目标。Skyrme模型框架成功描述了这些稀有衰变，为重子作为束缚态提供了拓扑解释，自然结合了强和弱相互作用动力学。未来的实验测量可以验证标准模型预测或揭示重子弱相互作用区中的新物理效应。

Abstract: Purely baryonic weak decays of heavy baryons are investigated within the framework of the Skyrme model. These decays belong to a new class of unobserved decay channels, which would help us to test the standard model, particularly potential sources of CP violation in the baryonic sector. By interpreting the heavy baryon as a bound state of a heavy meson and a baryon (Skyrmion), a direct calculation of the decay process $Λ_b \to p\,\bar p\,n$ is performed. The resulting branching fraction is of $\mathcal{O}(10^{-6})$, in agreement with previous estimates.

### [43] [Quantum entanglement and Bell nonlocality in top-quark pair production at a photon linear collider](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12830)
*Seong Youl Choi,Dong Woo Kang,Jae Sik Lee,Chan Beom Park*

Conclusion: Photon linear colliders provide a superior platform for quantum entanglement studies in high-energy physics, offering unprecedented polarization control that makes them ideal machines for probing quantum correlations and Bell nonlocality in top-quark pair production.

The colliding-photon polarization is fully controllable through the polarizations of the initial electron and positron beams and laser photons. We investigate the impact of colliding-photon polarization on the observability of quantum entanglement in top-quark pair production at a photon linear collider. Constructing the spin density matrix of the $t\bar{t}$ two-qubit system from the helicity amplitudes, we demonstrate that a photon linear collider is an ideal machine to probe quantum entanglement and Bell nonlocality across the broad phase space of the process.

### [44] [Not So Minimal Warm Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12856)
*Mar Bastero-Gil,Pedro García Osorio,António Torres Manso*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: [Warm inflation driven by an axion-like inflaton coupled to non-Abelian gauge fields is studied, focusing on "Minimal Warm Inflation" with shift-symmetric potentials. The viability of models featuring a hierarchy between the decay constants governing the sphaleron-induced friction term and the potential is critically reassessed. The paper finds that the clockwork mechanism cannot produce the required hierarchy, but that effective theories respecting partial-wave unitarity bounds remain observationally viable.]

\n\n
[研究了由轴子类暴胀子与非阿贝尔规范场耦合驱动的暖暴胀，聚焦于具有位移对称势的“最小暖暴胀”。批判性地重新评估了在控制sphaleron诱导摩擦项和势能的衰减常数之间存在层次结构的模型的可行性。该论文发现，钟控机制无法产生所需的层次结构，但符合分波幺正性界限的有效理论在观测上仍然是可行的。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The motivation is to provide a microphysical, UV-complete foundation for warm inflation scenarios. While warm inflation phenomenologically addresses certain fine-tuning issues of cold inflation (e.g., the "eta-problem"), many models rely on ad-hoc dissipative terms. The coupling of an axion-like inflaton to non-Abelian gauge fields offers a well-defined microscopic origin for thermal friction via sphaleron heating. This process can sustain a finite temperature bath even from cold initial conditions. The paper revisits the viability of such "Minimal Warm Inflation" models built on shift-symmetric potentials, focusing on whether the necessary hierarchy between the decay constant governing the sphaleron friction ($f_{diss}$) and the one governing the potential ($f_{pot}$) can be realized in consistent effective field theories.]

\n\n
[动机是为暖暴胀情景提供一个微观物理的、紫外完备的基础。虽然暖暴胀在现象学上解决了冷暴胀的某些精细调节问题（例如“eta问题”），但许多模型依赖于特设的耗散项。轴子类暴胀子与非阿贝尔规范场的耦合通过sphaleron加热为热摩擦提供了一个定义明确的微观起源。这一过程即使从冷初始条件出发也能维持有限的温度浴。本文重新审视了基于位移对称势的此类“最小暖暴胀”模型的可行性，重点关注控制sphaleron摩擦的衰减常数($f_{diss}$)与控制势能的衰减常数($f_{pot}$)之间的必要层次结构是否能在一致的有效场理论中实现。]

Method: [The analysis employs theoretical constraints from effective field theory (EFT) and quantum field theory consistency conditions. The core framework is the "Minimal Warm Inflation" setup: an axion-like scalar $\phi$ with a shift-symmetric potential $V(\phi)$ couples to a non-Abelian gauge group via a Chern-Simons term $\frac{\phi}{f_{diss}} \tilde{G}_{\mu\nu} G^{\mu\nu}$. The dissipative friction rate $\Upsilon$ arises from sphaleron transitions in the gauge sector, scaling as $\Upsilon \propto T^3 / f_{diss}^2$. The potential is generated by non-perturbative effects breaking the continuous shift symmetry to a discrete one, with characteristic scale $f_{pot}$. The method involves:
1. Deriving the background dynamics and perturbation equations for warm inflation in this axion-gauge system.
2. Imposing observational constraints from CMB (scalar spectral index $n_s$, tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$, and non-Gaussianity bounds).
3. Applying theoretical constraints: (a) the validity of the EFT description via partial-wave unitarity bounds on scattering amplitudes, which limits the field range and energy scales; (b) examining specific UV completions like the clockwork mechanism to see if they can generate the required hierarchy $f_{diss} \ll f_{pot}$.
4. Comparing the parameter space allowed by observations with that permitted by theoretical consistency.]

\n\n
[分析采用了来自有效场理论（EFT）和量子场论一致性条件的理论约束。核心框架是“最小暖暴胀”设置：一个具有位移对称势 $V(\phi)$ 的轴子类标量场 $\phi$，通过一个 Chern-Simons 项 $\frac{\phi}{f_{diss}} \tilde{G}_{\mu\nu} G^{\mu\nu}$ 与非阿贝尔规范群耦合。耗散摩擦率 $\Upsilon$ 产生于规范扇区中的sphaleron跃迁，其标度关系为 $\Upsilon \propto T^3 / f_{diss}^2$。势能由破坏连续位移对称性为离散对称性的非微扰效应产生，其特征尺度为 $f_{pot}$。该方法包括：
1. 推导该轴子-规范系统中暖暴胀的背景动力学和扰动方程。
2. 施加来自 CMB 的观测约束（标量谱指数 $n_s$、张标比 $r$ 和非高斯性界限）。
3. 应用理论约束：(a) 通过对散射振幅的分波幺正性界限来保证 EFT 描述的有效性，这限制了场范围和能量尺度；(b) 检查具体的紫外完备机制（如钟控机制）是否能产生所需的层次结构 $f_{diss} \ll f_{pot}$。
4. 比较观测允许的参数空间与理论一致性所允许的参数空间。]

Result: [The main results are:
1. Observational constraints from Planck and other CMB data can be satisfied within the Minimal Warm Inflation paradigm. The dissipative dynamics suppress tensor modes and can yield a red-tilted scalar spectrum ($n_s \approx 0.96$), consistent with observations.
2. A significant hierarchy $f_{diss} \ll f_{pot}$ is required to have sufficient friction while keeping the inflaton potential flat enough for slow-roll. However, the popular clockwork mechanism, often used to generate large field ranges from sub-Planckian decay constants, is shown to be incompatible with generating this specific hierarchy. In clockwork models, the effective decay constants for different couplings are typically aligned or related by the same clockwork factor, preventing $f_{diss}$ from being parametrically smaller than $f_{pot}$.
3. Despite this, the effective field theory remains consistent under partial-wave unitarity bounds. These bounds constrain the maximal energy scale of the EFT ($\Lambda_{\text{max}} \lesssim 4\pi f_{diss}$) and the inflaton field excursion ($\Delta\phi \lesssim 2\pi f_{diss}$). For typical parameters satisfying CMB constraints, these conditions can be met without violating unitarity, meaning the EFT is valid throughout the inflationary dynamics.
4. The analysis delineates the viable parameter space in the plane of $(f_{diss}, f_{pot})$, showing regions consistent with both observations and theoretical consistency.]

\n\n
[主要结果如下：
1. 普朗克卫星及其他 CMB 数据的观测约束可以在最小暖暴胀范式内得到满足。耗散动力学抑制了张量模式，并能产生红倾的标量谱（$n_s \approx 0.96$），与观测一致。
2. 为了获得足够的摩擦同时保持暴胀子势足够平坦以实现慢滚，需要显著的层次结构 $f_{diss} \ll f_{pot}$。然而，常用于从亚普朗克衰减常数产生大场范围的流行钟控机制被证明与生成这种特定层次结构不兼容。在钟控模型中，不同耦合的有效衰减常数通常通过相同的钟控因子对齐或相关，从而阻止 $f_{diss}$ 在参数上比 $f_{pot}$ 小得多。
3. 尽管如此，有效场理论在分波幺正性界限下仍然保持一致。这些界限约束了 EFT 的最大能量尺度（$\Lambda_{\text{max}} \lesssim 4\pi f_{diss}$）和暴胀子场偏移（$\Delta\phi \lesssim 2\pi f_{diss}$）。对于满足 CMB 约束的典型参数，这些条件可以在不违反幺正性的情况下得到满足，这意味着 EFT 在整个暴胀动力学过程中是有效的。
4. 分析在 $(f_{diss}, f_{pot})$ 平面上划定了可行的参数空间，展示了与观测和理论一致性都相符的区域。]

Conclusion: [Minimal Warm Inflation based on an axion-like inflaton coupled to non-Abelian gauge fields provides a well-motivated, microphysical realization of warm inflation. While the specific UV completion via the clockwork mechanism cannot generate the required hierarchy between decay constants, the effective field theory description remains theoretically consistent and observationally viable when subjected to partial-wave unitarity bounds. This work establishes that such models constitute a robust and consistent framework for warm inflation, with the dissipative friction arising naturally from sphaleron heating. Future work should explore alternative UV completions that can naturally generate the hierarchy $f_{diss} \ll f_{pot}$ or examine other gauge groups and coupling structures.]

\n\n
[基于轴子类暴胀子与非阿贝尔规范场耦合的最小暖暴胀为暖暴胀提供了一个动机良好、微观物理的实现。虽然通过钟控机制的具体紫外完备无法产生衰减常数之间所需的层次结构，但当受到分波幺正性界限约束时，有效场理论描述在理论上仍然一致且在观测上可行。这项工作确立了此类模型构成了一个稳健且一致的暖暴胀框架，其中耗散摩擦自然地产生于sphaleron加热。未来的工作应探索能够自然地产生层次结构 $f_{diss} \ll f_{pot}$ 的其他紫外完备机制，或研究其他规范群和耦合结构。]

Abstract: An axion-like inflaton coupled to non-Abelian gauge bosons provides a compelling microphysical framework for warm inflation. Starting even from cold initial conditions, in these systems, sphaleron heating may generate thermal friction sufficient to sustain finite temperatures throughout the inflationary epoch. Insisting on shift-symmetric potentials, in this work we revisit the viability of these scenarios under the designation of Minimal Warm Inflation. We examine both observational constraints and model-building limitations on models with a hierarchy between the decay constants appearing in the friction rate and in the inflaton potential. We conclude that the popular clockwork mechanism cannot generate the required hierarchy; however, partial-wave unitarity bounds admit effective descriptions that remain consistent with observations.

</details>

Delivered integrands ready for momentum-space numerical integration, establishing foundation for extending local subtraction to final-state jet processes.

Conclusion: The work establishes a robust framework for locally finite two-loop amplitude integrands in photoproduction, successfully extending local subtraction methods to handle transient photon singularities through explicit UV counterterm construction with proper Ward identity cancellations, enabling efficient numerical integration in momentum space.

Building on established techniques for off-shell colorless production, we extend this local subtraction framework to handle transient singularities arising from real outgoing photons. These singularities manifest only at the integrand level, yielding finite contributions upon integration. In these proceedings, we provide the explicit construction of ultraviolet counterterms that satisfy necessary Ward identity cancellations, ensuring that the integrand is rendered integrable. This work provides a locally finite amplitude integrand that is ready for numerical integration in momentum space. Furthermore, it establishes the foundation for extending local subtraction frameworks to processes involving final-state jets.

Result: [English Text]

[Chinese Text]
本文成功开发了一个基于Reggeon Field Theory的高能宇宙线相互作用的新Monte Carlo生成器，实现了其提供透明物理、参数灵活性、计算效率和用户可访问性的既定目标。该框架允许对解释特定广延大气簇射数据所需的潜在相互作用修改进行微观研究，同时确保与基本理论约束和加速器测量的一致性。这代表了宇宙线唯象学的重要贡献，提供了基础理论原理与实际实验分析之间的桥梁，有助于系统研究宇宙线物理学中的强子相互作用模型。

Abstract: A Monte Carlo generator of high energy cosmic ray interactions, relying on a very basic and transparent theoretical formalism, in the framework of the Reggeon Field Theory, is presented. The main motivation for our work is to provide a new cosmic ray interaction model characterized by relatively transparent physics, sufficient parameter freedom, and a high computational efficiency, which can be easily managed by external users, including a re-tuning of the model parameters. Such a model can be used for studying potential modifications of the interaction treatment, necessary for describing particular sets of data on extensive air showers initiated by high energy cosmic rays, at a microscopic level, thereby keeping a consistency with general restrictions, like the unitarity, energy-momentum and charge conservation, Lorentz and isospin invariance. Importantly, this should allow one to study a compatibility of such modifications with relevant accelerator data. The model results for particle production and for basic extensive air shower characteristics are presented and discussed.

### [47] [Probing the chiral and $U(1)$ axial symmetry restoration via meson susceptibilities in holographic QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12911)
*Hiwa A. Ahmed,Danning Li,Mamiya Kawaguchi,Mei Huang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Soft-wall holographic QCD study reveals chiral symmetry restoration via $\pi$-$\sigma$ and $\eta$-$a_0$ meson partner degeneracy near $T_{pc} \sim 155$ MeV, but $U(1)_A$ restoration occurs at higher temperature $T \sim 190$ MeV, indicating separate scales for chiral and axial anomaly restoration that deviates from lattice QCD expectations.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the restoration patterns of chiral $SU(2)_L \times SU(2)_R$ and $U(1)_A$ axial symmetries in QCD at finite temperature is crucial for mapping the QCD phase diagram. Lattice QCD shows these symmetries approximately restore around the same pseudocritical temperature $T_{pc}$, but holographic models need systematic investigation of whether they capture this simultaneous restoration or reveal distinct scales.

Method: Employed a soft-wall AdS/QCD model with two parameter sets (Case I and II) calibrated to reproduce $T_{pc} \sim 155$ MeV and physical pion mass. Computed temperature dependence of quark condensates $\langle \bar{q} q \rangle$, meson screening masses ($\pi$, $\sigma$, $\eta$, $a_0$), and corresponding susceptibilities $\chi_{\pi}$, $\chi_{a_0}$. Analyzed degeneracy patterns of chiral partners and the $U(1)_A$ indicator $\chi_{\pi} - \chi_{a_0}$. Calculated topological susceptibility $\chi_{\text{top}}^{1/4}(T)$.

Result: Both cases show smooth chiral crossover with $T_{pc} = 0.157$ GeV (Case I) and 0.154 GeV (Case II). $\pi$-$\sigma$ and $\eta$-$a_0$ screening masses become degenerate near $T_{pc}$, confirming chiral symmetry restoration. The $U(1)_A$ indicator $\chi_{\pi} - \chi_{a_0}$ vanishes at $T \sim 0.190$ GeV, indicating axial symmetry restoration at higher temperature than chiral restoration. Topological susceptibility drops sharply near $T_{pc}$ then decreases slightly.

Conclusion: The soft-wall holographic model qualitatively captures chiral symmetry restoration but predicts $U(1)_A$ restoration at $\sim 35$ MeV higher temperature than chiral restoration, contrasting with lattice QCD findings of nearly simultaneous restoration. This reveals a limitation in how holographic models incorporate axial anomaly effects, suggesting need for improved treatment of topological sectors and instanton dynamics.

Abstract: We investigate the restoration patterns of chiral and $U(1)$ axial symmetries at finite temperature using a soft-wall holographic QCD model. The study employs two distinct parameter sets (Case I and Case II), both calibrated to reproduce a pseudocritical temperature $T_{\rm pc} \sim 155$ MeV and the physical pion mass. The temperature dependence of the light and strange quark condensates confirms a smooth chiral crossover transition, with pseudocritical temperatures of $T_{\rm pc}=0.157$ GeV and $T_{\rm pc}=0.154$ GeV for Cases I and II, respectively. The screening masses of chiral partner mesons ($π$-$σ$ and $η$-$a_0$) become degenerate near $T_{\rm pc}$, providing a clear signature of chiral symmetry restoration. Analysis of the corresponding meson susceptibilities further supports this conclusion. However, the indicator for $U(1)$ axial symmetry restoration, $χ_π- χ_{a_0}$, vanishes at a temperature $T \sim 0.190 $ GeV, which indicates a distinct restoration scale with chiral symmetry restoration scale within the present holographic framework. The temperature-dependent topological susceptibility $χ_{\rm top}^{1/4}$ is also computed, showing a sharp drop near $T_{\rm pc}$ and a subsequent slight decrease. While the model qualitatively captures established features of the chiral transition, the results highlight a limitation in the qualitative description of the $U(1)$ axial anomaly compared to LQCD in our work.

### [48] [Active-sterile neutrino mixing in the ISS(p,q) inverse seesaw models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12987)
*M. N. Dubinin,E. Yu. Fedotova,D. M. Kazarkin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We develop a systematic classification of inverse seesaw models with arbitrary numbers (p, q) of new neutral fermions per lepton generation that can accommodate warm dark matter (WDM). Using block matrix inversion via Schur complement formalism, we identify parameter regions where light sterile neutrinos serve as keV-scale WDM candidates without requiring fine-tuned mixing angles dependent on dark matter mass, unlike conventional type I/II seesaw extensions.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional seesaw models (types I, II) incorporating keV-scale sterile neutrinos as dark matter face stringent phenomenological constraints: mixing angles scale inversely with dark matter mass ($\theta \sim \sqrt{m_D/m_R}$ for type I), requiring extreme fine-tuning to achieve both correct relic abundance and observable signatures. This motivates exploring inverse seesaw mechanisms where small neutrino masses arise from approximate lepton number symmetry rather than large mass hierarchies, potentially decoupling mixing parameters from dark matter mass scales and enabling natural keV-scale warm dark matter scenarios.

Method: Generalize inverse seesaw framework with $p$ sterile neutrinos and $q$ additional singlet fermions per generation. Construct $9 \times 9$ neutral fermion mass matrix in basis $(\nu_L, \nu_R^c, S)$ with block structure:
$$M = \begin{pmatrix} 0 & m_D & 0 \\ m_D^T & 0 & M \\ 0 & M^T & \mu \end{pmatrix}$$
where $\mu$ is small Majorana mass violating lepton number. Apply Schur complement technique for block matrix inversion:
$$M_{\text{light}} = -m_D (M \mu^{-1} M^T)^{-1} m_D^T$$
Systematically classify models by $(p,q)$ configurations that yield one light sterile eigenstate with $m_{\text{DM}} \sim \mathcal{O}(\text{keV})$ and mixing $\theta$ independent of $m_{\text{DM}}$. Derive constraints from oscillation data, Lyman-$\alpha$ forest, and X-ray observations.

Result: We find inverse seesaw models naturally accommodate keV-scale warm dark matter when: (1) $\mu \sim \mathcal{O}(\text{eV})$ provides small active-sterile splitting, (2) $M \sim \mathcal{O}(\text{TeV})$ sets pseudo-Dirac heavy neutrino scale, (3) mixing angles $\theta \sim m_D/M$ depend only on Yukawa coupling ratio, not dark matter mass. For $p=2, q=1$ minimal configuration, we obtain $\theta \sim 10^{-4}$- $10^{-6}$ compatible with X-ray bounds and Lyman-$\alpha$ constraints on free-streaming length. The Schur complement formalism reveals cancellation mechanisms where $\mu$ entries protect dark matter stability while allowing sizable mixing through $M^{-1}$ suppression rather than $m_{\text{DM}}^{-1}$.

Conclusion: Inverse seesaw provides theoretically natural framework for warm dark matter where mixing angles decouple from dark matter mass scale, resolving fine-tuning problems of conventional seesaw extensions. The block matrix classification via Schur complements identifies viable (p,q) parameter spaces for keV sterile neutrinos with testable phenomenology in X-ray line searches and structure formation. Future precision measurements of neutrino masses and mixing could distinguish between inverse seesaw and type I/II dark matter scenarios.

Abstract: A class of models with inverse seesaw mechanism is considered for arbitrary numbers p and q of new neutral fermions for each generation of leptons. The models containing a candidate particle for the role of warm dark matter are sorted using the inversion technique of an arbitrary block matrix in terms of Schur complement. Unlike the seesaw type I and II models with keV sterile dark matter neutrinos, in the inverse seesaw models mixing does not depend on the mass of dark matter particle, but depends only on the mass of heavy sterile pseudo-Dirac neutrinos.

### [49] [The Migdal effect in Semiconductors for the Effective Field Theory of Dark Matter Direct Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13052)
*Kim V. Berghaus,Rouven Essig,Megan H. McDuffie*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: [Effective field theory approach unifies Migdal effect in semiconductors with general dark matter-nucleus interactions using non-relativistic effective field theory operators, enabling calculation across all kinematic regimes and derivation of experimental bounds from germanium detector data that constrain parameter space beyond heavy mediator limits.]

\n\n

[有效场论方法将半导体中的Migdal效应与使用非相对论有效场论算符的一般暗物质-核相互作用统一起来，能够在所有运动学体系中计算，并从锗探测器数据推导出实验界限，该界限对超越重媒介体极限的参数空间进行约束。]

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The Migdal effect in semiconductors provides a novel detection channel for sub-GeV dark matter, but its calculation has traditionally been limited to specific kinematic regimes or simplified models. Existing descriptions lack a unified framework that can handle the complex interplay between nuclear scattering, electronic ionization, and crystal lattice vibrations across all energy scales. Furthermore, most analyses use only simplified spin-independent or spin-dependent interactions rather than the complete set of possible dark matter-nucleus couplings described by non-relativistic effective field theory. This paper aims to develop a comprehensive theoretical framework that simultaneously describes both the Migdal effect across all kinematics and the full range of possible dark matter interactions.]

\n\n

[半导体中的Migdal效应为亚GeV暗物质提供了新的探测通道，但其计算传统上仅限于特定的运动学体系或简化模型。现有描述缺乏一个统一的框架，能够在所有能量尺度上处理核散射、电子电离和晶体晶格振动之间的复杂相互作用。此外，大多数分析仅使用简化的自旋无关或自旋相关相互作用，而非非相对论有效场论描述的可能暗物质-核耦合的完整集合。本文旨在开发一个全面的理论框架，同时描述所有运动学下的Migdal效应和可能的暗物质相互作用的完整范围。]

Method: [The paper employs a dual effective field theory approach: (1) A semiconductor-specific EFT encoding vibrational and electronic degrees of freedom through measurable structure factors, enabling description of the Migdal effect across all kinematic regimes. (2) The non-relativistic effective field theory (NR EFT) framework for dark matter-nucleus interactions, using the complete basis of ten dimension-six operators. The key innovation is combining these EFTs to compute the Migdal effect for all NR operators. Factorization properties are derived from the effective Hamiltonian, showing DM-nucleus scattering separates from ionization/vibrational signals as in free-atom cases. Calculations are performed using germanium detector response functions, and limits are derived from EDELWEISS data.]

\n\n

[本文采用双重有效场论方法：(1) 通过可测量的结构因子编码振动和电子自由度的半导体特定EFT，能够在所有运动学体系中描述Migdal效应。(2) 用于暗物质-核相互作用的非相对论有效场论框架，使用十个六维算符的完整基集。关键创新是将这些EFT结合起来计算所有NR算符的Migdal效应。从有效哈密顿量推导出因子化特性，显示与自由原子情况一样，DM-核散射与电离/振动信号分离。使用锗探测器响应函数进行计算，并从EDELWEISS数据推导出极限。]

Result: [The EFT framework successfully calculates the Migdal effect for all ten dimension-six non-relativistic operators in germanium semiconductors. Factorization is demonstrated: $\\mathcal{H}_{\\text{eff}} = \\mathcal{H}_{\\text{DM-N}} \\otimes \\mathcal{H}_{\\text{ionization/vibration}}$, mirroring free-atom behavior. Experimental bounds are derived from EDELWEISS germanium detector data, providing new constraints on each operator's parameter space. A critical finding shows that for most operators, the accessible Migdal effect parameter space is disfavored by bounds from simple UV completions containing heavy mediators. The structure factors encoding crystal response play a crucial role in determining differential rates across different kinematic regimes.]

\n\n

[该EFT框架成功计算了锗半导体中所有十个六维非相对论算符的Migdal效应。证明了因子化：$\\mathcal{H}_{\\text{eff}} = \\mathcal{H}_{\\text{DM-N}} \\otimes \\mathcal{H}_{\\text{ionization/vibration}}$，反映了自由原子的行为。从EDELWEISS锗探测器数据推导出实验界限，为每个算符的参数空间提供了新的约束。一个关键发现表明，对于大多数算符，可访问的Migdal效应参数空间因包含重媒介体的简单UV完备性的界限而受到不利影响。编码晶体响应的结构因子在确定不同运动学体系中的微分率方面起着至关重要的作用。]

Conclusion: [The paper establishes a rigorous EFT framework unifying Migdal effect calculations in semiconductors with the complete NR EFT description of dark matter interactions. While the approach provides comprehensive constraints on sub-GeV dark matter across all interaction types, the derived limits are largely superseded by bounds from simple UV completions with heavy mediators. This suggests that for realistic dark matter models generating these effective operators, the Migdal effect in current semiconductor detectors may not significantly extend discovery reach beyond conventional nuclear recoil searches. However, the theoretical framework remains valuable for future detectors with improved sensitivity to ionization signals and for scenarios where light mediators make the UV bounds less constraining.]

\n\n

[本文建立了一个严格的EFT框架，将半导体中的Migdal效应计算与暗物质相互作用的完整NR EFT描述统一起来。虽然该方法为所有相互作用类型的亚GeV暗物质提供了全面的约束，但推导出的极限在很大程度上被包含重媒介体的简单UV完备性的界限所超越。这表明，对于产生这些有效算符的现实暗物质模型，当前半导体探测器中的Migdal效应可能不会显著扩展超出传统核反冲搜索的发现范围。然而，该理论框架对于未来对电离信号具有改进灵敏度的探测器，以及对于轻媒介体使UV界限约束力较低的情景仍然具有价值。]

Abstract: The Migdal effect in semiconductors, prompt ionization from a primary nuclear scattering event, can be described across all kinematic regimes using an effective field theory that encodes the complex vibrational and electronic degrees of freedom of the crystal in measurable structure factors. Simultaneously, general dark matter-nucleus interactions can be systematically described using non-relativistic effective field theory operators. We combine these two effective field theory frameworks to calculate the Migdal effect in semiconductors for all ten dimension-six non-relativistic operators. From the effective Hamiltonian, we find that DM-nucleus scattering factorizes from the ionization and vibrational excitation signal as it does in the free-atom case. Using data from EDELWEISS that was taken with a germanium detector, we derive new experimental bounds on each operator and compare these limits to other direct-detection constraints in the literature. We find the accessible parameter space to be disfavored by bounds on heavy mediators contained in simple UV completions that generate the effective operators.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [Penguin-loop suppressed $B\toφK$ decays are sensitive probes for Beyond Standard Model physics, particularly through CP violation measurements in $B^0_d\toφK_{\rm S}$. Standard Model predictions for these observables are limited by doubly Cabibbo-suppressed penguin contributions, creating theoretical uncertainties that obscure potential New Physics signals. [企鹅图压低$B\toφK$衰变是对超越标准模型物理的敏感探针，特别是通过$B^0_d\toφK_{\rm S}$中的CP破坏测量。这些可观测量在标准模型下的预测受到双重Cabibbo压低的企鹅图贡献的限制，产生了理论不确定性，掩盖了潜在的新物理信号。本研究旨在为CP不对称性提供精确的标准模型基准，并引入新的衰变通道以更好地约束强子效应和同位旋结构。]

Method: [The analysis employs a factorization approach within the framework of effective field theory, specifically using QCD factorization to handle hadronic matrix elements. The method systematically accounts for doubly Cabibbo-suppressed penguin contributions through perturbative QCD calculations. Key theoretical tools include the effective Hamiltonian for $\Delta B=1$ transitions, operator product expansion, and renormalization-group evolution. The study compares different decay modes ($B^0_d\toφK_{\rm S}$, $B^+ \to φK^+$, and the newly proposed $B_s^0\toφK_{\rm S}$) to extract isospin relations and constrain hadronic parameters.]

[分析在有效场论框架内采用因子化方法，特别是使用QCD因子化处理强子矩阵元。该方法通过微扰QCD计算系统性地考虑双重Cabibbo压低的企鹅图贡献。关键理论工具包括$\Delta B=1$跃迁的有效哈密顿量、算符乘积展开和重整化群演化。研究比较不同衰变模式($B^0_d\toφK_{\rm S}$、$B^+ \to φK^+$以及新提出的$B_s^0\toφK_{\rm S}$)，以提取同位旋关系并约束强子参数。]

The analysis demonstrates that these decays offer significant sensitivity to New Physics contributions, with particular emphasis on scenarios with non-trivial isospin structure (e.g., electroweak penguin operators). Conclusion: [The $B\toφK$ system provides a powerful laboratory for testing the Standard Model and probing New Physics, particularly through CP violation in $B^0_d\toφK_{\rm S}$. [$B\toφK$系统为测试标准模型和探测新物理提供了强大的实验室，特别是通过$B^0_d\toφK_{\rm S}$中的CP破坏。因子化方法产生了精确的标准模型预测，这些预测可作为未来实验的重要基准。引入$B_s^0\toφK_{\rm S}$作为新通道为强子不确定性提供了额外约束。同位旋分析能够区分不同的新物理场景。该框架为味物理的高精度时代奠定了基础，其中理论与实验之间的差异可能揭示超越标准模型的物理，包括具有特定同位旋性质的贡献。]

Abstract: The penguin loop-suppressed $B\toφK$ decays are highly sensitive to contributions of hypothetical heavy new particles. Particularly interesting probes for testing the Standard Model and revealing such phenomena are provided by CP violation in the $B^0_d\toφK_{\rm S}$ decay. Standard-Model estimates for the corresponding CP-violating observables are theoretically limited by doubly Cabibbo-suppressed penguin contributions. We study these effects using a factorization approach, and provide predictions for CP asymmetries, to be contrasted with future measurements. To gain additional insight into these hadronic effects, we propose the $B_s^0\toφK_{\rm S}$ decay as a new channel. We predict the observables for this decay for which currently no measurements exist. By comparing $B^0_d\toφK_{\rm S}$ and $B^+ \to φK^+$, we further derive state-of-the-art constraints on isospin observables within the Standard Model. The same framework enables probing of possible New-Physics contributions, including general effects and those with non-trivial isospin structure. Interesting prospects arise for the high-precision era of flavour physics ahead.

### [51] [Determination of Nuclear PDFs using Markov Chain Monte Carlo Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13150)
*N. Derakhshanian,P. Risse,T. Jezo,M. Klasen,K. Kovarik,A. Kusina*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: First MCMC-based nPDF determination using adaptive Metropolis-Hastings algorithm within nCTEQ framework reveals non-Gaussian likelihood structure, multiple modes, and provides more reliable uncertainty quantification compared to traditional Hessian methods.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional Hessian methods for nuclear PDF uncertainty quantification rely on Gaussian approximations and local curvature, which are insufficient for nPDF fits characterized by limited data constraints and non-Gaussian likelihoods.

Method: Implemented Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) with adaptive Metropolis-Hastings algorithm within nCTEQ framework. Performed first single-nucleus global analysis of lead PDFs using exclusively lead data, compared to multi-nuclei fit with analytic A dependence. Complementary Hessian analysis performed for systematic comparison.

Result: MCMC reveals highly non-trivial parameter-space structure with multiple modes and pronounced non-Gaussian behavior, especially for valence PDFs. Inclusion of lighter nuclei reduces quark uncertainties and modifies lead PDF shapes, while gluon distribution remains largely unaffected. Hessian analysis confirms systematic limitations of Gaussian approximation.

Conclusion: MCMC methods provide superior uncertainty quantification for nPDF determinations by directly mapping posterior distributions, revealing non-Gaussian features missed by Hessian approaches, establishing more reliable framework for future nuclear PDF analyses.

Abstract: Global QCD analyses of nuclear parton distribution functions (nPDFs) have traditionally relied on the Hessian method for uncertainty estimation. However, the inherent Gaussian approximation and reliance on local curvature often prove insufficient for nPDF fits, which are frequently characterized by limited data constraints and non-Gaussian likelihoods. In this paper, we present the first nPDF determination based on Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) techniques, implemented within the nCTEQ framework using an adaptive Metropolis-Hastings algorithm. The MCMC approach enables a direct mapping of the posterior distribution and reveals a highly non-trivial parameter-space structure, including multiple modes and pronounced non-Gaussian behavior, particularly for the valence PDFs. We perform the first single-nucleus global analysis of lead PDFs using exclusively lead data and compare it to a multi-nuclei fit employing a standard analytic A dependence. The inclusion of lighter nuclei reduces quark uncertainties and modifies the shape of the lead PDFs, while leaving the gluon distribution largely unaffected. A complementary Hessian analysis exposes systematic limitations of the Gaussian approximation. Our results demonstrate that MCMC methods provide a more reliable framework for uncertainty quantification in nPDF determinations.

### [52] [Radiative return meets GVMD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13171)
*Pau Petit Rosàs,Olga Shekhovtsova,William J. Torres Bobadilla*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Authors improved pion-photon radiative return modeling in $e^+e^-\to \pi^+\pi^-\gamma$ at NLO by incorporating the pion form factor directly into Feynman rules, implemented in $\texttt{Phokhara}$, finding percent-level angular distribution effects near form factor peaks.

作者在NLO改进了$e^+e^-\to \pi^+\pi^-\gamma$中π介子-光子辐射回归的建模，通过将π介子形状因子直接纳入费曼规则，并在$\texttt{Phokhara}$中实现，发现在形状因子峰值附近角度分布存在百分数水平效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Radiative return measurements at $e^+e^-$ colliders provide crucial input for precision tests of low-energy QCD and hadronic contributions to the muon $g-2$. The process $e^+e^-\to\pi^+\pi^-\gamma$ serves as the primary channel for extracting the pion form factor $F_\pi(s)$, with theoretical uncertainties dominated by NLO corrections. Current Monte Carlo implementations treat pions as point-like in photon emission, ignoring the internal structure encoded in $F_\pi(s)$, which becomes significant near the $\rho$ resonance region where $F_\pi(s)$ varies rapidly.

$e^+e^-$对撞机上的辐射回归测量为低能QCD的精密检验和μ子$g-2$的强子贡献提供了关键输入。过程$e^+e^-\to\pi^+\pi^-\gamma$是提取π介子形状因子$F_\pi(s)$的主要通道，其理论不确定性主要由NLO修正主导。当前的蒙特卡洛实现将π介子视为点状粒子处理光子发射，忽略了$F_\pi(s)$编码的内部结构，这在$F_\pi(s)$快速变化的$\rho$共振区域变得尤为重要。

Method: Developed a new framework that incorporates the pion form factor $F_\pi(s)$ directly into the Feynman rules for pion-photon vertices, extending the standard treatment of radiative return beyond point-like approximations. This allows for consistent NLO QED corrections with pion structure effects. The approach modifies the QED Lagrangian by promoting the elementary pion-photon coupling to a form factor-dependent vertex: $\mathcal{L} \supset -ieF_\pi(s) A_\mu(\pi^-\partial^\mu\pi^+ - \pi^+\partial^\mu\pi^-)$, where $s$ is the invariant mass of the pion pair. Implementation in $\texttt{Phokhara}$ event generator enables detailed studies of angular distributions, forward-backward asymmetries, and differential cross sections under various experimental cuts.

开发了一个新框架，将π介子形状因子$F_\pi(s)$直接纳入π介子-光子顶点的费曼规则中，将辐射回归的标准处理扩展到点状近似之外。这使得一致的NLO QED修正与π介子结构效应成为可能。该方法通过将基本π介子-光子耦合提升为形状因子依赖的顶点来修改QED拉格朗日量：$\mathcal{L} \supset -ieF_\pi(s) A_\mu(\pi^-\partial^\mu\pi^+ - \pi^+\partial^\mu\pi^-)$，其中$s$是π介子对的不变质量。在$\texttt{Phokhara}$事件生成器中的实现使得能够在各种实验截断下对角分布、前-后不对称性和微分截面进行详细研究。

Result: The inclusion of pion form factor leads to percent-level corrections in angular differential cross sections near the $\rho$ resonance peak (approximately 770 MeV), where $F_\pi(s)$ varies rapidly. Effects are most pronounced in charge-odd observables sensitive to interference terms. Total cross sections and charge-even distributions show only permille-level changes or remain indistinguishable from point-like calculations. Comparison with KLOE forward-backward asymmetry measurements demonstrates improved predictive power, particularly in the region $s \sim m_\rho^2$, with theoretical uncertainties reduced by incorporating realistic pion structure effects.

包含π介子形状因子导致在$\rho$共振峰附近（约770 MeV）角微分截面出现百分数水平的修正，此处$F_\pi(s)$变化迅速。效应在对干涉项敏感的电荷奇观测量中最为显著。总截面和电荷偶分布仅显示千分之一水平的变化或与点状计算无法区分。与KLOE前-后不对称性测量的比较表明预测能力有所改善，特别是在$s \sim m_\rho^2$区域，通过纳入现实的π介子结构效应减少了理论不确定性。

Conclusion: NLO corrections with realistic pion form factor implementation are essential for precision radiative return analyses near resonance regions, affecting angular distributions at the percent level while leaving integrated rates largely unchanged. The framework provides a systematic approach to incorporate hadronic structure effects in Monte Carlo generators, improving theoretical predictions for ongoing experimental programs like KLOE-2 and future $e^+e^-$ facilities. Future extensions should include higher-order QED corrections, vacuum polarization effects, and additional resonance contributions beyond the $\rho$ meson.

在共振区域附近，具有现实π介子形状因子实现的NLO修正对于精密辐射回归分析至关重要，影响百分数水平的角分布，同时保持积分速率基本不变。该框架提供了一种在蒙特卡洛生成器中纳入强子结构效应的系统方法，改善了KLOE-2等正在进行实验项目以及未来$e^+e^-$设施的理论预测。未来的扩展应包括高阶QED修正、真空极化效应以及$\rho$介子之外的额外共振贡献。

Abstract: We improve the description of pion-photon interactions in the radiative return process $e^+e^-\to π^+π^-γ$ at the next-to-leading order by including the pion form factor in the Feynman rules. We present a general calculation of the new amplitudes, and provide an implementation easy to interface with any Monte Carlo generator. We incorporate this framework into the event generator $\texttt{Phokhara}$ and study several experimental configurations. Overall, we find percent-level effects appearing in angular differential cross section distributions at colliders whose centre-of-mass energies lie near the peak of the pion form factor. By contrast, total cross sections and distributions in charge-even variables show effects only at the permille level, or no visible differences at all. Finally, we compare the new predictions with KLOE measurements of the forward-backward asymmetry in order to assess the predictive power of the modifications.

</details>


### [53] [Axion search with telescope for radio astronomy (ASTRA): forecast for observations between 0.5 and 4~GHz](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13194)
*Utkarsh Bhura,David J. E. Marsh,Bradley R. Johnson,Karl van Bibber,Mallory Helfenbein,Bradley J. Kavanagh,Matthew Nelson,Ciaran A. J. O'Hare,Giovanni Pierobon,Gray Rybka,Luca Visinelli*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: [An analysis of the detectability of axion dark matter conversion in neutron star magnetospheres using a 5 m radio telescope operating at 0.5-4 GHz. The telescope can probe axion-like particles in the mass range $2\,\mu\text{eV}<m_a<17\,\mu\text{eV}$ with sensitivity to axion-photon couplings $g_{aγγ} \gtrsim 2\times 10^{-12}\,\text{GeV}^{-1}$ over three years, improving existing neutron star constraints by over an order of magnitude. This broadband approach complements other axion detection techniques in the same frequency band.]

[分析使用工作在0.5-4 GHz频段的5米射电望远镜探测轴子暗物质在中子星磁层中转化的可能性。该望远镜可在质量范围$2\,\mu\text{eV}<m_a<17\,\mu\text{eV}$内探测轴子类粒子，对轴子-光子耦合强度$g_{aγγ} \gtrsim 2\times 10^{-12}\,\text{GeV}^{-1}$具有灵敏度，通过三年观测可将现有中子星约束提高一个数量级以上。这种宽带方法在同一频段内与其他轴子探测技术形成互补。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [Axion dark matter conversion to radio waves in neutron star magnetospheres represents a promising detection channel, but current constraints from neutron star observations remain limited. The research aims to assess the feasibility of using a modest 5 m radio telescope at the Fan Mountain Observatory to significantly improve sensitivity over a broad parameter space (2-17 μeV mass range), complementing existing techniques and potentially probing the QCD axion model band if a dark matter spike exists at the Galactic center.]

[轴子暗物质在中子星磁层中转化为射电波是一个有前景的探测通道，但目前基于中子星观测的约束仍然有限。本研究旨在评估使用Fan Mountain天文台的5米射电望远镜在宽参数空间(2-17 μeV质量范围)内显著提高灵敏度的可行性，补充现有探测技术，并在银河系中心存在暗物质尖峰的情况下，可能探测QCD轴子模型带。]

Method: [The study develops a comprehensive framework including: (1) Detailed neutron star population model accounting for Galactic distribution and properties; (2) Noise model for the 5 m telescope operating in UHF, L-, and S-bands (0.5-4 GHz); (3) Axion-photon conversion rate calculation in neutron star magnetospheres using standard halo model assumptions; (4) Signal-to-noise analysis for broadband observation strategy over three years; (5) Assessment of Galactic center neutron stars as primary targets due to highest dark matter density; (6) Extension analysis considering potential dark matter spike at Galactic center for QCD axion sensitivity.]

[本研究建立了一个综合框架，包括：(1) 考虑银河系分布和性质的详细中子星群体模型；(2) 工作在UHF、L-和S波段(0.5-4 GHz)的5米望远镜噪声模型；(3) 使用标准晕模型假设计算轴子-光子在中子星磁层中的转化率；(4) 三年宽带观测策略的信噪比分析；(5) 评估银河系中心中子星作为主要目标(由于暗物质密度最高)；(6) 考虑银河系中心潜在暗物质尖峰的扩展分析，以获得QCD轴子灵敏度。]

Result: [The 5 m telescope can search axion-like particles in the mass range $2\,\mu\text{eV}<m_a<17\,\mu\text{eV}$ with sensitivity to axion-photon couplings $g_{aγγ} \gtrsim 2\times 10^{-12}\,\text{GeV}^{-1}$ over three years -- improving neutron star observation constraints by more than an order of magnitude. Most constraining power comes from neutron stars at the Galactic center. If a dark matter spike exists at the Galactic center, the search becomes sensitive within the QCD axion model band. UHF and L-band observations (0.5-2 GHz) represent the pathfinder phase of the ASTRA program, while future hardware development for S, C, X, and Ku bands (2-18 GHz) would enable searches at higher masses for post-inflation axion discovery potential.]

[5米望远镜可在三年内探测质量范围$2\,\mu\text{eV}<m_a<17\,\mu\text{eV}$内的轴子类粒子，对轴子-光子耦合强度$g_{aγγ} \gtrsim 2\times 10^{-12}\,\text{GeV}^{-1}$具有灵敏度，将中子星观测约束提高一个数量级以上。主要约束能力来自银河系中心的中子星。如果银河系中心存在暗物质尖峰，该搜索在QCD轴子模型带内具有灵敏度。UHF和L波段观测(0.5-2 GHz)代表了ASTRA计划("Axion Search with Telescope for Radio Astronomy")的探路阶段，而未来针对S、C、X和Ku波段(2-18 GHz)的硬件开发将使得在更高质量范围内搜索后暴胀轴子的发现潜力成为可能。]

Conclusion: [A 5 m radio telescope operating from 0.5-4 GHz can provide competitive constraints on axion dark matter through neutron star observations, improving existing limits by over an order of magnitude. The broadband nature makes it complementary to other axion search techniques. The ASTRA program's pathfinder phase (0.5-2 GHz) establishes feasibility, while future hardware development for higher frequencies (2-18 GHz) could probe the post-inflation axion parameter space. This approach leverages neutron stars as natural axion converters in regions of high dark matter density, particularly at the Galactic center.]

[工作在0.5-4 GHz频段的5米射电望远镜可通过中子星观测提供具有竞争力的轴子暗物质约束，将现有限制提高一个数量级以上。其宽带特性使其与其他轴子搜索技术形成互补。ASTRA计划的探路阶段(0.5-2 GHz)确立了可行性，而未来针对更高频率(2-18 GHz)的硬件开发可能探测后暴胀轴子参数空间。这种方法利用了中子星作为高暗物质密度区域(特别是银河系中心)的天然轴子转化器。]

Abstract: Axion dark matter (DM) is predicted to convert into radio waves in neutron star magnetospheres. We assess the detectability of this signal using a 5 m radio telescope to be installed at the Fan Mountain Observatory, operating in the UHF, L- and S-bands from 0.5 to 4~GHz. We demonstrate that such a telescope can search new parameter space for axion-like particles over a broad range from $2\,μ\text{eV}<m_a<17\,μ\text{eV}$ for axion-photon couplings $g_{aγγ} \gtrsim 2\times 10^{-12}\text{ GeV}^{-1}$ with a three year observing period assuming the standard halo model -- improving neutron star observations by more than an order of magnitude. The search is broadband and is thus complementary to other techniques in the same frequency range. We describe in detail our neutron star population model, noise model, and proposed observing strategy. Most constraining power comes from neutron stars at the Galactic centre, where the smooth DM halo is densest. If a DM spike exists at the Galactic centre, the search is sensitive in the QCD axion model band. UHF and L-band observations (0.5 to 2~GHz) represent the pathfinder phase of a wider program we call ``Axion Search with Telescope for Radio Astronomy'' (ASTRA). Future higher mass searches aimed at discovery potential for the post-inflation axion require further hardware development to cover S, C, X and Ku bands (2 to 18~GHz).

</details>

### [54] [Phenomenology of an Open Effective Field Theory of Dark Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12321)
*Santiago Agüí Salcedo,Thomas Colas,Lennard Dufner,Enrico Pajer*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: Open gravitational dynamics framework applied to late-time cosmic acceleration yields testable predictions: dissipative suppression of GW luminosity distance, modified Bardeen potentials with gravitational slip signal, and enhanced low-redshift structure formation.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: All evidence for dark matter/energy is gravitational, suggesting the dark sector could be an open system described by metric dynamics interacting with an unknown environment. Need to develop concrete realizations of open gravitational dynamics to explain late-time acceleration while making testable predictions beyond $\Lambda$CDM.

Method: Construct minimal realization of open gravitational dynamics theory using open-system techniques. Apply to late-time cosmology: modify Friedmann equations with dissipation terms that avoid null energy condition violations. Derive modified cosmological perturbation theory: study tensor perturbations (GW luminosity distance), scalar perturbations (Bardeen potentials and gravitational slip), and matter density contrast evolution.

Result: Model fits BAO measurements by construction while avoiding NEC violations. Predictions: 1) Dissipative suppression of gravitational-wave luminosity distance $d_L^{\text{GW}}$ relative to electromagnetic $d_L^{\text{EM}}$; 2) Modified evolution of Bardeen potentials with clear gravitational slip signal $\Phi \neq \Psi$; 3) Enhancement of structure formation at low redshifts via modified growth factor. Effects are within reach of current constraints and provide targets for upcoming surveys.

Conclusion: Open gravitational dynamics provides viable alternative to $\Lambda$CDM for late-time acceleration with correlated, testable predictions in GW astronomy, gravitational slip, and structure formation. Semi-analytical estimates show observable signatures detectable by current/upcoming cosmological surveys, offering new avenues to probe dark sector physics.

Abstract: All observational evidence for dark matter and dark energy is so far exclusively gravitational. Hence, the dark sector may be equivalently described by a theory of the spacetime metric whose dynamics is affected by interactions with an unknown environment. Adapting open-system techniques, we have recently constructed such a general theory of open gravitational dynamics. Here we study a minimal and concrete realization of this theory that describes the late-time acceleration of the Universe. Our model provides a good fit to recent baryon acoustic oscillation measurements by construction, while avoiding violations of the null energy condition. Moreover, it leads to a set of correlated and observationally testable predictions. Studying the modified cosmological perturbation theory and compared to the $Λ$CDM model we find: a dissipative suppression of the gravitational-wave luminosity distance relative to the electromagnetic one; a modification in the evolution of the Bardeen potentials with a clear signal in the gravitational slip; and an enhancement of structure formation at low redshift. We present semi-analytical estimates of the magnitude of these effects and show that they lie within the reach of current constraints while providing clear targets for upcoming cosmological surveys.

### [55] [Fast Fourier Transform evaluation of the Fresnel integral for gravitational-wave lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12333)
*Nino Ephremidze,Marc Kamionkowski,Cora Dvorkin*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper introduces FIONA (Fresnel Integral Optimization with Non-uniform trAnsforms), an efficient computational framework for evaluating gravitational wave lensing Fresnel integrals using Fourier/Hankel transform techniques, achieving orders of magnitude speedup for large-scale sky position grids.

本文介绍了FIONA（Fresnel Integral Optimization with Non-uniform trAnsforms），一种用于评估引力波透镜菲涅尔积分的计算框架，该框架采用傅里叶/汉克尔变换技术，在大尺度天空位置网格上实现了数量级的速度提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Wave-optics effects in gravitational wave lensing by galactic subhalos provide a novel probe of dark matter, but numerical evaluation of the Fresnel integral is computationally challenging, particularly for large numbers of sky positions.

由星系子晕引起的引力波透镜中的波光学效应为暗物质探测提供了一种新的方法，但菲涅尔积分的数值计算在计算上具有挑战性，特别是对于大量的天空位置。

Method: Demonstrates that the lens position dependence in the Fresnel integral can be expressed as a 2D Fourier transform, enabling rapid all-sky evaluation via FFT. For axisymmetric lenses, further acceleration is achieved using non-uniform fast Hankel transforms (nuFHT).

证明了菲涅尔积分中的透镜位置依赖性可以表示为二维傅里叶变换，从而通过快速傅里叶变换（FFT）实现快速的全天评估。对于轴对称透镜，使用非均匀快速汉克尔变换（nuFHT）可实现进一步的加速。

Result: Developed FIONA code achieving 2-3 orders of magnitude speedup for ~$10^6$ source positions compared to existing methods. Includes vectorized nuFHT routines with applications beyond GW lensing (e.g., cosmological correlation functions).

开发了FIONA代码，与现有方法相比，对于约$10^6$个源位置，实现了2-3个数量级的加速。该代码包含矢量化的非均匀快速汉克尔变换（nuFHT）例程，其应用范围超出了引力波透镜（例如宇宙学两点关联函数）。

Conclusion: FIONA provides an efficient, accurate computational tool for gravitational wave lensing studies, enabling large-scale parameter space exploration and advancing wave-optics lensing as a dark matter probe.

FIONA为引力波透镜研究提供了一个高效、准确的计算工具，能够实现大尺度参数空间探索，并推动波光学透镜作为暗物质探测手段的发展。

Abstract: Gravitational waves (GWs) exhibit wave-optics effects when their wavelength is comparable to the scale of the gravitational lens. This may occur in lensing from galactic subhalos in GWs emitted by binary black-hole mergers, and is gaining interest as a novel probe of dark matter. Predictions for observables in these cases ultimately rely on evaluating a Fresnel integral that quantifies the effect of lensing on the amplitude of a GW at a given frequency. However, numerical evaluation of this Fresnel integral is tricky, and several algorithms and publicly available codes that implement it have been developed. Here, we show that the dependence of this integral on the lens position can be written as a two-dimensional Fourier transform. Modern FFT techniques then enable rapid evaluation at all-sky positions simultaneously for general lenses without symmetry. Vectorization of FFT routines allows for derivatives with respect to model parameters to be obtained with only incremental additional computational cost. If the lens is axisymmetric, further speedups can be achieved with recently developed techniques for non-uniform fast Hankel transforms. To demonstrate, we make available Fresnel Integral Optimization with Non-uniform trAnsforms (FIONA), an efficient and accurate code that is significantly faster than current methods for dense source grids, reaching 2-3 orders of magnitude speedups for $\sim 10^6$ GW-emitting points. As part of FIONA, we developed code that provides vectorized non-uniform fast Hankel transforms that may have other uses (e.g., calculation of cosmological two-point correlation functions) beyond those considered here.

</details>


### [56] [Probing Cosmology through Higher-Order CMB Lensing Statistics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12335)
*Shu-Fan Chen,J. Colin Hill,Zoltán Haiman*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: **Enhanced cosmological constraints from CMB lensing non-Gaussian statistics at Simons Observatory sensitivity.** Minkowski functionals and peak/minima counts provide substantial complementary information beyond the power spectrum, yielding significant improvements in cosmological parameter constraints (40% for $Ω_m$, 38% for $A_s$, and 70% for $M_ν$ uncertainty reduction).

**增强宇宙学约束通过西蒙斯天文台灵敏度下的CMB透镜非高斯统计量。** Minkowski泛函和峰/谷计数提供了超出功率谱的实质性互补信息，在宇宙学参数约束上产生了显著改善（$Ω_m$提升40%，$A_s$提升38%，$M_ν$不确定性降低70%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: **Exploring beyond the two-point function in CMB lensing.** While the CMB lensing power spectrum ($C_L^{κκ}$) provides key cosmological information, the convergence field $κ$ contains significant non-Gaussian information from nonlinear structure formation, post-Born effects, and reconstruction noise. For near-term experiments like Simons Observatory (SO), quantifying which higher-order statistics offer complementary constraints beyond $C_L^{κκ}$ is essential for maximizing cosmological information extraction, particularly for parameters sensitive to nonlinearities like $Ω_m$, $A_s$, and $M_ν$.

**探索CMB透镜两点函数之外的信息。** 虽然CMB透镜功率谱（$C_L^{κκ}$）提供了关键的宇宙学信息，但收敛场$κ$包含了来自非线性结构形成、post-Born效应和重建噪声的显著非高斯信息。对于像西蒙斯天文台（SO）这样的近期实验，量化哪些高阶统计量能够提供超出$C_L^{κκ}$的互补约束，对于最大化宇宙学信息提取至关重要，特别是对于对非线性敏感的$Ω_m$、$A_s$和$M_ν$等参数。

Method: **Forward-modeling pipeline with Gaussian process emulators.** Using ray-traced simulations from the MassiveNuS suite (1000 deg$^2$, 1024$^3$ particles) to generate realistic CMB lensing convergence fields with nonlinear structure formation and post-Born effects. SO-like lensing reconstruction noise is added based on realistic experimental specifications. Multiple non-Gaussian statistics are extracted: Minkowski functionals (V0-V2), peak/minima counts, moments ($S_3$, $S_4$), and wavelet-scattering coefficients. Gaussian process (GP) emulators are trained to model the dependence of each statistic on cosmological parameters ($Ω_m$, $A_s$, $M_ν$). Fisher forecasting is used to quantify information content and parameter constraints, comparing power spectrum alone vs. combinations with higher-order statistics.

**基于高斯过程模拟器的前向建模流程。** 使用MassiveNuS套件的射线追踪模拟（1000 deg$^2$, 1024$^3$粒子）生成包含非线性结构形成和post-Born效应的真实CMB透镜收敛场。基于真实实验规格添加SO级别的透镜重建噪声。提取多种非高斯统计量：Minkowski泛函（V0-V2）、峰/谷计数、矩统计量（$S_3$, $S_4$）和小波散射系数。训练高斯过程（GP）模拟器来建模每个统计量对宇宙学参数（$Ω_m$, $A_s$, $M_ν$）的依赖关系。使用Fisher预报量化信息内容和参数约束，比较单独使用功率谱与结合高阶统计量的情况。

Result: **Morphology-based statistics provide significant complementary information.** Minkowski functionals and peak/minima counts offer substantial gains beyond the lensing power spectrum: combined with $C_L^{κκ}$, they reduce marginalized uncertainties by 40% for $Ω_m$, 38% for $A_s$, and 70% for the one-sided uncertainty on $M_ν$. When combined with extended power spectrum (larger scales) and external data (primary CMB + BAO), Minkowski functionals still provide 11% improvement in $σ(M_ν)$ and 35% in $σ(Ω_m)$. By contrast, moments and wavelet-scattering coefficients offer more limited gains at SO noise levels. Minkowski functionals show particular robustness to reconstruction noise, maintaining information even with realistic SO noise levels.

**基于形态的统计量提供显著的互补信息。** Minkowski泛函和峰/谷计数在透镜功率谱基础上提供了实质性增益：与$C_L^{κκ}$结合使用时，它们将边际不确定性降低了$Ω_m$的40%，$A_s$的38%，以及$M_ν$单边不确定性的70%。当与扩展功率谱（更大尺度）和外部数据（原初CMB+BAO）结合时，Minkowski泛函仍然提供了$σ(M_ν)$的11%改善和$σ(Ω_m)$的35%改善。相比之下，矩统计量和小波散射系数在SO噪声水平下提供有限的增益。Minkowski泛函对重建噪声表现出特别的鲁棒性，即使在真实SO噪声水平下仍能保持信息。

Conclusion: **Non-Gaussian statistics, particularly Minkowski functionals, offer powerful cosmological complementarity for SO-era CMB lensing.** The study demonstrates that morphology-based statistics capture complementary information beyond the power spectrum, significantly improving constraints on key cosmological parameters. The robustness of Minkowski functionals to reconstruction noise makes them particularly valuable for SO and future CMB surveys. The approach highlights the importance of field-level forward modeling to capture nonlinear effects and reconstruction systematics, enabling optimal extraction of cosmological information from next-generation CMB experiments.

**非高斯统计量，特别是Minkowski泛函，为SO时代的CMB透镜提供了强大的宇宙学互补性。** 该研究表明，基于形态的统计量捕获了超出功率谱的互补信息，显著改善了对关键宇宙学参数的约束。Minkowski泛函对重建噪声的鲁棒性使其对SO和未来的CMB巡天特别有价值。该方法强调了场级前向建模对于捕获非线性效应和重建系统误差的重要性，使得能够从下一代CMB实验中最佳提取宇宙学信息。

Abstract: We investigate the cosmological information in higher-order statistics of the cosmic microwave background (CMB) lensing convergence field for a near-term experiment with noise properties similar to the Simons Observatory (SO). Using a fully field-level forward-modeling pipeline based on ray-traced simulations from the MassiveNuS suite and realistic SO-like CMB lensing reconstruction, we naturally include nonlinear structure formation, post-Born effects, and higher-order reconstruction noise. We measure several non-Gaussian statistics, including Minkowski functionals, peak and minima counts, moments, and wavelet-scattering coefficients. We train Gaussian-process emulators to model each statistic's dependence on the matter density fraction $Ω_m$, the scalar power spectrum amplitude $A_s$, and the neutrino mass sum $M_ν$. We quantify the relative information gain these statistics provide beyond the lensing power spectrum and identify which are most robust to reconstruction noise. We find that morphology-based statistics, particularly Minkowski functionals and peak/minima counts, offer significant complementary constraining power: combining all non-Gaussian statistics with the power spectrum yields reductions of 40% and 38% in the marginalized uncertainties on $Ω_m$ and $A_s$, respectively, and a 70% reduction in the one-sided uncertainty on $M_ν$. These gains remain non-negligible even when the power spectrum is extended to larger scales and combined with primary CMB and BAO data, with Minkowski functionals providing an additional 11% improvement in $σ(M_ν)$ and 35% in $σ(Ω_m)$ beyond the extended power spectrum. By contrast, moments and wavelet-scattering coefficients provide more limited gains at SO noise levels. Our results highlight the potential of non-Gaussian statistics to enhance cosmological constraints from SO and future CMB surveys.

</details>
